# Deferred work (code-review carry-forward)

Items surfaced by `/bmad-code-review` adversarial triage that were classified `defer` rather than `patch`. Each entry cites the originating review and the reason for deferral so future stories can absorb the work with full context.

## Deferred from: code review of story-1.8 (2026-04-20)

_Story 1.8 (`invariants.manifest.ts` contract + exporter) — iter-7 `/bmad-code-review (args: "2")`. Three-layer adversarial review (Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter + Acceptance Auditor). Auditor returned zero AC violations; the six defers below all originate from Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter defensive-hardening findings that are either explicitly Story 1.9's enforcement-side scope (per Story 1.8's § Scope Carve-Out + FR43) or spec-silent tightening candidates._

- **contentHash drift validation at manifest-use time.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts` (all 9 entries). _Nature:_ the manifest stores a pre-computed `contentHash` but never re-reads the `sourcePath` file to verify the hash is still current. _Carry-to:_ Story 1.9 sync-gate — FR43 enforcement side explicitly owns the anchor-walker + file-read + sha256 re-computation + drift-detection flow. Absorbed naturally; no action needed ahead of Story 1.9.
- **sourcePath path-traversal / format guard in Zod schema.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts:6` (`sourcePath: z.string().min(1)`). _Nature:_ schema accepts absolute paths, `..` traversal, Windows backslashes, leading slashes. Current 9 entries are all repo-relative forward-slash, so no live exposure. _Carry-to:_ Story 1.9 walker does file-resolution and will naturally reject non-resolvable paths; if tightening the schema itself is wanted earlier, a one-line `.regex(/^[^/\\][^\\]*$/).refine(p => !p.includes('..'))` does it — but that's scope creep vs Story 1.8's contract-only remit.
- **`id` uniqueness across array not enforced by schema.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts:11` (`InvariantsSchema = z.array(InvariantSchema)`). _Nature:_ Zod's `z.array` permits duplicate elements; two entries with the same `id` would silently validate. Acceptance Auditor confirmed current 9 IDs are unique. _Carry-to:_ Story 1.9's drift-detection gate treats unregistered / duplicate-registered rules as drift per AC 3 enforcement side — duplicates surface there. Alternatively, a `.superRefine(arr => Set uniqueness check)` on `InvariantsSchema` in Story 1.9's refactor pass.
- **Shared-sourcePath cross-entry `contentHash` consistency refine.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts:11`. _Nature:_ four current entries pair up on two shared source files (`eslint.config.keel-invariants.js` hosts `INV-eslint-shared` + `INV-eslint-import-boundary`; `.pre-commit-config.yaml` hosts `INV-prek-pre-commit-config` + `INV-prek-commit-msg-config`). Whole-file carve-out means these pairs MUST share identical `contentHash` values (they do — auditor verified). If a future authoring error broke that invariant (same `sourcePath`, different `contentHash`), the schema wouldn't catch it. _Carry-to:_ Story 1.9 walker re-computes `sha256` per distinct `sourcePath` and surfaces cross-entry mismatch immediately.
- **`invariants` array immutability — `readonly` / `Object.freeze`.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts:89` (`export const invariants: Invariant[]`). _Nature:_ consumer of `@keel/keel-invariants` receives a live reference to a mutable array; a misbehaving consumer (`invariants.push(...)` / `invariants[0].id = '...'`) would corrupt the module-level singleton for every other importer. No current consumer is known to mutate it. _Carry-to:_ Story 1.9 refactor — two-line change (`readonly Invariant[]` type + `Object.freeze(InvariantsSchema.parse(raw))`). Spec-silent hardening; low-cost but out-of-scope for contract-only 1.8.
- **Schema-evolution metadata on `Invariant` entries (`schemaVersion` / `deprecated` / `since`).** _Source:_ Blind Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts:3-9` (`InvariantSchema` object shape). _Nature:_ no first-class way to mark an invariant as deprecated-but-not-yet-drifted, no schema version field on the root manifest, no `since` / introduced-in-story field per entry. _Carry-to:_ Story 1.9's enforcement side will need "deprecated ≠ drift" semantics at minimum (otherwise sunsetting a rule and removing its registration both look like drift). Natural home for this expansion. If earlier would be valuable, a later substrate-hardening story (1.16 scope or adjacent) can add it.

## Deferred from: code review of story-1.9 (2026-04-20)

_Story 1.9 (Invariant sync-gate runtime tooling — reader/walker/drift-detector) — iter-7 `/bmad-code-review (args: "2")`. Three-layer Ralph-hosted adversarial fan-out (Blind Hunter as `bmad-agent-architect` / Edge Case Hunter as `bmad-tea` / Acceptance Auditor as `bmad-agent-dev`). Convergent CRITICAL (regex-class bug on `ANCHOR_REGEX` — Edge + Auditor both reproduced live) + 3 HIGH content-accuracy drifts + 2 MEDIUM framing/citation drifts → 6 patches queued. The 10 defers below are all defensive-hardening candidates natural-scope for Story 1.10+ substrate refactors OR the Story 1.16 test-runner landing; none are exploitable in the current single-consumer, linux-only, text-sources-only baseline._

- **Shallow `Object.freeze` vs "readonly + Object.freeze" spec claim.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts:~130`. _Nature:_ `Object.freeze(invariants)` locks the top-level array but entries and their `anchors` sub-arrays remain mutable at runtime (`invariants[0].id = 'HACKED'` succeeds; `invariants[0].anchors.push('X')` succeeds; `invariants.push(fake)` throws because only the outer array is frozen). `readonly Invariant[]` is a compile-time TS signal with zero runtime effect. Task 3 (Story 1.9 CR defer #5 from Story 1.8) advertised "readonly + Object.freeze" as a runtime guarantee; the landed implementation is the shallow-only variant. Not exploitable in-process today (no consumer mutates entries), but the spec over-advertises the guarantee. _Carry-to:_ either Story 1.10+ deep-freeze refactor (`entry + entry.anchors` Object.freeze) OR amend spec text to "shallow freeze (array-reassignment guard only)". Two-line code change either way.
- **`check.ts` lacks try/catch around `runSyncGate` — raw ENOENT stacktrace on missing INVARIANTS.md.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/check.ts` (top-level await). _Nature:_ if `INVARIANTS.md` is absent (cwd mismatch, dist-layout drift, moved-file) or `repoRoot` resolution misfires, Node emits `UnhandledPromiseRejection` + raw ENOENT stacktrace. AC 6's intent is "non-zero reliably fails the workflow AND the drift report renders in CI logs" — raw stacktrace exits non-zero but violates the "renders a report" half. _Carry-to:_ wrap the top-level await in try/catch, emit `{status: 'error', message: e.message}` and exit 1. Belongs with Story 1.16 CI-wiring story where the error-surface is tested end-to-end in GitHub Actions logs.
- **Traversal refine gaps in `sourcePath` Zod validation.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts:~10` (`refine(p => !p.startsWith('/') && !p.startsWith('\\\\') && !p.includes('..') && !p.includes('\\\\'))`). _Nature:_ (a) `foo/bar/%2e%2e/etc/passwd` passes (percent-encoded `..` — benign today since `readFile` doesn't URL-decode, but the refine message implies broader guard); (b) `D:/Windows` passes (Windows drive-absolute — low-risk on Linux CI, non-zero on Windows contributors); (c) null-byte / newline / CR characters not rejected; (d) symlinks defeat the refine at the FS layer regardless (`readFile` follows symlinks, so a committed `src/foo` → `/etc/passwd` symlink hashes the foreign content). _Carry-to:_ tighten refine (`!/\0|\n|\r/.test(p)`, `!/^[a-zA-Z]:/.test(p)`) + use `fs.lstat` + reject `S_IFLNK`. Natural Story 1.10+ schema-hardening pass.
- **UTF-8 binary-file mangling in `manifest-reader.ts`.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/manifest-reader.ts:8` (`readFile(absPath, 'utf-8')`). _Nature:_ reading bytes as utf-8 string and hashing the decoded string diverges from byte-level sha256 on any non-UTF-8 content (binary files, files with invalid sequences). All current invariants source text files; vacuous today. But a future invariant targeting a binary file (lockfile digest, wasm module) would hash inconsistently with `sha256sum` CLI output. _Carry-to:_ swap to `readFile(absPath)` → Buffer, then `createHash('sha256').update(buffer).digest('hex')` — aligns byte-for-byte with `sha256sum`. One-line change.
- **`Promise.all` error-swallow at `sync-gate.ts:47-57`.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/sync-gate.ts:47-57` (catch-all returning `null` inside `Promise.all`). _Nature:_ all non-ENOENT failures (permission denied, I/O error, path-is-a-directory) collapse to `removed-from-source-only` drift. Misleading root-cause analysis in CI. _Carry-to:_ narrow catch to `err.code === 'ENOENT'`; re-throw others OR emit `error`-kind drift. Natural hardening alongside the check.ts try/catch defer above.
- **Anchor-parser O(n·m) complexity.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/sync-gate.ts` (single-pass regex over doc per entry). _Nature:_ linear in entries × doc lines; at current scale (10 entries × ~60 doc lines) sub-millisecond; at 500 entries × 500 lines still sub-second. Not a live risk; flagged for principled scale-awareness. _Carry-to:_ no action needed for 1.x; if manifest grows past ~500 entries or doc past ~5000 lines, revisit with a single-pass map-building approach.
- **Duplicate-id refine message shape.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts:~22-28` (id-uniqueness `.superRefine`). _Nature:_ triplicate IDs emit 2 separate issue messages (one per extra occurrence), not one-per-pair. Cosmetic Zod UX only; does not affect correctness (duplicates are still caught). _Carry-to:_ tighten refine to emit a single grouped issue per duplicate-ID cluster. Trivial fix, low priority.
- **Whitespace-in-anchor backtick normalisation.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/sync-gate.ts` (anchor regex). _Nature:_ a hypothetical anchor line with trailing whitespace inside the backticks (`` `INV-foo-bar ` `` vs `` `INV-foo-bar` ``) would be treated as distinct IDs. Regex doesn't allow spaces today (character class excludes space), so not exploitable. Principled hardening for future-syntax-drift tolerance. _Carry-to:_ `.trim()` the capture group before `anchors.add`. One-line change.
- **`<500ms internal target` prose vs 0.77s measured.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter. _Location:_ `_bmad-output/implementation-artifacts/1-9-…md:128` § Performance posture. _Nature:_ spec declares an internal target of `<500ms` + `<100ms cold` + `<20ms warm` as prose guidance. Task 5 measured 0.77s wall-clock (770ms) — the AC threshold `<2s` is met (AC 7 PASS), but the prose internal target was exceeded by ~50%. The prose is informational (not an AC), so not a fix-task candidate; flagged to either amend the prose down to realistic levels (`<1s warm, ~800ms cold`) OR re-benchmark with the node-module cache warm. _Carry-to:_ cleanup iteration alongside a trace/perf-regression follow-up. Low impact.
- **Provisional-ID bullet leftover "(Actually — …)" scratch-commentary.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter. _Location:_ `_bmad-output/implementation-artifacts/1-9-…md:130` (§ Provisional-ID header discharge bullet). _Nature:_ story file retains parenthetical scratch commentary `"(Actually — Task 2 edits invariants.manifest.ts, not INVARIANTS.md; INVARIANTS.md stays as-is since the 10th anchor is already there since commit 5cfa055. The provisional header removal is a cosmetic docs edit; wire it into Task 5 alongside sprint-status bump.)"` — reads as hand-edit scratch-pad leakage, not polished prose. Cosmetic only. _Carry-to:_ docs-cleanup iteration; replace the parenthetical with a concise "Provisional-header removed alongside Task 5 sprint-status bump." sentence.

## Deferred from: code review RE-RUN of story-1.9 (2026-04-20)

_Story 1.9 (Invariant sync-gate runtime tooling) — iter-14 `/bmad-code-review (args: "2")` CR RE-RUN after iter-8..iter-13 fix pass. Three-layer Ralph-hosted adversarial fan-out. **Acceptance Auditor verdict PASS** (all 7 AC validated end-to-end with LIVE reproductions including byte-identical revert-restore for AC 2 manifest-side missing-anchor + AC 5 docs-side orphan-anchor smokes). **Edge Case Hunter verdict MINOR_ONLY** (4 LOW new-edge-case findings — 2 new + 2 reconfirmations of iter-7 defers). **Blind Hunter verdict NEW_FINDINGS** (3 HIGH trace-bundle residue + 1 MEDIUM spec self-contradiction — all absorbed into iter-15..iter-17 fix queue as Fix A/B/C; NOT deferred)._

_The 4 defers below are all Edge Case Hunter LOWs — defensive-hardening candidates natural-scope for Story 1.10+ schema-hardening OR the Story 1.16 test-runner landing; none exploitable in current single-consumer linux-only text-sources-only baseline with column-0 bullet convention and code-fence-free INVARIANTS.md. No patches required for these defers; adversarial-triage-default holds (per `PROMPT_build.md § Story Lifecycle`)._

- **Anchor-regex `^-\s+` column-0 binding forbids indented bullets.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter (iter-14 re-run). _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/sync-gate.ts:24` (`ANCHOR_REGEX = /^-\s+\*\*\`(INV-[a-z0-9]+(?:-[a-z0-9]+)+)\`\*\*/gm`). _Nature:_ the leading `^-\s+` binds column 0 with multiline-mode `^`. Indented bullets (`  - **\`INV-foo\`**`) do NOT match. Reproducible: `node -e "console.log([...'  - **\`INV-foo-bar\`**'.matchAll(/^-\s+\*\*\`(INV-[a-z0-9]+(?:-[a-z0-9]+)+)\`\*\*/gm)])"` → `[]`. All current INVARIANTS.md entries are column-0 bullets (verified — zero indented matches), so zero active drift. If a future section groups invariants as sub-bullets under a parent header (a natural Markdown editing pattern — e.g., "### Core invariants → - **\`INV-*\`**"), those anchors will be silently invisible to the gate → treated as "manifest-only" → trip false `added-to-source-only` drift on otherwise-valid manifest entries. No spec in the story forbids nested bullets in INVARIANTS.md. _Carry-to:_ Story 1.10+ schema-hardening — relax leading anchor to `^\s*-\s+` to accept optional indent; OR add an explicit spec clause forbidding indented anchor bullets in INVARIANTS.md and a lint-rule gate (latter is zero-cost guard-rail discipline).
- **Anchor-regex matches anchors inside code fences.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter (iter-14 re-run). _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/sync-gate.ts:24` (`ANCHOR_REGEX` + `readAnchors` loop at `:26-34`). _Nature:_ the regex is applied to the raw markdown file content without code-fence stripping. An anchor-like bullet inside a triple-backtick fenced block (e.g., documenting the anchor ID format by example: `` ```\n- **\`INV-example-id\`**\n``` ``) will be matched. With no corresponding manifest entry for `INV-example-id`, the gate emits `removed-from-docs-only` and exits 1 on an otherwise-valid CI run. Current INVARIANTS.md has no code fences containing INV-prefixed content (verified — zero matches in fenced blocks), so zero active exposure. However, the spec is silent on forbidding code-fence examples with INV-prefixed IDs, making this an easy footgun for future doc editors who want to document the anchor format. _Carry-to:_ Story 1.10+ schema-hardening — strip code fences before regex application (`const stripped = docText.replace(/^```[\s\S]*?^```/gm, '')`) OR augment the spec with an explicit "INVARIANTS.md SHALL NOT contain INV-prefixed anchor bullets inside code fences" clause + a lint gate.
- **Reconfirmation: traversal refine `!p.includes('..')` over-broad rejection.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter (iter-14 re-run — complements iter-7 defer "Traversal refine gaps in sourcePath Zod validation"). _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts:~10` (`.refine(p => … && !p.includes('..') …)`). _Nature:_ new angle on iter-7's traversal-refine defer. iter-7 flagged false-negatives (`foo/%2e%2e/etc/passwd` passes); iter-14 flags the inverse false-positive: any innocuous filename containing the literal two-character sequence `..` (e.g., `packages/foo/bar..config.js`, `modules/lib..test.js`) is rejected by the refine with a misleading "traversal" message. No current sourcePath contains `..` — zero active impact — but an over-broad guard that forbids legal filenames. Correct guard: split on `/` and reject segments equal to `..`, not any substring occurrence. _Carry-to:_ subsumed by iter-7's Story 1.10+ schema-hardening traversal-refine pass; refactor to path-segment-aware guard (e.g., `!p.split('/').includes('..')`) alongside the null-byte / CR / Windows-drive tightening already flagged.
- **Reconfirmation: UTF-8 byte-lossy hashing in `manifest-reader.ts`.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter (iter-14 re-run — duplicate of iter-7 defer "UTF-8 binary-file mangling in `manifest-reader.ts`"). _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/manifest-reader.ts:~7-9` (`readFile(absPath, 'utf-8')` then sha256 the decoded string). _Nature:_ same defect as iter-7 defer; re-surfaced by iter-14 Edge Case Hunter's independent branch-walking. Hashing decoded UTF-8 strings instead of raw bytes means a sourcePath containing invalid UTF-8 sequences (binary file accidentally listed, config with stray 0xFF, lockfile) yields U+FFFD replacement characters and hashes lossily. Two files differing only in non-UTF-8 bytes would hash identically. All current sourcePaths are well-formed UTF-8 text (.json / .js / .ts / .md / .yaml) → zero active exposure. Contract silently coerces rather than failing loud, contradicting the story's "fail loudly on drift" framing at line 11. _Carry-to:_ subsumed by iter-7's one-line fix (`readFile(absPath)` → Buffer → `createHash('sha256').update(buffer).digest('hex')`). Independent second-source confirmation strengthens the defer's signal but adds no new carry-to.

## Deferred from: code review RE-RUN of story-1.10 (2026-04-20)

_Story 1.10 iter-52 `/bmad-code-review (args: "2")` CR RE-RUN #2 against post-Fix-CR-1 diff (`535bee0..HEAD`, now including iter-51's 3-line delta: `packages/ui/tokens.schema.json:328` `required: ["light", "dark"]` + `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts:133` hash char-swap `abb5bc4c...e07ac → 15380636...b055e6`). Three-layer Ralph-hosted parallel fan-out. **Acceptance Auditor: PASS** (14 positive checks; CR-1 PATCH cleanly discharged; all 4 ACs satisfied). **Edge Case Hunter: PASS** (no unhandled edges — modesOverlay required guard closes the iter-50 convergent gap; hash-resync byte-integrity verified). **Blind Hunter: NEW_FINDINGS** (8 raw — 5 MEDIUM + 3 LOW; all single-layer without Edge or Auditor convergence per iter-36 doctrine)._

_Triage: **0 PATCH** (halving-to-zero trajectory achieved at round 2 — matches iter-36 residue-family catalogue's prediction that post-convergent-fix CR rounds collapse when only single-layer residue remains), **3 DEFER** (below — 2 reconfirmations of iter-50 DEFER class + 1 new story-spec editorial item), **5 DISMISS** (forward-compat `$def`s not dead; section-ID-enumeration vs publishable-slug prose conflation; frozen trace-artefact byte-count + line-pointer drift per iter-30 paper-trail rule; spec-intentional mode asymmetry). - **Dark-mode `status.<X>.fg` contrast failures against overridden `status.<X>.bg`.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (convergent). _Location:_ `packages/ui/tokens.json:58-78` (light `status.*.fg`) + `:187-202` (dark `$modes.dark.status.*.bg` overrides). _Nature:_ story Task 1 explicitly mandates "keep `fg` values equal across modes", so the dark `$modes.dark` overlay remaps only `status.<X>.bg` — leaving light-tuned fg (e.g. `status.critical.fg = oklch(45% 0.20 15)`) paired against dark bg (`oklch(20% 0.08 15)`) at ECH-computed ratios info **3.35:1**, success **3.03:1**, warning **3.79:1**, error **2.78:1**, critical **2.37:1** (all below AA 4.5 threshold). Story AC 1 only requires schema validation; contrast math is explicitly a Story 1.13 gate. _Carry-to:_ **Story 1.13** — add dark-mode `status.<X>.fg` remaps (e.g. `oklch(75% 0.14 <hue>)`) OR accept status fg inheritance with AA-failure signalling via the gate. **Story 1.12** emitter pipeline may also synthesize dark-mode fg via contrast-targeting algorithm.

- **`text.accent` + `border.accent` fail AA on several surface pairings.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (convergent). _Location:_ `packages/ui/tokens.json:51` (light `text.accent` = `{color.accent.default}`), `:56` (light `border.accent` = `{color.accent.focus}`), `:169-186` + `:524-536` (dark mode overlays without `accent` under `text` or `border`). _Nature:_ ECH computed `text.accent` (resolves to `accent.500 = oklch(54% 0.18 245)`) on dark `surface.default` **4.29:1** (fail), dark `surface.raised` **4.15:1** (fail), light `surface.raised` **4.31:1** (fail); only light `surface.default` passes at 4.71. `$modes.dark.color.text` + `.border` overlays omit `accent` remaps — only `accent.fg` is remapped. _Defer reason:_ same class as dark-mode status.fg defer above — substrate deliberately ships `accent.500` constant across modes; dark-mode text/border.accent contrast is Story 1.13 gate scope. _Carry-to:_ **Story 1.13** — three options: (a) add dark-mode `$modes.dark.color.text.accent` + `.border.accent` remaps pointing to a lighter accent variant (e.g. `{color.accent.400}`); (b) retune `accent.500` L upward; (c) emit `text.accent` as raised-surface-only constraint in Story 1.12 emitter with fallback to `text.primary` on default surfaces.
- **Surface slot collapse: `raised` / `inset` (light) + `raised` / `inset` / `overlay` (dark) alias to identical neutral values.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (convergent). _Location:_ `packages/ui/tokens.json:42-44` (light `surface.{raised,inset,overlay}`) + `:168-172` (dark). _Nature:_ light `surface.raised` and `surface.inset` both alias `{color.neutral.100}`; dark `surface.raised` + `surface.inset` + `surface.overlay` all alias `{color.neutral.900}`. - **OKLCH out-of-sRGB-gamut leaves: `status.warning.fg` (75°), `status.error.fg` (25°), `status.critical.fg` (15°) yield slightly-negative linear RGB components.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/ui/tokens.json:68` (warning.fg), `:72` (error.fg), `:76` (critical.fg). _Nature:_ ECH computed `oklch(58% 0.14 75)` → linear RGB `[0.40, 0.15, -0.019]` (blue channel negative); `oklch(45% 0.20 15)` → `[0.39, -0.012, 0.028]` (green channel negative); `oklch(52% 0.18 25)` → `[0.49, 0.024, 0.027]` (tight but in-gamut). Browsers clip on render, altering perceived hue/chroma and shifting actual contrast vs computed. _Defer reason:_ gamut-mapping is rendering-layer concern, not source-layer; Direction A value-fidelity is preserved at source. _Carry-to:_ **Story 1.12** emitter — optional gamut-check + fallback-to-in-gamut-neighbour pass on emit (map OKLCH to nearest sRGB boundary preserving hue). **Story 1.13** contrast gate — gamut-map before AA math so the gate operates on rendered pairings rather than abstract OKLCH literals.

---

### Classification methodology (`/bmad-code-review (args: "2")` — "Create action items")

Three parallel adversarial layers per `.claude/skills/bmad-code-review/steps/step-02-review.md`: Blind Hunter (`bmad-review-adversarial-general`; diff-only, no project context), Edge Case Hunter (`bmad-review-edge-case-hunter`; diff + repo read access; path-enumeration method), Acceptance Auditor (diff + spec file + context docs; AC-violation-only).

Triage bucketing per `step-03-triage.md`:

- `patch` — fix unambiguous, no human input needed.
- `defer` — real issue, not actionable now (e.g. scope carve-out, spec-silent hardening).
- `dismiss` — false positive, by-design, or handled elsewhere.
- `decision_needed` — ambiguous choice (not applicable when auditor found zero AC violations).

Under adversarial-triage-is-default (per `.ralph/PROMPT_build.md § Story Lifecycle: "EVERY CR action item becomes a QUEUE fix task unless IP records defer: <reason> per item. Adversarial triage is the default."`): every non-dismissed finding must either get a `patch` fix task queued or an explicit `defer: <reason>` recorded. Story 1.8's 6 defers above are all either Story 1.9-enforcement-side scope or spec-silent hardening — no patches needed for the `sm-verified → done` transition.

_Story 1.12 (token emitter pipeline → web CSS + Tailwind preset + TUI theme) — iter-66 `/bmad-code-review (args: "2")`. Three-layer adversarial review on commit `c14b6df` code surface (Ralph-bookkeeping files excluded). Acceptance Auditor returned **3 spec deviations**. After iter-36+iter-52+iter-59 two-layer convergence-doctrine triage + iter-58+iter-65 ZERO-PATCH doctrine applied to AA1: **0 PATCH, 0 DECISION-NEEDED, 10 DEFER (below), 26 DISMISS**. All 10 defers route to Story 1.13 (sync-gate / schema-validation / reliability / observability absorption), Story 1.13+ spec amendments (AA1/AA2/AA3), reliability follow-up (REPO_ROOT), or Epic 7/3 consumer stories (fontSize line-height). Closure: Story State `sm-verified → done` per FR14n matrix row 9 ZERO-PATCH + 10 DEFER ceiling (matches iter-59 Story 1.11 precedent within "5-10 DEFER" target). 7-iteration lifecycle held exactly (iter-60 drafted → iter-61 validated → iter-62 atdd-scaffolded → iter-63 in-dev → iter-64 traced → iter-65 sm-verified → iter-66 done). **Story 1.12 THIRD cumulative ZERO-PATCH CR precedent** (matches Story 1.10 iter-52 RE-RUN + Story 1.11 iter-59 first-round)._

- **Source-SHA resolver command literal deviation from spec § AC 1 carve-out.** _Source:_ Acceptance Auditor (pre-staged defense at iter-64 IP + iter-65 SM ZERO-PATCH precedent). _Location:_ `packages/ui/scripts/generate-tokens.ts:309` uses `git log -1 --format=%h --abbrev=12 -- packages/ui/tokens.json`; spec § AC 1 carve-out prescribes `git rev-parse --short=12 HEAD -- packages/ui/tokens.json`. _Nature:_ structurally-impossible-literal — `rev-parse --short=12 HEAD -- <path>` returns repo HEAD regardless of path (the `--` is a rev/path separator in `rev-parse` syntax, not a log-filter arg), violating the same carve-out paragraph's "NOT `HEAD` of the repo" constraint. Intent-matching `git log` returns the file's latest commit SHA (`6b1790a02adb`) — satisfies AC 1 prose literally. Deviation documented at 3 sites (emitter source-file header + Debug Log References row + Change Log v1.2 row). _Defer reason:_ ZERO-PATCH doctrine (iter-58+iter-65) — literal is self-contradictory, impl is correct per AC prose. Spec text should be harmonised at next opportunity. _Carry-to:_ **Story 1.13** pre-dev drafting — amend Story 1.12 § AC 1 carve-out literal command to the intent-matching `git log` form so future CR scans see matching spec + impl; or a dedicated spec-editorial story.
- **`.prettierignore` entry bypasses Task 6 prettier-normalization of two emitted outputs.** _Source:_ Acceptance Auditor + Blind Hunter (AA2 + BH#12 convergent). _Location:_ `.prettierignore:13-16` adds `packages/ui/src/tokens.css` + `packages/ui/tailwind.preset.ts`; spec Task 6 prescribes `pnpm exec prettier --write packages/ui/scripts/generate-tokens.ts packages/ui/src/tokens.css packages/ui/tailwind.preset.ts packages/devbox/tui/theme.py ...` before format:check. _Nature:_ prettier normalises OKLCH decimals (`0.20 → 0.2`), converts attribute-selector quote style (`"dark" → 'dark'`), and converts JSON-stringify double-quotes to single-quotes — none of which the emitter reproduces natively; running prettier on emitter outputs would break AC 2 byte-identical round-trip guarantee. Rationale documented in Debug Log ("emitter owns canonical byte-form of generated files; prettier owns the emitter source"). Task 6 format:check is green because outputs are ignored, not because they match prettier — AC 2 byte-identical holds because determinism is owned by emitter alone. _Defer reason:_ multi-layer-corroborated authoring-choice finding per iter-59 doctrine; fix is a spec-text amendment, not a code change. _Carry-to:_ **Story 1.13** (pre-merge source-output sync gate) spec drafting — amend Story 1.12 Task 6 prose to exclude emitted outputs from the prettier-normalization list + document the `.prettierignore` entry as part of the "emitter owns canonical byte-form" contract clause.
- **Manifest entry `INV-tokens-emitter` description paraphrases spec Task 5 trailing parenthetical.** _Source:_ Acceptance Auditor only (AA3). _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts:155` uses `... (emitter re-run + diff).`; spec Task 5 line 163 prescribes `... (emitter --check mode).`. _Nature:_ cosmetic description-text deviation — description field has no functional impact on `INV-tokens-emitter` contract (contract is `contentHash` pin + `sourcePath` + `id`). iter-63 dev described what the sync gate is expected to actually do (invoke emitter, diff outputs vs tracked state), not what its CLI verb is. _Defer reason:_ Story 1.13's sync-gate invocation nomenclature is TBD; reconciling now risks thrashing if Story 1.13 lands `re-run + diff` verb. _Carry-to:_ **Story 1.13** drafting — formalise sync-gate invocation nomenclature (`--check` vs `re-run + diff`) + align `invariants.manifest.ts:155` description text at that time.
- **`resolveSourceSha` invoked 4× per emitter run — TOCTOU window + perf.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (BH#2 + EH convergent). _Location:_ `packages/ui/scripts/generate-tokens.ts:309` called from `emitCss:409`, `emitTailwind:439`, `emitPython:582`, `main:624`. _Nature:_ each of the three emit stages plus `main` independently spawns `execFileSync('git', ...)` — 4 subprocess spawns per run. Theoretical TOCTOU: concurrent `tokens.json` rewrite mid-emission could stamp three outputs with two different SHAs. Not a correctness defect under normal invocation (Story 1.12 determinism smokes run without concurrent edits; all three outputs carry matching SHA `6b1790a02adb`). _Defer reason:_ authoring factoring decision per iter-59 doctrine; no AC violation. _Carry-to:_ **Story 1.13** (pre-merge sync gate) — hoist SHA resolution to `main` once and pass through as a param; benefit amplified when sync-gate invokes emitter in `--check` mode (single subprocess vs four).
- **`resolveSourceSha` silent fallback to `uncommitted-<content-hash>` swallows multiple failure modes.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (BH#1 + EH{git-missing, maxBuffer, empty-stdout, whitespace-stdout, non-hex-stdout} — 5-vector convergent). _Location:_ `packages/ui/scripts/generate-tokens.ts:307-321`. _Nature:_ fallback activates on any `execFileSync` non-zero exit OR empty stdout, treating "git not on PATH / stdlib maxBuffer exceeded / git output malformed / file untracked" as a single branch with no observability. Under normal conditions (git present + file tracked), fallback is never reached. _Defer reason:_ multi-layer-corroborated reliability gap per iter-59 doctrine; not triggered under Story 1.12 AC-validation scope. _Carry-to:_ **Story 1.13** pre-commit gate observability — distinguish `uncommitted` vs `git-missing` vs `stderr-error` in the provenance header (e.g. `source-sha: git-unavailable-<hash>`) so CI pipelines can fail-fast on environment misconfiguration instead of silently switching to content-hash provenance.
- **Alias-cycle detector may false-positive on diamond alias DAGs.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (BH#4 + EH{diamond-false-positive} convergent). _Location:_ `packages/ui/scripts/generate-tokens.ts:360-384` (`resolveValue` `visited` Set handling). _Nature:_ `visited` accumulates alias paths via `new Set([...visited, seg])` but the set tracks segments by path-string, not by canonical leaf identity — a diamond graph (A→B, A→C, B→D, C→D resolved within a single leaf's chain) could trigger false-positive "cycle" error. Not triggered by current `tokens.json` (no diamond aliases present; smoke 2's 2-hop chains exercised successfully). _Defer reason:_ multi-layer-corroborated path gap per iter-59 doctrine; not triggered. _Carry-to:_ **Story 1.13** test harness — add synthetic diamond-DAG fixture to exercise alias-cycle detector; key `visited` on resolved-leaf identity rather than alias-path strings.
- **`walkLeaves` silently drops non-leaf, non-object values.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (BH#5 + EH{array-as-node, non-object-primitive} convergent). _Location:_ `packages/ui/scripts/generate-tokens.ts:342-354`. _Nature:_ if `tokens.json` contains an array, a raw string, or a stray number at a non-leaf path, `walkLeaves` skips it without warning; regressions from typos-in-source are invisible. Trusted DTCG input today (all sources Story 1.11-frozen and schema-validated); not triggered. _Defer reason:_ multi-layer-corroborated schema-validation gap per iter-59 doctrine. _Carry-to:_ **Story 1.13** schema-validation gate — `tokens.json` must schema-validate before the emitter runs so malformed sources fail fast; emitter can then trust its input invariants.
- **`REPO_ROOT` resolver brittle — 3 hardcoded `..` hops + no `realpath` guard.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (BH#7 + EH{fileURLToPath-no-realpath, hardcoded-depth} convergent). _Location:_ `packages/ui/scripts/generate-tokens.ts:278-281`. _Nature:_ `REPO_ROOT = path.resolve(dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url)), '..', '..', '..')` assumes the emitter lives exactly at `packages/ui/scripts/`. If moved, symlinked, or invoked via pnpm-store path, `REPO_ROOT` resolves silently wrong. Not triggered in Story 1.12 scope (emitter ran successfully 5× across determinism smokes). _Defer reason:_ multi-layer-corroborated portability concern per iter-59 doctrine. _Carry-to:_ reliability follow-up story OR **Epic 3** (packages/ralph install-boundary scope) — discover repo root via `git rev-parse --show-toplevel` OR upward `package.json` walk with `name === 'ralph-bmad'` sentinel; fall back to hardcoded depth.
- **`parseInt` on breakpoint values silently accepts non-`px` suffix + NaN leak to Python literal.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (BH#9 + EH{rem-em-suffix, NaN-on-garbage} convergent). _Location:_ `packages/ui/scripts/generate-tokens.ts:571` (`collectPyGroups` breakpoint branch). _Nature:_ `parseInt(resolved.replace(/px$/, ''), 10)` accepts `640rem` as `640` (silently drops `rem`), accepts `abc` as `NaN` (which stringifies as bare `NaN` in the Python output — not a valid literal without `float('nan')` wrap; import-time `SyntaxError` in `theme.py`). Current `tokens.json` breakpoints are all `px`-suffixed (enforced by iter-56 source authoring); not triggered. _Defer reason:_ multi-layer-corroborated schema-validation gap per iter-59 doctrine. _Carry-to:_ **Story 1.13** schema-validation — regex-pin breakpoint `$value` to `/^\d+px$/` or equivalent; emitter-side defense: throw if resolved doesn't match `/^\d+px$/` instead of silent NaN.
- **`emitFontSize` hardcodes `lineHeight: "1.5"` for every scale step.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (BH#19 + EH{hardcoded-line-height} convergent). _Location:_ `packages/ui/scripts/generate-tokens.ts:504`. _Nature:_ every size in the Tailwind preset receives the same 1.5 line-height regardless of source; ux-design-specification.md Direction A does not specify per-scale line-heights (tight headlines / generous body / compact captions). Authoring choice at iter-63 dev — Tailwind v4 `fontSize` tuple form supports `['size', 'lineHeight']` but iter-56 source does not populate per-scale line-heights. Not an AC violation — AC 4 does not mandate per-scale line-heights. _Defer reason:_ multi-layer-corroborated authoring-choice finding per iter-59 doctrine (DEFER not PATCH). _Carry-to:_ **Epic 7 Story 7-1** (`packages/ui` scaffolding + token consumption) — reveal whether consumer components need ramp-specific line-heights; if yes, extend `tokens.json` `type` group with per-scale `lineHeight` leaves in a follow-up source-layer story and remap emitter to pull per-scale values. OR **Epic 3 Story 3-X** (TUI theme consumption) — Textual line-height is row-based; may not exercise this gap at all.

## Deferred from: code review of 1-13-token-quality-gates-schema-validation-wcag-aa-contrast-source-output-sync (2026-04-21)

_Story 1.13 (token quality gates — schema validation + WCAG AA contrast + source-output sync) — iter-73 `/bmad-code-review (args: "2")`. Three-layer adversarial review on commit `8f5d6f4` code surface (`.ralph/tmp/story-1-13-cr-diff.patch`; Ralph-bookkeeping files excluded). Blind Hunter ~30 findings diff-only; Edge Case Hunter ~80 findings diff + project read (path-enumeration method); Acceptance Auditor 14 spec deviations (5/6 ACs MET, 6/7 Tasks MET). After iter-36+iter-52+iter-59+iter-65+iter-66 two-layer convergence-doctrine triage + iter-58+iter-65+iter-72 ZERO-PATCH doctrine applied to authoring-choice findings + iter-71 architectural-defer precedent: **0 PATCH, 0 DECISION-NEEDED, 13 DEFER (below), ~112 DISMISS**. - **Post-commit SHA drift on emitter outputs.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (convergent; pre-flagged at iter-71 trace). _Location:_ `packages/ui/scripts/generate-tokens.ts` `resolveSourceSha` + `makeProvenanceHeader`. _Nature:_ emitter SHA-resolver uses `git log -1 --format=%h --abbrev=12 -- packages/ui/tokens.json` to stamp outputs. At dev-time (pre-commit), the resolver returns the PREVIOUS commit SHA because the new commit hasn't landed. After the commit lands (post-commit), re-running `--check` computes the NEW SHA → provenance header byte-differs → sync-gate reports drift on unchanged source. Inline iter-71 fix: re-emit + commit-again. Architectural bug, not a Story 1.13 regression — the Story 1.12 SHA-resolver contract carries the defect. _Defer reason:_ HIGH-severity but architectural; fix requires either (a) switch provenance identifier to content-hash-of-source (deterministic + uncommitted-safe — PREFERRED); (b) document dual-commit pattern + add post-commit CI hook; (c) accept + document as known limitation. Fix design warrants its own story. _Carry-to:_ **Epic 3** reliability (or new Story 1.17-TBD) — ship option (a) with a content-hash provenance header that eliminates the dual-commit workflow entirely.
- **Pre-commit `files:` regex triggers only on `packages/ui/tokens.json`; schema/contrast gates don't fire on schema-only or source-file-only edits.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (convergent). _Location:_ `.pre-commit-config.yaml:84,91` — `files: ^packages/ui/tokens\.json$` on both `tokens-schema` and `tokens-contrast` hooks. _Nature:_ editing `tokens.schema.json` (Story 1.10-frozen schema) OR `color-math.ts` / `check-tokens-contrast.ts` (the gate's own source) does NOT re-trigger the gates at pre-commit. Pre-merge `keel-invariants:check-all` does catch drift via manifest hash + sync-gate, but the pre-commit coverage hole exists. _Defer reason:_ scope carve-out per Story 1.13 § AC 5 pre-commit tier budget (≤10s; running the full gate on every schema/src edit is out of budget); deliberate authoring choice. _Carry-to:_ future hardening story (pre-commit `files:` regex union for schema + gate sources with caching) or CI-side enforcement (pre-merge slow `keel-invariants:check-all` covers the gap today).
- **`parseOklch` accepts unitless L without `%`; L>1 produces silent garbage luminance.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (convergent). _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/color-math.ts` `parseOklch` regex + L-extraction. _Nature:_ regex `^oklch\(\s*([\d.]+)(%?)\s+...` makes `%` optional. `oklch(50 0.18 245)` (typo dropping `%`) parses to L=50 (not 0.5), producing enormous LMS values that hard-clamp to [0,1] — downstream contrast math runs on nonsense luminance with no warning. Schema gate would catch this via `leafColor` OKLCH pattern (requires `%`) so trigger is unreachable in practice, but defence-in-depth is absent. _Defer reason:_ input-validation robustness gap; schema gate already enforces the `%` at the source layer. _Carry-to:_ Story 1.17-TBD color-math hardening — tighten `parseOklch` regex to reject unitless L + surface an `oklch-parse-error` finding kind distinct from ratio failures.
- **`gamutMap` 3-iteration cap + silent hard-clamp may skew luminance on severely out-of-gamut OKLCH leaves.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (convergent; carry-forward from iter-59 Story 1.11 defer #5 contrast-side and iter-71 post-staged). _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/color-math.ts` `gamutMap` (3-iteration chroma-reduction loop then hard-clamp). _Nature:_ `oklch(78% 0.20 15)` (dark-mode `status.critical.fg`) at high L + high C in red direction may need >3 iterations to reach gamut. After iter-3, hard-clamp applies per-channel — changing luminance non-uniformly. The gate's ratio then diverges from what a CSS-Color-4-compliant browser would render (browsers use binary-search gamut mapping). No `isInGamut` post-clamp check; no `gamut-mapped-to-clamp` finding kind. _Defer reason:_ multi-layer-corroborated authoring-choice per iter-59 doctrine — algorithm is deterministic + fixes Story 1.11 CR defer #5 (OKLCH out-of-gamut leaves); advanced convergence is Epic 7 consumer concern. _Carry-to:_ **Epic 7** advanced color pipeline OR Story 1.17-TBD — replace `C*=0.9` schedule with CSS Color 4 binary-search gamut mapping; add `mapped-to-clamp` kind in finding output.
- **`parseOklch` alpha channel silently dropped; compositional contrast not measured.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter (single-layer; upgraded by convergence with Blind Hunter `parseOklch` pair). _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/color-math.ts:23` alpha group `(?:\s*\/\s*[\d.]+%?)?` is non-capturing. _Nature:_ `oklch(50% 0.18 245 / 0.5)` parses to L=50%, C=0.18, H=245; alpha discarded. Semi-transparent foreground over a known bg would show a compositional colour with lower effective contrast; the gate measures the un-composited fg. Current tokens.json has no alpha-bearing leaves (source schema disallows via leafColor pattern) — gap unreachable today but robustness concern for future overlay modes. _Defer reason:_ authoring-style input-validation concern; not triggered by Story 1.11-frozen source. _Carry-to:_ **Epic 7** advanced color pipeline — add alpha composition + warn on alpha-bearing leaves in the gate when the source schema is relaxed to allow rgba-style colors in overlays.
- **SHA resolver conflates `exit-nonzero empty-stderr` with `exit-0 empty-stdout` — both map to `uncommitted-<hash>`.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (convergent). _Location:_ `packages/ui/scripts/generate-tokens.ts` `resolveSourceSha` catch-block. _Nature:_ spec AA1 design distinguished 4 branches (`<12-hex-sha>` / `git-unavailable-` / `stderr-error-` / `uncommitted-`); impl's catch handles `ENOENT` → `git-unavailable-`, `stderr.trim().length > 0` → `stderr-error-`, else → `uncommitted-`. A broken git that exits non-zero with empty stderr (unusual but possible — signal termination, git hard-killed) falls to the `uncommitted-` branch, losing the AA1 distinction. _Defer reason:_ rare failure mode, pragmatic tradeoff; architectural fix needs design around `execFileSync` error shape. _Carry-to:_ emitter reliability follow-up (Epic 3 or Story 1.17-TBD) — enumerate `err.code` / `err.signal` / `err.status` branches explicitly; add `ci-misconfig-<hash>` tag for the empty-stderr non-zero-exit case.
- **Pair-enumeration incomplete — missing `accent.fg × accent.*`, `accent.focus × surface.*`, `severity × surface.{raised,inset,overlay}`, `state × non-default`, `text.accent × surface.{inset,overlay}`, `status.*.fg × surface.*` cross-surface pairs.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter × 5 findings + Acceptance Auditor (convergent). _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/check-tokens-contrast.ts` `PAIRS` table (51 entries). _Nature:_ `accent.fg` (near-white `oklch(99% 0 0)`) is used as foreground on accent buttons; no pair enumerates `accent.fg × accent.default` or `accent.fg × accent.600`. `accent.focus` is a WCAG 1.4.11 UI-component indicator not tested against surfaces. `severity.*` and `state.*` only tested against `surface.default` (tooltip/menu-on-raised scenarios uncovered). `text.accent` only paired with `surface.default`/`surface.raised`, not `inset`/`overlay`. `status.*.fg` only paired with its own `status.*.bg`, not free-surface rendering. _Defer reason:_ authoring-choice scope (spec pair-enumeration table was intentionally finite at drafting time; full cartesian is pre-commit budget-expensive); contrast-gate completeness follow-up. _Carry-to:_ **Story 1.17-TBD** contrast-gate completeness — expand PAIRS to include accent.fg × accent.* / accent.focus × surface.* / severity × raised/inset/overlay / state × raised / text.accent × inset/overlay / status.*.fg × surface.* cross-surface; budget audit vs pre-commit ≤500ms target.
- **`border.default × surface.*` pairs dropped from gate by dev reclassification ("decorative separator not WCAG 1.4.11 UI component"); not reflected in spec text.** _Source:_ Acceptance Auditor (single-layer spec deviation) + Edge Case Hunter (implicit). _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/check-tokens-contrast.ts:228-259` (impl omits) vs spec line 127 (enumeration table mandates 4 `border.*` pairs at threshold 3.0). _Nature:_ spec mandated border.default × surface.default/raised at threshold 3.0 (per WCAG 1.4.11 non-text UI component). Dev iter-70 dropped both `border.default` pairs citing "decorative separator between same-family surfaces is not a WCAG-1.4.11 UI-component"; kept only `border.accent × surface.*` at threshold 3.0 (focus indicator). Ratio computation with current tokens showed `border.default` pairs failing at 1.11-1.31 vs threshold 3.0 — dev reclass avoided red-on-landing at the cost of spec deviation. Recorded in dev IP + Debug Log inline comment, not in spec text. _Defer reason:_ authoring-choice finding per iter-59 doctrine; dev rationale is defensible but should be captured as a spec amendment. _Carry-to:_ spec editorial amendment (Story 1.13 v1.7 Change Log row OR new spec-amendments story) — harmonise spec pair-table line 127 with the "decorative-separator-not-UI-component" distinction + cite WCAG 1.4.11 scope.
- **`color.accent.500` (54→50%) + `color.accent.600` (46→42%) retunes applied beyond Task 2 retune table.** _Source:_ Acceptance Auditor (single-layer spec deviation). _Location:_ `packages/ui/tokens.json:22-31` (retuned leaves with `$description` citing Story 1.13 retune). _Nature:_ Task 2 retune table listed only `color.status.info.fg` (52→42%) + `color.status.warning.fg` (58→44%) for light-mode retunes. Dev iter-70 added accent.500 + accent.600 L-ramp retunes citing "text-on-raised-surface headroom" (Debug Log). Retunes land in source alongside `$description` provenance + are documented in manifest INV-tokens-source hash + emitter re-run. Scope decision is sound (resolve text.accent × surface.raised 4.47 light failure) but not spec-authorised. _Defer reason:_ over-scope retune documented in-place with rationale; spec v1.7 amendment should reflect. _Carry-to:_ spec editorial amendment — add light-mode accent.500 + accent.600 entries to Task 2 retune table (or new § AC 2 carve-out subsection "accent-ramp headroom retune") with cited reasoning + pre/post ratios.
- **`INV-tokens-contrast-check` description paraphrases spec (pair-ordering + added `border.accent × surface` + "mode-aware walker" wording).** _Source:_ Acceptance Auditor (single-layer) + Blind Hunter implicit (manifest-paraphrase is iter-66 AA3 pattern). _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts:170-171`. _Nature:_ spec Task 5 line 199 mandated category order `text × surface / severity × surface / state × surface / status.fg × status.bg / accent × surface`; impl reordered to `text × surface / status.fg × status.bg / severity × surface / state × surface / accent × surface / border.accent × surface pair`. Added `border.accent × surface` addendum + replaced `alias-flatten walker as the emitter` with `mode-aware walker (dark overlay wins when present, else base; aliases then flatten against base)`. Functional contract held by `contentHash` pin + `sourcePath` + `id`; description field is cosmetic. _Defer reason:_ iter-66 AA3 precedent — manifest description paraphrase under ZERO-PATCH doctrine; harmonise at editorial pass. _Carry-to:_ spec editorial or dedicated manifest-description tightening — align `invariants.manifest.ts:170-171` text to spec Task 5 line 199 OR amend spec to match impl's more-accurate wording.
- **`leafBreakpoint` regex has redundant nested `^...$` inside outer `^...$` alternation.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter + Acceptance Auditor (3-layer convergent; functionally harmless). _Location:_ `packages/ui/tokens.schema.json:55` — `"pattern": "^(\\{[a-z][a-z0-9]*(\\.[a-z0-9][a-z0-9-]*)+\\}|^\\d+px$)$"`. _Nature:_ inner `^\d+px$` within outer `^...$` alternation works correctly (ECMA regex accepts redundant anchors) but is authoring imprecision; `^(\\{...\\}|\\d+px)$` is the clean form. Also permits `0px`, `00000px`, etc. (no leading-zero forbid), and does not permit `1.5px`, `16rem`, `4em` (deliberate narrowing). _Defer reason:_ cosmetic; schema contract functionally correct. _Carry-to:_ schema hygiene pass (Story 1.17-TBD or editorial amendment) — collapse to `^(\\{...\\}|\\d+px)$`; optionally forbid leading zeros via `[1-9]\d*|0`.
- **Dark-mode `severity.*` + `state.*` overlays authored as explicit OKLCH literals instead of alias propagation through `status.*.fg`/`accent.default`.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter + Acceptance Auditor (convergent). _Location:_ `packages/ui/tokens.json:211-222` — `$modes.dark.color.severity.{low,medium,high,critical}` + `$modes.dark.color.state.{pending,in-progress,blocked,done}` as literal OKLCH rather than `{color.status.*.fg}` / `{color.accent.default}` aliases. _Nature:_ spec § AC 2 carve-out line 148 expected severity + state to ALIAS into `color.status.*.fg` / `color.accent.default` — "dark-mode retunes propagate automatically through the alias graph to severity + state pairs". Impl converted to explicit literals because dark-overlay `severity.low` aliasing to `{color.status.info.fg}` would pick up LIGHT-mode `status.info.fg` (since `resolveAgainstBase` doesn't consult the overlay for alias targets) — literal overlay was the pragmatic fix. Future retunes of `status.*.fg` will NOT propagate to dark `severity.*` silently. No invariant enforces the "dark severity tracks status" relationship. _Defer reason:_ authoring-style deviation with implementation-rational cause; fix is either (a) mode-aware alias resolution in walker (scope-creep) or (b) document the break-the-cascade pattern in spec. _Carry-to:_ Story 1.17-TBD authoring-style alignment — either extend alias resolver to prefer overlay when resolving alias targets, or pin spec language that dark-overlay severity/state must be authored as literals (not aliases).
- **Ajv `strict: true` mode could fail-closed on `tokens.schema.json` edits introducing unknown keywords.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (convergent). _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/check-tokens-schema.ts:33` — `new Ajv2020({ allErrors: true, strict: true })`. _Nature:_ strict-mode Ajv throws at `ajv.compile(schema)` on unknown keywords (custom DTCG vocabulary, stray `$comment` at unusual levels, unrecognised format). The gate's try/catch swallows this to `{ status: 'error', message }` + exit 1, indistinguishable from "token drift" at the CI layer. A harmless schema edit could hard-fail the gate. _Defer reason:_ robustness concern; fixed under current Story 1.10 schema (Ajv recognises all current keywords). _Carry-to:_ schema-gate robustness follow-up — distinguish `status: 'schema-error'` from `status: 'error'` (Ajv compile failure vs thrown exception); surface Ajv's `addKeyword` / `addVocabulary` hook if DTCG vocabulary grows.


## Deferred from: code review of 1-14-release-please-monorepo-config-single-bundled-mode (2026-04-21)

_Story 1.14 (`release-please monorepo config — single-bundled mode`) — iter-80 `/bmad-code-review (args: "2")`. Three-layer adversarial review (Blind Hunter 20 findings diff-only + Edge Case Hunter ~27 findings diff + repo-read + Acceptance Auditor 6/6 ACs MET / SCOPE-CARVED). FOURTH cumulative ZERO-PATCH CR precedent (Stories 1.11 iter-59 + 1.12 iter-66 + 1.13 iter-73 + 1.14 iter-80). 10 DEFER + ~13 DISMISS after convergence-doctrine triage. All 10 items route to Story 13.5 (6), spec amendments (3), or Epic 3 reliability (1)._

- **Root `.` has no `version` field in `package.json`; `release-type: node` expects `package.json.version`.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter + Blind Hunter (convergent). _Location:_ `package.json` (root — verified absent: `private: true`, no `version` field) vs `.github/release-please-config.json:20` (pins `. : { component: keel, package-name: keel }`) + `.github/.release-please-manifest.json:2` (`.`: `0.0.0`). _Nature:_ release-please's `node` release-type reads/writes `package.json.version`; the root has no such field. On first-run release-please may throw, synthesize a `version` key (mutating root shape), or fall back to `release-as`-style behavior (undocumented). _Defer reason:_ runtime-only failure surfaces at Story 13.5 first-run; substrate-level fix options are architectural (add root `"version": "0.0.0"`, OR remove `.` entry from config+manifest, OR switch root to `release-type: manifest` while keeping workspaces as `node`). _Carry-to:_ Story 13.5 workflow delivery — resolve root-path handling in config OR root package.json shape before first Release PR.
- **`linked-versions.components: ["keel"]` plugin shape — 17 packages all carry `component: "keel"` but `linked-versions.components` lists only one component name.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (convergent). _Location:_ `.github/release-please-config.json:8` (`plugins: [{ type: linked-versions, groupName: keel, components: [keel] }]`) vs `:21-37` (17 packages × `component: keel`). _Nature:_ release-please's `linked-versions` plugin uses `components` as the list of MEMBER components to link. Listing one component "keel" when 17 packages share `component: "keel"` may deduplicate to "group of one member," leaving 16 packages un-linked and producing 16 separate Release PRs despite `separate-pull-requests: false`. Alternatively, release-please may interpret this correctly as "one group spanning all 17 packages bearing component: keel." Empirical validation needed. _Defer reason:_ plugin semantics not verifiable without live release-please invocation; Story 13.5 workflow first-run is the natural test bed. _Carry-to:_ Story 13.5 workflow delivery — empirically validate single-bundled PR shape on first `push` to `main`; adjust plugin config if 16 separate PRs surface.
- **`docs/invariants/release.md` § Commit-type → semver mapping table has three semantic errors.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (convergent). _Location:_ `docs/invariants/release.md:34-46`. _Nature:_ (a) `bump-patch-for-minor-pre-major` flag description at line 14 + 43 misstates the flag's effect — per release-please docs the flag downgrades pre-1.0 BREAKING-change minor → patch, not `feat:` → patch; (b) table row `perf:`, `refactor:`, `docs:` → patch contradicts release-please default (only `feat:` emits minor, `fix:` emits patch, BREAKING emits major; `perf:`/`refactor:`/`docs:` are non-bumping and appear only in changelog); (c) hidden-types row `chore:`, `test:`, `build:`, `ci:` claims "no user-visible bump" which conflates `changelog-sections` visibility with bump arithmetic — release-please's bump classifier is independent of section visibility. _Defer reason:_ spec-authoring error documented in release.md; no impl-side fix needed (config flags are correct); spec amendment needed. _Carry-to:_ release.md spec amendment — rewrite § Commit-type → semver mapping to correctly describe what each flag governs + split non-bumping types into their own row.
- **Missing `bootstrap-sha` / `initial-version` config pins — first-run release-please scans full git history.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (convergent). _Location:_ `.github/release-please-config.json` (top-level; no `bootstrap-sha` or `initial-version` field present). _Nature:_ release-please on first run against a manifest-based single-bundled config with every entry at `0.0.0` and no existing tags will scan the full git history from the first commit to find conventional-commit bumps. The first Release PR may be enormous / slow / cross-cutting pre-invariant-discipline commits. Also: `0.0.0` starting state interacts idiosyncratically with `bump-minor-pre-major` (whether `feat:` emits `0.1.0` or `0.0.1` at the bootstrap boundary). _Defer reason:_ runtime-only concern; Story 13.5 workflow owns the pin. _Carry-to:_ Story 13.5 workflow delivery — pin `bootstrap-sha: <merge-commit-of-Story-1.14>` + optionally `initial-version: "0.1.0"` to sidestep the `0.0.0` bootstrap boundary.
- **Missing release-PR ergonomic + safety config — no `pull-request-title-pattern`, header, labels, `draft`, or `prerelease`.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter. _Location:_ `.github/release-please-config.json` (top-level). _Nature:_ the config omits `pull-request-title-pattern` (defaults may collide with repo's `chore/*` / `feat/*` PR-title conventions), `pull-request-header`, release-PR labels (important for triage automation), and `draft: true` / `prerelease: true` safety flags. The moment Story 13.5 merges the first Release PR, release-please auto-publishes a real GitHub Release at whatever semver bumps have accumulated — unreviewed. _Defer reason:_ safety + ergonomics not load-bearing at substrate-authoring time; Story 13.5 workflow owns the first-run safety gate. _Carry-to:_ Story 13.5 workflow delivery — before merging the first Release PR set `draft: true` or `prerelease: true`, add release-PR labels (`release`, `release-please`), pin a title pattern, and author a header.
- **Single-bundled hash-cascade — release-please rewrites `.github/.release-please-manifest.json` atomically on Release-PR merge, invalidating `INV-release-please-manifest` pinned `contentHash` (`4df2aacf…`).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts:197` (INV-release-please-manifest). _Nature:_ linked-versions single-bundled merge atomically updates every manifest key; contentHash drift at the Story 1.9 sync-gate will trigger on the next merge unless something regenerates the pin. No automation wires this. Similar cascade exists for `INV-release-please-config` when a fork edits the config per `release.md § Fork extension`. _Defer reason:_ cascade behaviour surfaces first at Story 13.5; one fix-class (post-merge hook to regenerate hash + amend invariants.manifest.ts) is Story 13.5 scope; another (exclude manifest file from content-hash pinning and pin shape via schema check) is a substrate architectural choice. _Carry-to:_ Story 13.5 workflow delivery — add post-Release-PR-merge hash-regen hook that updates `invariants.manifest.ts` for `INV-release-please-manifest` in the Release PR commit itself (atomic) OR switch `INV-release-please-manifest` from contentHash-pin to schema-pin.
- **Release-please-action default `config-file` + `manifest-file` paths differ from `.github/` placement.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `docs/invariants/release.md:52-54` (§ Consumption). _Nature:_ `googleapis/release-please-action`'s default `config-file` + `manifest-file` inputs resolve to repo-root `release-please-config.json` + `.release-please-manifest.json` (NOT `.github/`-prefixed). Story 1.14 pins `.github/`-prefixed paths per AC 1 (Epic-1 preference over architecture.md:807 root placement). release.md § Consumption asserts Story 13.5 will override via explicit `config-file:` + `manifest-file:` inputs — this claim is correct but the release.md text doesn't assert the default-vs-override distinction prominently. A Story 13.5 workflow author who misses the override will see a runtime "config file not found" CI failure. _Defer reason:_ scope-carved to Story 13.5 workflow authoring; release.md can be tightened. _Carry-to:_ Story 13.5 workflow delivery — explicit `config-file: .github/release-please-config.json` + `manifest-file: .github/.release-please-manifest.json` action inputs; OR release.md amendment hardening § Consumption "default search is repo-root; `.github/` requires explicit overrides" language.
- **`architecture.md:597` citation stale — cites "package-extraction posture" but `:597` is `null vs undefined` content.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter + Acceptance Auditor (convergent). _Location:_ `_bmad-output/planning-artifacts/architecture.md:597` (confirmed live content: "Null vs undefined: `undefined` for absent…"); cited from `docs/invariants/release.md:26` + Story 1.14 spec line 148. _Nature:_ line-number citation drifted from source; the spec inherited the stale pointer at drafting time, dev-story faithfully propagated it. Pre-existing spec error, not a dev-story deviation. _Defer reason:_ editorial amendment across 2 sites (spec line 148 + release.md:26) — actual "package-extraction posture" content needs locating in architecture.md (likely moved or re-anchored). _Carry-to:_ release.md + Story 1.14 spec citation amendment — either remove `:597` qualifier (point at section, not line) OR locate the actual package-extraction paragraph and re-cite.
- **`architecture.md:807` source-tree drift — shows `release-please-config.json` at repo root (not `.github/`).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `_bmad-output/planning-artifacts/architecture.md:807` (source-tree section shows `release-please-config.json` at root and `.github/release-please-manifest.json` under `.github/` — inconsistent placement). _Nature:_ architecture.md § Source-tree drifted from Story 1.14 AC 1 `.github/`-prefixed path decision. Per RALPH.md 2026-04-19 Epic-1-wins-over-architecture precedent, Epic-1 AC is authoritative; architecture.md amendment is the route. _Defer reason:_ editorial amendment on architecture.md; follow-up substrate-story scope. _Carry-to:_ architecture.md source-tree amendment — align to Story 1.14 AC 1 (`.github/release-please-config.json` + `.github/.release-please-manifest.json`) + consistent `.github/` placement for both files.
- **contentHash line-ending / Prettier normalization drift (class-of-issue shared with all 19 prior substrate hash-pins).** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (convergent; multi-layer). _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts:189,197,205` (INV-release-please-config + INV-release-please-manifest + INV-release-please-rationale). _Nature:_ hashes computed over file bytes including trailing newline. Any editor / Prettier / EditorConfig that normalizes line endings (CRLF → LF, LF → CRLF), trailing-newline presence, BOM, etc. invalidates the pinned sha256 at the Story 1.9 sync-gate. No `.gitattributes` entries pin these 3 files to `text eol=lf`. This is the same architectural class as Story 1.13 iter-71 post-commit SHA-drift finding (iter-73 CR absorbed that as a DEFER to content-hash provenance work). _Defer reason:_ architectural class — candidate resolution is content-hash-of-normalised-source (LF-canonical) OR switch to a provenance identifier that survives format-only edits (e.g., canonical-JSON hash, AST hash). Same Epic 3 reliability scope as Story 1.13 iter-71 finding. _Carry-to:_ Epic 3 reliability — content-hash provenance hardening story (unified fix covering all 20 invariant entries; optionally add `.gitattributes` `text eol=lf` + BOM stripping as a bridge tactic).
- **`docs/invariants/release.md` § Fork extension incomplete — regen-script path under-documented; tag-separator migration implicit.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `docs/invariants/release.md:48-50`. _Nature:_ (a) § Fork extension says "letting the Story 1.9 sync-gate re-hash the file at pre-merge" but the sync-gate is a VERIFIER (reports drift), not a re-hasher — no regen script exists. A fork that edits the config must manually regenerate `invariants.manifest.ts:INV-release-please-config.contentHash`; the section doesn't document that. (b) Switching to per-package mode introduces tag-separator concerns (unique per-component tags like `@keel/audit-v0.1.0`) that the fork-extension section doesn't cover; the claim "manifest format is unchanged across both modes" is true for the manifest file shape itself but incomplete in the broader migration picture. _Defer reason:_ documentation gap; substrate behaviour correct; spec expansion. _Carry-to:_ release.md § Fork extension amendment — add regen command (e.g., `sha256sum .github/release-please-config.json | awk '{print $1}'` + update `invariants.manifest.ts:INV-release-please-config.contentHash`) + note tag-separator implications when switching to per-package mode.

## Deferred from: code review of 1-15-renovate-config-with-version-pinning-rules-i7 (2026-04-21)

_Story 1.15 (`.github/renovate.json` I7 version-pinning config + `INV-deps-version-pinning` + `INV-renovate-rationale`) — iter-87 `/bmad-code-review (args: "2")`. Three-layer Ralph-hosted adversarial fan-out in parallel fresh-context Sonnet subagents: Blind Hunter (diff-only) 6 findings, Edge Case Hunter (diff + repo-read) 10 findings, Acceptance Auditor (AC-verification) all 4 ACs MET / SCOPE-CARVED + 2 pre-existing spec Dev Notes citation drifts. FIFTH cumulative ZERO-PATCH CR precedent (Stories 1.11/1.12/1.13/1.14 → 1.15). 7-iteration `drafted → done` lifecycle held exactly (iter-81 → iter-87). 10 DEFERs — all defensive-hardening / spec-amendment / downstream-consumer-validation candidates natural-scope for Story 2.1 devbox landing OR Epic 3 reliability OR follow-up renovate.md + spec amendments; none are shipping-blockers for the substrate-only `.github/renovate.json` + 2 invariants landing._

- **Redundant `matchPackageNames: ["vitest"]` on Vitest packageRule; fork-maintainer footgun.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (convergent). _Location:_ `.github/renovate.json:13-14` (Vitest rule). _Nature:_ `matchPackageNames: ["vitest"]` is fully redundant with the `^vitest($|/)` pattern which also matches the bare `vitest` package (alternation: `vitest` followed by end-of-string OR `/`). The additive-OR semantics of `matchPackageNames` + `matchPackagePatterns` mean both are live but only the patterns load-bear for scoped `@vitest/*` coverage. Zero functional defect today. Risk: a fork maintainer reads the rule, concludes `matchPackageNames` is the primary hook, removes the pattern, and inadvertently unguards `@vitest/*` ecosystem + any future `vitest/` subpath package. _Defer reason:_ cosmetic; no runtime impact; downstream fork-hardening. _Carry-to:_ packageRule cleanup pass (drop redundant `matchPackageNames: ["vitest"]`) OR renovate.md § Per-package pinning rules amendment clarifying the redundancy.

- **`vitest-environment-*` hyphen-separator coverage gap.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.github/renovate.json:13` (Vitest `matchPackagePatterns`). _Nature:_ `^vitest($|/)` matches bare `vitest` + `vitest/subpath`, and `^@vitest/` catches scoped `@vitest/ui`, `@vitest/browser`, etc. Neither pattern covers hyphen-separated community packages like `vitest-environment-nuxt`, `vitest-environment-miniflare`, `vitest-pool-workers` — they match `^vitest` but not `^vitest($|/)` (the alternation requires `/` or end-of-string after `vitest`). If a downstream story installs one, it falls through to top-level `rangeStrategy: replace` rather than the `vitest` pin group. _Defer reason:_ spec enumerates only Vitest core + `@vitest/*`; community packages fall outside I7 substrate scope until a consumer story installs them. _Carry-to:_ Epic 13 test-runner landing OR Story 1.16 Vitest install — add a fifth `matchPackagePatterns` entry like `^vitest-` to the Vitest rule when the first `vitest-environment-*` package actually lands.

- **pg_uuidv7 Docker rule `matchPackageNames` vs `matchDepNames` registry-prefix behaviour.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.github/renovate.json:95-96` (pg_uuidv7 rule). _Nature:_ Renovate's docker datasource may normalise the depName by stripping the registry prefix (`ghcr.io/`) — if so, the rule's `matchPackageNames: ["ghcr.io/fboulnois/pg_uuidv7"]` silently never matches because Renovate stores the depName as `fboulnois/pg_uuidv7`. The canonical docker-datasource filter in v37+ is `matchDepNames`. Zero live exposure today (devbox compose is Story 2.1 landing; Renovate App not yet installed against the repo). _Defer reason:_ empirically verifiable only at Story 2.1 + Renovate App install landing. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.1 devbox docker-compose first-run empirical validation — on first Renovate-proposed image bump, observe whether the pg-uuidv7 group materializes; if not, switch to `matchDepNames` or strip the `ghcr.io/` prefix.

- **No exhaustiveness guard against future I7 ecosystem additions silently defaulting to `replace`.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.github/renovate.json:9` (top-level `rangeStrategy: "replace"`) + all 4 packageRules. _Nature:_ top-level `replace` is intended catch-all for non-I7 packages per spec scope carve-out, but provides no guard against a future I7 ecosystem being missed. If Epic 5/13/14 introduces a fifth pinned-deps decision and a dev-story omits adding a new packageRule, the pinning gets silently skipped. Substrate cannot detect "I7 decision lacks matching packageRule" at pre-commit. _Defer reason:_ principled hardening beyond substrate scope. _Carry-to:_ Epic 3 reliability — declarative-policy-coverage check (e.g. keel-invariants extension that cross-references architecture.md § I7 decisions against `.github/renovate.json` packageRule groupName coverage) OR per-I7-decision lint at substrate-level.

- **`lockFileMaintenance` cannot retroactively pin a previously-range-specified package.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.github/renovate.json:42-46` (lockFileMaintenance block). _Nature:_ `lockFileMaintenance` re-resolves the lockfile within existing version-range constraints — it does NOT rewrite declared ranges to pins. A package previously specified as `^1.0.0` that acquires an I7 pin rule after-the-fact will not be collapsed to an exact version by lockFileMaintenance alone; only a regular Renovate dependency PR (triggered by the matching packageRule) will do that. `rangeStrategy` at top-level does not propagate into `lockFileMaintenance` semantics. _Defer reason:_ documentation clarity; substrate behaviour correct. _Carry-to:_ `docs/invariants/renovate.md` § Grouping rationale OR § I7 posture amendment — note that pin enforcement requires a regular Renovate dependency PR cycle, not lockFileMaintenance.

- **`config:recommended` → `config:best-practices` preset-merge automerge interaction (load-bearing assumption).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.github/renovate.json:3` (`extends`). _Nature:_ `config:recommended` transitively includes `config:best-practices` which may append an `automerge: true` packageRule for devDependencies (Renovate v37+). The per-rule `automerge: false` on the 4 I7 rules wins ONLY because Renovate's packageRule merge order places repo-authored rules AFTER preset rules (last-match-wins). This ordering is currently safe but is a load-bearing assumption about Renovate's internal preset-merge semantics — any future Renovate change to preset-merge ordering could invert the precedence and silently flip automerge on for I7 devDeps. _Defer reason:_ empirically verifiable only once App is installed + first preset-merge-order regression test runs against a Vitest/OTEL bump. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.1+ empirical validation once App is installed; OR Epic 3 reliability hardening (preset-merge-order regression test covering I7 devDep + top-level `automerge: false` + `config:best-practices` interaction).

- **Fork-extension doc claim misleading — `sync-gate re-pins` vs `sync-gate blocks`.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `docs/invariants/renovate.md:48`. _Nature:_ the § Fork extension section reads "the Story 1.9 sync-gate then re-pins the new file-byte state on the fork's landing", but the sync-gate is a VERIFIER (reports drift + exits non-zero at pre-merge), NOT a re-hasher. A fork that edits `.github/renovate.json` without also updating `INV-deps-version-pinning.contentHash` in `invariants.manifest.ts` will FAIL the sync-gate, not pass it. The required manual action (recompute sha256 + update manifest contentHash) is un-documented. Class-of-issue identical to Story 1.14 iter-80 defer #10 (`release.md` § Fork extension incomplete on regen-script gap) + Story 1.9 iter-7 defer "no regen script exists". _Defer reason:_ documentation gap; substrate behaviour correct; spec expansion. _Carry-to:_ renovate.md § Fork extension amendment — add regen command (e.g., `sha256sum .github/renovate.json | awk '{print $1}'` → update `invariants.manifest.ts:INV-deps-version-pinning.contentHash`) + unify the gap fix across release.md + tokens.md + renovate.md § Fork extension sections as a class-of-issue correction.

- **No `ignorePaths` / `enabledManagers` — Renovate scans all paths once App is installed.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.github/renovate.json` (config root; missing fields). _Nature:_ once the Renovate GitHub App installs against the repo, it scans all paths for every enabled manager (`config:recommended` enables `dockerfile`, `docker-compose`, `github-actions`, `npm`, `pnpm` — effectively all). Future devbox compose files under `packages/devbox/` + `.claude/` tooling + any Dockerfile in non-product paths will trigger unsolicited image-update PRs. Mitigated by `automerge: false` (manual close required), but creates dashboard noise. _Defer reason:_ empirically observable only once App is installed + Story 2.1 devbox compose lands; mitigation is a config amendment, not a substrate defect. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.1 devbox landing — add `ignorePaths: [".claude/**", "**/test/**", …]` OR scope `enabledManagers` to managers in active substrate use.

- **contentHash prettier-formatter version-drift sensitivity (class-of-issue — shared with all 21 prior substrate hash-pins).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts:213,221` (`INV-deps-version-pinning` + `INV-renovate-rationale` contentHash fields). _Nature:_ hashes computed over prettier-formatted file bytes including trailing newline + indent width. A future prettier version that changes JSON formatting rules (indent, trailing comma, key ordering) invalidates the pinned sha256 at the Story 1.9 sync-gate. Architectural class identical to Story 1.13 iter-71 + Story 1.14 iter-80 defer #9 content-hash provenance finding. No `.gitattributes` entry pins these 2 files to `text eol=lf`. _Defer reason:_ architectural class — unified fix spans all 22 invariant entries. _Carry-to:_ Epic 3 reliability — content-hash provenance hardening story (unified fix covering all 22 invariant entries; candidate resolutions: pin content-hash of normalised-source LF-canonical, switch to AST / canonical-JSON hash that survives format-only edits, or add `.gitattributes` `text eol=lf` + BOM stripping as a bridge tactic).

- **Spec Dev Notes citation drift — architecture.md:305 + architecture.md:649 stale.** _Source:_ Acceptance Auditor. _Location:_ `_bmad-output/implementation-artifacts/1-15-renovate-config-with-version-pinning-rules-i7.md:198-199` (Dev Notes § Story 1.15 architecture + PRD references). _Nature:_ line 198 cites "Architecture line 305 (§ Party-Mode-driven Implementation Invariants)" but live `architecture.md:305` content is `Client-runtime env vars (front-end build):` (VITE env-vars section); line 199 cites "Architecture line 649 (§ Repository layout / Dev-time tooling)" but live `architecture.md:649` content is `Boundaries: one React error boundary per top-level route…` (Process Patterns § Error handling). The verbatim I7 text actually lives at `architecture.md:342` (rationale doc correctly cites :342 at line 149); the Dev-time tooling enumeration of `.github/renovate.json` appears elsewhere near `architecture.md:810` (§ Source-tree). Pre-existing spec error inherited by dev-story; NOT a dev-story deviation. Class-of-issue identical to Story 1.14 iter-80 defer #6 (architecture.md:597 stale citation pattern). _Defer reason:_ editorial amendment across 2 sites in Story 1.15 spec; implementation-correct. _Carry-to:_ Story 1.15 spec Dev Notes amendment — either (a) relocate the Implementation Invariants index citation to architecture.md:342 + the Dev-time tooling enumeration to the correct § Source-tree line near :810, or (b) remove the exact line-number qualifier and point at section headers only (more resilient to architecture.md line-number drift).
