- **Template placeholder `_(add fork-specific invariants here)_` survives past fork-operator first edit.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter #11. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/templates/INVARIANTS.fork.md § Fork invariants index` line 278. _Nature:_ when fork operator `cp`'s template and adds first FORK-* entry, the italic placeholder is easy to leave behind, producing a permanently-empty "add here" note in committed fork file. No lint enforces removal. _Defer reason:_ standard scaffold-template convention. _Carry-to:_ template-polish candidate — add inline HTML comment `<!-- delete this line once you add entries -->` alongside placeholder.
- **`FORK-<fork-slug>-<category>-<slug>` category/slug parsing ambiguity.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter #12 + Edge Case Hunter #6 (merged). _Location:_ `docs/invariants/fork.md § INVARIANTS.fork.md scaffold` + `packages/keel-invariants/templates/INVARIANTS.fork.md § Extension`. _Nature:_ pattern `<fork-slug>-<category>-<slug>` implies 3 components, but example `FORK-acme-tenancy-region-lock` has 4 hyphen-separated segments after the FORK prefix, and the "≥ 2 hyphen-separated segments after `FORK-<slug>-`" rule allows multi-hyphen slugs — creating ambiguity between `category=tenancy, slug=region-lock` vs. `category=tenancy-region, slug=lock`. Future fork-specific tooling that parses category vs. slug has no machine-readable separator. Inherits upstream `INV-<category>-<slug>` pattern's identical ambiguity at `invariants.manifest.ts:4`. _Defer reason:_ substrate-wide convention — applies to both INV-* and FORK-* IDs. _Carry-to:_ Epic 3 reliability — INV-* / FORK-* naming convention tightening story (candidate: enforce exactly-2-hyphen pattern OR state "category is single-segment; remaining segments are slug").
- **Files section mixes hash-pinned + unpinned entries under one heading.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter #13. _Location:_ `docs/invariants/fork.md § Files`. _Nature:_ two bullets end "Knowledge-file pointer, not a hash-pinned invariant source" alongside two bullets linking to `INV-*` IDs. Naive reader may assume drift-detection covers AGENTS.md + CLAUDE.md too. _Defer reason:_ deliberate one-stop reference list with explicit per-bullet "hash-pinned" vs. "knowledge-file pointer" tags disambiguating status. _Carry-to:_ future prose-organization refactor — split into sub-lists "Hash-pinned substrate surfaces" vs. "Unpinned knowledge-file pointers".
- **`packages/create-keel-app/` shell exists today as Story 1.1 output; doc claims "future" / "when that package lands".** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter #1. _Location:_ `docs/invariants/fork.md:6/:43/:85`. _Nature:_ the `@keel/create-keel-app` package shell exists since Story 1.1 monorepo scaffold (`packages/create-keel-app/src/index.ts = export {};` + declared pnpm workspace with `@keel/keel-invariants` dep); doc language treats it as nonexistent. **INHERITED-SPEC-DRAFTING-DRIFT** class per Story 1.14 iter-80 defer #6 + Story 1.15 iter-87 defer (architecture.md:305 + :649 stale citations) + Story 1.16 iter-93 SM surface (inherited drafting-drift class carry-forward into iter-94 CR DEFER). AC 4 is satisfied semantically (CLI BEHAVIOUR non-auto-create: no `--include-fork-invariants` flag in the shell), not package-directory-existence. _Defer reason:_ inherited drafting-drift + Epic 15a scope — correction lands naturally when Epic 15a authors the CLI + flag + regression tests; rewording `fork.md` unilaterally now de-syncs the doc from the eventual Epic 15a PR. _Carry-to:_ Epic 15a landing — update `docs/invariants/fork.md:6/:43/:85` phrasing from "future package" / "when that package lands" / "the CLI itself is Epic 15a scope" to "the `--include-fork-invariants` CLI flag in the existing `@keel/create-keel-app` shell (runtime landing in Epic 15a)" as part of Epic 15a's doc updates.

- **Sync-gate ANCHOR_REGEX matches only `INV-` prefix; `FORK-` anchors silently skipped if landed in upstream INVARIANTS.md.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter #3. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/sync-gate.ts:24` (`const ANCHOR_REGEX = /^-\s+\*\*\`(INV-[a-z0-9]+(?:-[a-z0-9]+)+)\`\*\*/gm;`). _Nature:_ regex hard-codes INV- prefix. Fork operators who paste FORK-* entries into upstream INVARIANTS.md (instead of their own `INVARIANTS.fork.md`) see anchors silently skipped rather than producing a useful error. Story 1.16 documentation does not mention this asymmetry. _Defer reason:_ by-design at 1.0 — substrate sync-gate scoped to substrate IDs; FORK-* drift-detection is the fork's responsibility. _Carry-to:_ docs-hardening candidate — add one-liner to `docs/invariants/fork.md § Precedence` noting "the substrate sync-gate ANCHOR_REGEX matches only `INV-` anchors; FORK- anchors are the fork's responsibility to drift-detect via its own tooling." VERSIONS.md § Bake log iter-123 records `psql 16.13`. _Defer reason:_ intentional Ubuntu default per AC 3 scope-clarification Dev Note ("Epic 6 forward-compat via baked `psql` without explicit version lock so Ubuntu-managed upgrades track"). **Not a defect** — by-design minor-version drift matching Ubuntu apt-provided psql. If tightening becomes desirable, future Epic 6 Story 6.5 (`pnpm rls:explain` landing) can pin explicitly. _Carry-to:_ Epic 6 Story 6.5 if psql-specific behaviour regression observed.
- **Atomic README benchmark-log append.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter #6. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/benchmark.sh:129-140`. _Nature:_ current `{ echo ...; echo ...; } >> README` pattern writes multiple lines non-atomically; interrupt between lines produces malformed markdown. _Defer reason:_ low-probability fault (append is operator-triggered, not automated); acceptable Low severity. Fix is one-line (build entry in variable, single `printf` append). _Carry-to:_ next `benchmark.sh` iteration after AI-4 safety bundle lands.
- **`/workspace` read-only mount handling in `entrypoint.sh`.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter #16. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/entrypoint.sh` workspace chown block. _Nature:_ future Story 2.11 shared-workspace-mode mounts `:ro` for non-owner forks; chown fails with EROFS and current blanket `|| true` swallows silently. Future `dev:dev` user (Story 2.5) then can't write to `/workspace`. _Defer reason:_ **Story 2.11 (per-fork vs shared-devbox mode `KEEL_DEVBOX_SHARED`) scope** — the `:ro` mount branch only exists after Story 2.11 lands. Touching `entrypoint.sh` now would add dead code. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.11 entrypoint.sh modification pass.
- **`chown` Linux host-ownership clobber on bind-mount.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter #13. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/entrypoint.sh` workspace chown block. _Nature:_ on macOS + Docker Desktop, bind-mount ownership is virtualised (chown no-ops host); on Linux, bind-mount ownership IS the host's — `chown root:root /workspace` rewrites the operator's worktree to UID 0, requiring `sudo chown -R` recovery. _Defer reason:_ iteration reference env is macOS backend-B at 2026-04-21 (no clobber); Linux-operator edge case surfaces after Story 2.5 non-root-user landing changes the chown target. Documented divergence. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.5 `USER dev` landing — reassess chown logic with the non-root-user pattern.
- **`architecture.md` hardcoded line-number references in `benchmark.sh` + `README.md`.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter #29. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/benchmark.sh:7`, `packages/devbox/README.md:513`. _Nature:_ `architecture.md:264-270` line refs are fragile; any upstream edit shifts the NFR28b section. _Defer reason:_ minor doc-staleness risk; not adversarial Story 2.1 scope. Longer-term fix is anchor-based refs (§ NFR28b) + a sync-gate check. _Carry-to:_ future doc-polish pass OR Story 1.9 sync-gate extension (anchor-ref validation).
- **`uv` installer path assumption (`mv /root/.local/bin/uv`).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter #19. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/Dockerfile:306-309`. _Nature:_ Astral installer is not contract-stable on install-dir; if Astral changes to `~/.cargo/bin` or `/usr/local/bin` directly, the `mv` fails. _Defer reason:_ upstream Astral installer contract — no clean fix without Astral API guarantee or `find /root -name uv -executable` fallback. Not exploitable today (iter-123 bake landed uv 0.11.7 cleanly). _Carry-to:_ next Dockerfile iteration after AI-1..AI-9 land, OR Renovate-triggered uv upgrade if Astral changes install-dir.
- **`playwright@latest` vs explicit apt-list drift.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter #22. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/Dockerfile:375`. _Nature:_ `playwright @latest install-deps` can pull new apt packages silently; the explicit apt list in the earlier RUN layer doesn't reflect the new deps. Renovate doesn't track. _Defer reason:_ Renovate-tracked (Story 1.15) via VERSIONS.md; future Playwright major-version upgrade will surface the delta naturally. _Carry-to:_ next Renovate-triggered Playwright upgrade.
- **VERSIONS.md node minor-version drift across bakes.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter #25. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/VERSIONS.md § Bake log`. _Nature:_ iter-123 records Node 20.20.2; next bake will pull whatever NodeSource `setup_20.x` ships. VERSIONS.md stays at 20.20.2 unless manually refreshed. _Defer reason:_ known bake-log snapshot semantics — each iter-NN entry is provenance-dated to that bake. Auto-regeneration is Story 2.6's `pnpm devbox:*` lifecycle CLI scope, not Story 2.1. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.6 `pnpm devbox:rebuild` → VERSIONS.md bake-log-append side-effect.

## Deferred from: code review RE-RUN of story-2.1 (2026-04-21)

_Story 2.1 — iter-138 `/bmad-code-review (args: "2")` RE-RUN after iter-129..iter-137 drained AI-1..AI-9. Three-layer Ralph-hosted adversarial fan-out against `git diff main...HEAD` (2,504 lines / 20 files) post-fix. **Acceptance Auditor verdict**: 4 ACs re-verified SATISFIED ×2 + PARTIAL ×2 (AC 3 + AC 4 under pre-triaged WAIVED operator-owned carve-out from iter-126 — NOT new defects); scope-creep CLEAN; defer-list discipline CLEAN; all 9 AI-*s closure-evidence byte-matches the diff. **Blind Hunter** 16 findings; **Edge Case Hunter** 21 findings; deduplicated to 33 unique findings → 9 patch (bundled into 5 action items AR-1..AR-5 queued as TOP-of-QUEUE) + 18 defers below + 6 dismissed. Second CR gate for Story 2.1 (iter-128 → iter-138); infrastructure-smoke class precedent extension — first Epic 2 story requiring a second CR-re-run cycle, consistent with Story 1.9's iter-7 → iter-14 → iter-17 multi-cycle pattern._

- **NFR2 wall-clock sub-second measurement precision.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter (F2). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/benchmark.sh:~155-175` cold/warm `date +%s` subtraction. _Nature:_ `cold_seconds="$(( cold_end - cold_start ))"` uses integer epoch-second granularity; 1-second rounding ±error on every recorded NFR2 value. Header docstring advertises `time docker compose up --build -d` method; actual implementation rounds to seconds. _Defer reason:_ acceptable vs 30s warm / 300s cold budgets (rounding << budget). First-run variance floor is already ±20% M-series noise per arch.md NFR28b; sub-second precision is below the noise floor. _Carry-to:_ Epic 13 CI bench-timing harness where `process_time()`-style sub-millisecond measurement is the natural shape.

- **Invariant `description:` field duplicates ~900 words of `devbox-dind.md` — drift risk outside sync-gate.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter (F4). _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts:253` `INV-devbox-dind-available` entry. _Nature:_ the description string restates § Backend contract, § Safety rule, § NFR2 authority verbatim from the companion doc; FR43 sync-gate hashes `sourcePath` content only, not the description field; substantive edits to the doc that update `contentHash` will leave the manifest description silently stale. _Defer reason:_ by-design self-contained description for consumers that don't follow the `sourcePath` cross-reference; no active defect — description is accurate today. _Carry-to:_ Story 1.10+ invariant-schema hardening pass where `descriptionMaxLength` or `descriptionSyncedWith: sourcePath` schema rules could be added to the `InvariantSchema` Zod refine.

- **`detect_backend()` fast-path case-variant + containerd/podman fragility.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter (F6) + Edge Case Hunter #15 (F6 merged). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/benchmark.sh:~95-115` detect_backend case statement. _Nature:_ (a) `docker-desktop|*-docker-desktop|moby|linuxkit-*` case pattern is case-sensitive; enterprise Windows Docker Desktop installs occasionally report `Docker-Desktop` casing that falls through; Colima/Rancher wrappers use different prefixes; (b) non-Docker container runtimes (containerd/podman) without `/.dockerenv` file return A, misdetected as native host; would enable destructive prune against the wrong daemon. _Defer reason:_ fail-safe path already handles — `/.dockerenv` fallback catches true-container cases; case variants only affect the fast-path ergonomics (not safety). _Carry-to:_ Story 2.11 shared-mode (first-class multi-backend support) OR Epic 15a Growth-tier fork work (Windows/Colima variants need first-class support).

- **`npx --yes playwright@latest install-deps` unpinned — defeats Renovate pinning mechanism.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter (F7) + Edge Case Hunter #6 (merged). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/Dockerfile:~1742` playwright RUN layer. _Nature:_ `playwright@latest` resolves at build-time with no lockfile; `install-deps` silently `apt-get install`s libraries absent from the explicit apt list and from VERSIONS.md bake log; two bakes on different days yield different Playwright OS-dep snapshots. _Defer reason:_ already-listed in prior CR defer (iter-128 "playwright@latest apt-list drift"); Renovate tracks via VERSIONS.md iter-NN bake snapshots. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.6 `pnpm devbox:rebuild` auto-regen pattern that updates VERSIONS.md on every bake, making the snapshot drift observable in git diff.

- **`container_name` default collision when fork lacks `.envrc` override.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter (F9). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/docker-compose.yml:~38` (post-AI-2 `container_name: ${KEEL_DEVBOX_CONTAINER_NAME:-keel-devbox}`). _Nature:_ AI-2 provided the override mechanism but the default value is still the literal `keel-devbox`; a second worktree or a second fork on the same host that hasn't hand-written `KEEL_DEVBOX_CONTAINER_NAME=<unique>` in their `.envrc` still collides. Alternative defaults (e.g. `$(basename $PWD)` or `${COMPOSE_PROJECT_NAME}-devbox`) would prevent the collision without operator action. _Defer reason:_ AI-2 rationale-comment explicitly named log-greppability as the reason for keeping the literal default; collision in practice requires two worktrees on the same host, which is rare at M0.5 (single operator workstation). _Carry-to:_ Story 2.2 `.envrc.example` lands with per-worktree `KEEL_DEVBOX_CONTAINER_NAME` scaffolding that all worktrees inherit by default.

- **Dockerfile `wget` + `gnupg` + `lsb-release` installed without obvious consumer.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter (F10). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/Dockerfile:~62-72` apt install block. _Nature:_ the gh installation uses `curl | dd` (not gpg/apt-key); NodeSource `setup_20.x` ships its own keyring handling; no RUN invocation exercises `wget`, `gnupg`, or `lsb-release` visibly. Under the AI-9 "every upstream apt extra must justify itself" standard, these are undocumented carry-through. _Defer reason:_ removal requires transitive-dep analysis (NodeSource's `setup_20.x` might internally consume `gnupg` for apt-key fallback; `lsb-release` might be consumed by some Playwright dep); not a 1-line safe edit. _Carry-to:_ Story 11.x image-size optimization pass with empirical transitive-dep analysis (build image without each, observe what breaks).

- **Warm-run measurement contaminated by trailing cold `down` when both passes run.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter (F12). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/benchmark.sh:~175-195`. _Nature:_ cold branch ends with `docker compose down`; warm branch opens with another `docker compose down ... || true`; the two are not serialised against daemon convergence, so the recorded warm-start wall-clock may include residual teardown rather than the "down && up -d against pre-built image" defined in the header. _Defer reason:_ documented method; operator-owned authoritative timing on M4-Pro per AC 4. Pre-Epic-13, the ±20% first-run variance already swamps this contamination. _Carry-to:_ Epic 13 CI bench-timing harness where a clean sync-gate between cold and warm passes is natural.

- **NodeSource setup script piped to bash without checksum verification.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter #1 (E1). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/Dockerfile:~89-91` NodeSource `curl ... | bash -`. _Nature:_ compromised upstream or MITM at build-time executes arbitrary code in the image layer; no sha256 pinning. _Defer reason:_ upstream-canonical pattern (NodeSource itself documents this installation mode on [deb.nodesource.com](https://deb.nodesource.com)); supply-chain hardening is a cross-substrate concern. _Carry-to:_ Epic 4 Story 4.10 OWASP ASVS L1 baseline — already listed in prior CR defer as "`curl | sh` checksum-pinning for NodeSource / Astral / AWS / GitHub releases".

- **uv install script piped to sh without checksum verification.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter #2 (E2). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/Dockerfile:~131-134` uv Astral installer. _Nature:_ same supply-chain shape as NodeSource — `curl -LsSf https://astral.sh/uv/install.sh | sh`. No sha256. _Defer reason:_ upstream-canonical Astral installer pattern; shares defer carry-target with NodeSource. _Carry-to:_ Epic 4 Story 4.10.

- **GPG keyring empty via `curl | dd` pattern (no keyring integrity check).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter #3 (E3). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/Dockerfile:~117-124` gh keyring download. _Nature:_ `curl ... | dd of=...` pipeline lacks `set -o pipefail`; a curl failure producing empty body writes an empty keyring; subsequent apt repo fetches fail at repo-signature-verification time with an unclear error chain. _Defer reason:_ `curl -fsSL` handles HTTP errors with exit 22 (RUN exits non-zero); empty-body case is edge-case. Upstream gh install doc uses this pattern verbatim. _Carry-to:_ Epic 4 Story 4.10 OWASP ASVS L1 — concurrent absorb point for supply-chain hardening.

- **GitHub API anon rate-limit on Supabase release lookup.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter #4 (E4). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/Dockerfile:~164-181` supabase-cli release query. _Nature:_ same shape as the iter-128 CR defer for the same surface — anonymous 60/hr limit; back-to-back bakes or Epic 13 CI-parallel bakes can exceed. _Defer reason:_ already in prior CR defer list (iter-128). Not a new finding; confirmed by the re-run as still-deferred. _Carry-to:_ Epic 13 CI harness (`GITHUB_TOKEN` threading via `--build-arg`).

- **GitHub API anon rate-limit on git-delta release lookup.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter #5 (E5). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/Dockerfile:~183-201` git-delta release query. _Nature:_ same as supabase — anon rate limit. _Defer reason:_ already in prior CR defer list. _Carry-to:_ Epic 13 CI harness.

- **apt packages installed without version pins.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter #7 (E7). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/Dockerfile:~58-92` apt install block. _Nature:_ `apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends tini iproute2 dnsutils ...` with no `=VERSION` clause; Ubuntu pocket updates can change package versions between bakes. _Defer reason:_ intentional for Ubuntu security-update tracking; Renovate `apt` custom manager tracks via VERSIONS.md snapshots. Strict pinning is a larger supply-chain conversation. _Carry-to:_ Epic 11.x supply-chain hardening if strict pinning becomes required (tradeoff: pin-stability vs Ubuntu security-patch velocity).

- **`KEEL_DEVBOX_CONTAINER_NAME` override invalid-chars pre-flight validation.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter #9 (E9). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/docker-compose.yml:~27` (post-AI-2 parameterised container_name). _Nature:_ Docker's container-name restriction is `[a-zA-Z0-9_.-]`; an operator setting `KEEL_DEVBOX_CONTAINER_NAME="my devbox"` (space) or unicode would fail docker create with an opaque error. _Defer reason:_ Docker surfaces a clear error at create-time; pre-flight validation in start-script is Story 2.2 `pnpm devbox:up` wrapper concern. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.2 `scripts/devbox-start.sh` regex gate `[[ "$KEEL_DEVBOX_CONTAINER_NAME" =~ ^[A-Za-z0-9_.-]+$ ]] || exit 2`.

- **`KEEL_DEVBOX_WORKSPACE` path existence + host-shared-mount pre-flight.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter #10 (E10). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/docker-compose.yml:~63-66` bind-mount source path. _Nature:_ operator passing an invalid `KEEL_DEVBOX_WORKSPACE` to `docker compose up` produces "mounts denied" at container-create after the build cost has been paid. _Defer reason:_ partially-mitigated by iter-124 backend-B bind-mount-denial carve-out; pre-flight probe is queued as Story 2.1 follow-up IP Task 2 (already in prior CR defer as "Bind-mount pre-flight probe in `benchmark.sh`"). The docker-compose.yml surface itself cannot probe; responsibility belongs to start-script. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.2 `pnpm devbox:up` wrapper.

- **`/tmp` read-only under future hardening — `2>/tmp/chown.err` redirect fails.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter #12 (E12). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/entrypoint.sh:~57-60, :71-74` (AI-5 chown stderr-capture pattern). _Nature:_ Story 2.5 hardening will land `tmpfs` for `/tmp` with `nosuid,noexec` + size cap; if `/tmp` is read-only-by-accident or the tmpfs is full, the stderr redirect fails under `set -e` and the container startup aborts. _Defer reason:_ AR-2 (this re-run's patch) mitigates partially by replacing `/tmp/chown.err` with `mktemp -t chown.XXXXXX` + `chown_err=${chown_err:-/dev/null}` fallback. Full hardening against tmpfs-full landed tmpfs contract is Story 2.5 concern. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.5 hardening pass — verify entrypoint.sh chown-err capture still works under the new tmpfs tenure.

- **`mkdir -p` on read-only `/home` fails under `set -e`.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter #13 (E13). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/entrypoint.sh:~65-67` named-volume dir pre-creation loop. _Nature:_ Story 2.5 hardening will mount named-volumes at `/home/dev/.claude/` + `/home/dev/.config/gh/`; the loop in entrypoint.sh pre-creates those dirs — if the parent filesystem is readonly (future hardening), `mkdir -p` fails with EROFS and `set -e` aborts the container. _Defer reason:_ Story 2.5 contract concern; the named-volume mounts will satisfy the dir-existence precondition at compose runtime, making the pre-creation loop redundant. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.5 hardening pass — remove or refactor the mkdir loop once named-volumes land.

- **Flag `=value` form (`--skip-cold=1`) ergonomic gap.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter #18 (E18). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/benchmark.sh:~62-68` flag parser case statement. _Nature:_ Current parser accepts only `--skip-cold` (bare flag) and `--allow-broad-prune`; common-ergonomic `--skip-cold=1` or `--skip-cold=true` forms fall into the default unknown-arg exit 2. _Defer reason:_ Story 2.2 QoL pass will rewrite the flag parser with a uniform `case "$arg" in --skip-cold|--skip-cold=*) ...` pattern alongside the full `pnpm devbox:*` lifecycle CLI scope. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.2 lifecycle CLI.

## Deferred from: code review RE-RUN-2 of story-2.1 (2026-04-21)

_Story 2.1 — iter-144 `/bmad-code-review (args: "2")` RE-RUN-2 after iter-139..iter-143 drained AR-1..AR-5. Three-layer Ralph-hosted adversarial fan-out against `git diff main...HEAD` (2,704 lines / 20 files) post-AR-* fix-pass. **Acceptance Auditor verdict**: 4 ACs re-re-verified SATISFIED ×2 + PARTIAL ×2 (AC 3 + AC 4 under pre-waived operator-owned carve-out from iter-126); scope-creep CLEAN; defer-list discipline CLEAN; all 9 AI-*s + all 5 AR-*s closure-evidence byte-matches the diff (ZERO closure regressions); context-doc consistency CLEAN across devbox-dind.md / architecture.md / prd.md; sprint-status + trace-matrix CLEAN. **ZERO SUBSTANTIVE FINDINGS**. **Blind Hunter** 20 findings; **Edge Case Hunter** 16 findings; deduplicated to 33 unique findings → **0 patch** (the zero-patch verdict that closes the three-cycle CR sequence) + **7 defers below** + **26 dismissed** (noise / intentional / by-design / duplicates-of-existing-defers). Third CR gate for Story 2.1 (iter-128 + iter-138 + iter-144); matches Story 1.9's iter-7 → iter-14 → iter-17 multi-cycle envelope precedent. First zero-patch CR for Story 2.1 at its third gate; closes the `fixes-pending → done` transition and sets the three-cycle upper envelope as the Epic-2-infrastructure-smoke-story ceiling._

- **`KEEL_DEVBOX_WORKSPACE_OWNER` regex rejects numeric UID:GID (e.g. `1000:1000`).** _Source:_ Blind Hunter (F1) + Edge Case Hunter (E1; HIGH convergence, two independent subagents). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/entrypoint.sh:51` AR-2 regex anchor `^[A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_.+-]*:[A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_.+-]*$`. _Nature:_ Linux devcontainer-convention numeric-UID operator patterns (ubiquitous `KEEL_DEVBOX_WORKSPACE_OWNER=$(id -u):$(id -g)` shape for host-UID matching) rejected by the `[A-Za-z_]` first-char anchor; `chown` itself natively accepts numeric UID:GID. Story 2.1 default `root:root` passes regex (not blocking in default operation); iteration-context macOS Docker Desktop virtualises bind-mount ownership (numeric-UID unused today). _Defer reason:_ Story 2.5's non-root `dev` user redesign supersedes this surface — Story 2.5 bakes a fixed `dev:dev` user (UID 1000 baked-in), making the numeric-UID operator escape hatch superfluous. AI-5 (iter-133) + AR-2 (iter-140) intentionally scoped to POSIX username shape for option-parse-injection defence; widening now creates technical debt for Story 2.5's redesign. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.5 `USER dev` + non-root hardening pass — reassess chown regex shape (likely alternating `^([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_.+-]*|[0-9]+):([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_.+-]*|[0-9]+)$` if regex survives at all) in lock-step with the `dev:dev` default.

- **VERSIONS.md primary-table pin propagation asymmetry (AWS CLI + git-delta rows).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter (E11). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/VERSIONS.md:27,29` primary `## Baked at image-build` table. _Nature:_ AR-3 (iter-141) propagated iter-123 bake-log pins to the primary table for `uv` (0.11.7) and updated the Supabase row's Notes wording to match AI-6's fail-closed fix; AR-3 did NOT touch AWS CLI row (L27, still "v2 (arch-aware installer)") or git-delta row (L29, still "latest release `.deb` (arch-aware)") — both of which have captured pins in the `## Bake log § iter-123` table at L133-142 (AWS CLI 2.34.33; git-delta 0.19.2). Two-tier table-vs-bake-log asymmetry; Renovate `apt` custom manager scans the primary table first. _Defer reason:_ AR-3 scope was deliberately narrow (uv + supabase were the named-in-finding rows); completeness polish belongs to Story 2.6's `pnpm devbox:rebuild` lifecycle CLI which auto-regens VERSIONS.md on every bake, making pin propagation automatic rather than manual. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.6 `pnpm devbox:rebuild` → VERSIONS.md bake-log-append + primary-table sync side-effect.

- **`benchmark.sh` SIGPIPE uncovered in per-signal trap set.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter (E2). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/benchmark.sh:215-218` per-signal trap registration. _Nature:_ AR-1 (iter-139) bundled INT/TERM/HUP/QUIT per-signal traps; SIGPIPE (e.g. `benchmark.sh | head -1`) takes bash default behaviour (exit 141). The EXIT trap still fires — `cleanup_on_exit` runs `docker compose down` — so cleanup coverage is complete. However no per-signal `trap 'exit 141' PIPE` wrapper means exit-code semantics aren't script-controlled for the pipe-termination path; callers cannot distinguish "pipe consumer died" from "normal exit 141" (vanishingly rare for a shell script). _Defer reason:_ cleanup coverage is complete via the EXIT trap (AR-1's critical contribution); only exit-code DISTINGUISHABILITY is missing. Adding PIPE to the trap list would extend AR-1's comment block + add a thin wrapper, but the finding is Low-severity polish. _Carry-to:_ Epic 13 CI bench-timing harness where comprehensive signal-coverage (PIPE + USR1 + USR2 + ABRT) is natural alongside structured failure reporting.

- **`benchmark.sh` missing ERR diagnosis trap (no `file:line` of `set -e` failure).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter (E3). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/benchmark.sh:214` trap-registration block. _Nature:_ AR-1's EXIT-trap handoff for the ERR path provides cleanup coverage (verified iter-139 smoke: `false` under `set -e` → `cleanup fired; exit_code=1`) but no diagnostic — script never prints WHERE `set -e` tripped. An operator seeing `docker compose build` fail mid-pass gets the cleanup message with no indication of the failing command / line. _Defer reason:_ cleanup is correct (AR-1 target met); only DIAGNOSIS is missing. Adding `trap 'echo "ERR: ${BASH_SOURCE[0]}:${BASH_LINENO[0]}: failed command: ${BASH_COMMAND}" >&2' ERR` would extend AR-1 but introduces its own edge cases (ERR vs EXIT interaction; `$BASH_COMMAND` availability under `set -euo pipefail` pipefail paths; interaction with the `|| true` guards already in cleanup_on_exit). Low-severity polish; Epic 13 CI harness owns structured failure reporting. _Carry-to:_ Epic 13 CI bench-timing harness (JSON-lines format: `{"file": "...", "line": N, "signal": "ERR", "exit_code": N, "failed_command": "..."}`).

- **`detect_backend()` `/.dockerenv` heuristic misclassifies non-Docker OCI runtimes (podman / containerd+nerdctl / finch).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter (E6). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/benchmark.sh:148` `[[ -f /.dockerenv ]]` check. _Nature:_ Story 2.1 targets Docker/Compose per `INV-devbox-dind-available` § Backend contract. Non-Docker OCI runtimes use different container markers: podman → `/run/.containerenv`; containerd+nerdctl → no canonical marker; finch → uses its own daemon identifier. Script falls through `/.dockerenv` check to `echo A` → broad prune authorised against what may be a non-Docker daemon. _Defer reason:_ INV-devbox-dind-available § Backend contract currently enumerates Docker-specific backends A (true DinD) / B (host socket-passthrough); a podman-equivalent would require a backend C (isolated rootful/rootless podman daemon) with its own case-pattern discrimination + `/run/.containerenv` fallback. Multi-runtime support is Story 2.11 shared-mode (first-class multi-backend) or Epic 15a Growth-tier fork scope. Not a live defect in iteration context (backend-B macOS Docker Desktop) or operator M4-Pro baseline (native macOS Docker Desktop). _Carry-to:_ Story 2.11 shared-mode multi-backend support OR Epic 15a Growth-tier fork work (podman/finch-specific fork variants).

- **Ubuntu:24.04 base image not pinned by SHA digest (`FROM ubuntu:24.04@sha256:<digest>`).** _Source:_ Blind Hunter (F7). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/Dockerfile:17` `FROM ubuntu:24.04`. _Nature:_ Ubuntu's `24.04` tag is mutable on Docker Hub; Canonical pushes regular security-patch updates to the tag, so two bakes at different times ship different base layers. AI-1 through AI-9 (iter-128 gate) + AR-1 through AR-5 (iter-138 gate) hardened package-manager-level pins (claude-code, pnpm, uv, supabase-cli, git-delta); image-digest pinning is a further supply-chain layer not touched by those iterations. _Defer reason:_ extends the existing iter-128 defer "`curl | sh` checksum-pinning for NodeSource / Astral / AWS / GitHub releases" from package-fetch hardening to image-fetch hardening — same cross-substrate OWASP ASVS L1 concern, same scope carve-out (cross-Dockerfile supply-chain belongs to Epic 4). Renovate's `docker` custom manager tracks digest bumps when pinned. _Carry-to:_ Epic 4 Story 4.10 OWASP ASVS L1 baseline — bundle image-digest pin + Renovate `docker` manager alongside package-fetch hardening.

- **`detect_backend()` case-sensitive backend-name pattern matching (`Docker-Desktop` mixed-case, Colima / Rancher / Finch prefixes).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter (E13; extends iter-138 defer F6 "detect_backend fast-path case-variant fragility"). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/benchmark.sh:133-138` case-pattern statement (`docker-desktop|*-docker-desktop|moby|linuxkit-*`). _Nature:_ enterprise Windows Docker Desktop installs occasionally report `Docker-Desktop` (mixed-case casing); Colima (`colima-*`) wraps the daemon name without a canonical prefix recognised by this case list; Rancher Desktop and Finch use their own identifiers. For these variants the case-statement falls through, `/.dockerenv` fallback at L148 fail-safes to B. Safety is preserved — destructive prune is refused by default — but fast-path ergonomics degrade: operators running genuinely native backend-A Docker Desktop with a non-canonical casing / wrapper must pass `--allow-broad-prune` flag even though they are not in a nested container. _Defer reason:_ safety is preserved (fail-safe-B is the intentional posture from iter-131 AI-3); case-variant tolerance is operator-UX polish; same class as iter-138 defer F6 with Finch/Rancher extension. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.11 shared-mode multi-backend support (first-class Colima + Rancher + Finch treatment) OR Epic 15a Growth-tier fork work (enterprise Windows variants).

## Deferred from: code review of story-2-2-envrc-parameterisation-contract (2026-04-21)

_Story 2.2 (`.envrc` parameterisation contract) — iter-151 `/bmad-code-review (args: "2")` first CR gate against `git show ff8121a` (16 files / 429+/109−). Three-layer Ralph-hosted adversarial fan-out (Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter + Acceptance Auditor). **Auditor verdict: 1 finding** (invariant-doc negative-smoke example contradicts basename-anchored regex — classified PATCH, absorbed into § Review Findings as action item AR-1). **Blind Hunter** ≈19 findings; **Edge Case Hunter** 15 JSON findings; deduplicated to 20 unique → **2 patch** (both doc-accuracy drifts in `docs/invariants/gitignored-secret-commit-deny.md`) + **14 defers below** + **5 dismissed** (3-layer pnpm indirection = standard workspace pattern; shebang-less dist binary = npm-bin handles chmod; gitignore bang-negation ordering = verified correct; tmpfs knobs unconsumed = BY DESIGN per AC 1 scope-clarification forward-declaring Story 2.5 consumers; `.env` payload not in denylist = OUT OF AC 5 SCOPE which names only `.envrc`/`.envrc.local`/`.secrets`). First Epic-2 post-SM CR opener with only 2 patch findings — materially tighter than Story 2.1 iter-128's 9-AI opener, validating iter-150 v1.4 SM forecast (NO operator-owned carve-out + all 5 ACs live-verified at trace + SM time + 36-line Node-only leaf lint-rule = minimal adversarial attack surface)._

- **Unit-suffix injection in `mem_limit` / `shm_size` / `cpus` parameterisation.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter (F4/F13) + Edge Case Hunter (E1/E2/E3). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/docker-compose.yml:69-71` `${KEEL_DEVBOX_MEMORY_GB:-12}g` / `${KEEL_DEVBOX_SHM_GB:-2}g` / `'${KEEL_DEVBOX_CPUS:-8}'`. _Nature:_ operator setting `KEEL_DEVBOX_MEMORY_GB=16g` (mirroring the `mem_limit` idiom they see in compose docs) renders as `16gg`; `KEEL_DEVBOX_SHM_GB=512m` renders as `512mg`; `KEEL_DEVBOX_CPUS=0` / `-1` / `abc` / `8.5` flows through verbatim into YAML. `docker compose config` exits 0 for all these malformed substitutions because YAML-parse is lenient; only `docker compose up` (at daemon-attach time) rejects. _Defer reason:_ Story 2.2 AC 3 scope is retunability-at-YAML-substitution-time, not operator-input-validation. The `.envrc.example` header already documents "integer GB only, no suffix" style via the reference-default format + inline comments; defensive validation is Story 2.16 operator-UX / hooks scope OR a dedicated `pnpm devbox:env:check` preflight in Story 2.6's `pnpm devbox:*` lifecycle CLI. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.6 `pnpm devbox:env:check` or Story 2.16 pretooluse-hooks substrate — bundle with `KEEL_DEVBOX_NOFILE` overflow defer below under a shared "operator-env defensive validation" umbrella.

- **`KEEL_DEVBOX_NOFILE` overflow / suffix / zero / negative values pass YAML-parse gate.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter (F5 inline) + Edge Case Hunter (E4). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/docker-compose.yml:76-77` `ulimits.nofile.{soft,hard}: ${KEEL_DEVBOX_NOFILE:-65536}`. _Nature:_ operator setting `KEEL_DEVBOX_NOFILE=9999999999` (above kernel `fs.nr_open`) / `0` / `-1` / `65536k` flows through verbatim; `docker compose config` exits 0; container start fails with `invalid ulimit` or kernel EPERM / ERANGE. Separate sub-finding: `KEEL_DEVBOX_NOFILE` aliases both `soft:` and `hard:` — operator can never raise hard > soft without editing compose (semantic mismatch with `ulimit`'s separate-cap convention). _Defer reason:_ same defensive-validation class as `mem_limit` / `cpus` cluster above; soft/hard aliasing is BY DESIGN for Story 2.2 single-knob ergonomics (AC 1 naming convention mirrors the "knobs NOT underlying compose keys" scope clarification). _Carry-to:_ Story 2.6 `pnpm devbox:env:check` preflight OR Story 2.16 hooks defensive-validation substrate; split into `KEEL_DEVBOX_NOFILE_SOFT` + `KEEL_DEVBOX_NOFILE_HARD` only if Story 2.5 hardening's ulimit tuning needs the axis.

- **`KEEL_DEVBOX_CPUS` invalid-value pass-through (0 / −1 / fractional / non-numeric).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter (E3). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/docker-compose.yml:69` `cpus: '${KEEL_DEVBOX_CPUS:-8}'`. _Nature:_ listed as sub-finding but separate because the `cpus:` key is the most likely candidate for operator mis-use — docs often describe CPU caps as floats, and `0` has a genuine "no cap" interpretation in some tools (not compose). `docker compose config` passes all invalid values; daemon runtime rejects later. _Defer reason:_ same cluster; separate bullet recorded because the sub-mechanism differs (CPU scheduler has different edge values than memory). _Carry-to:_ Story 2.6 `pnpm devbox:env:check` preflight.

- **Whitespace-only env var expansion passes `${VAR:-default}` substitution gate.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter (E13). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/docker-compose.yml:70` (+ the whole `${KEEL_DEVBOX_*:-<default>}` cluster). _Nature:_ compose `${VAR:-default}` substitutes the default on unset/empty, NOT on whitespace-only. `export KEEL_DEVBOX_MEMORY_GB="  "` renders as `mem_limit: "  "g` — parse error. _Defer reason:_ operator-input-validation class; `.envrc.example` format mitigates by providing clean reference values, but a fork retune during editing can introduce whitespace trivially. _Carry-to:_ same cluster as the unit-suffix defer above — a `pnpm devbox:env:check` trim-and-validate pass handles this alongside unit-suffix validation.

- **Platform/arch mismatch cryptic failure on amd64 host without `KEEL_DEVBOX_ARCH` override.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter (F15) + Edge Case Hunter (E5). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/docker-compose.yml:34` `platform: ${KEEL_DEVBOX_ARCH:-linux/arm64}`. _Nature:_ amd64 operator who clones the repo and runs `docker compose up` without reading `.envrc.example` gets an arm64 image on amd64 — requires QEMU; if QEMU absent, failure is cryptic (`exec format error`). The `.envrc.example` header documents override, but operator-workstation-first-run may bypass the direnv copy-seed flow. _Defer reason:_ operator-env polish; `.envrc.example` comment already documents the knob; Story 2.6 `pnpm devbox:up` wrapper can shell out to `uname -m` and warn on mismatch. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.6 `pnpm devbox:up` preflight warning OR Story 2.11 shared-mode architecture-autodetection.

- **Loopback-only port publication (`127.0.0.1:…`) unreachable from remote-DinD / `DOCKER_HOST=tcp://…` operators.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter (F12). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/docker-compose.yml:78-82` four hardcoded `- '127.0.0.1:${KEEL_DEVBOX_PORT_*:-<default>}:<default>'` entries. _Nature:_ iter-146 pre-dev SM review fix (6) explicitly mandated `127.0.0.1:` prefix on port entries to reduce Story 2.12 rework surface. For operators driving a remote Docker daemon (remote DinD, `DOCKER_HOST=tcp://…`, corporate shared-runner setups), the bind IP `127.0.0.1` is the REMOTE host's loopback — unreachable from local workstation. No knob to override the bind IP. _Defer reason:_ Story 2.12 (loopback-bound port publication opt-in + `KEEL_DEVBOX_SSH` + `sshd`) explicitly owns this cross-cutting port-publication surface per epic plan; Story 2.2's role was to forward-declare the port knobs, not to parameterise the bind IP. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.12 `KEEL_DEVBOX_BIND_IP` knob alongside the SSH opt-in toggle — canonical remote-operator story for the loopback-bound-port-publication surface.

- **Port-knob collision (e.g. `KEEL_DEVBOX_PORT_WEB=3001` matches API default) has no cross-knob validation.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter (E6). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/docker-compose.yml:78-82` four parameterised port entries. _Nature:_ operator retuning `KEEL_DEVBOX_PORT_WEB=3001` without adjusting `KEEL_DEVBOX_PORT_API` (default 3001) collides on the same host port — `docker compose up` fails with `bind: address already in use`. Same class for any two of the four ports. No cross-knob validation in compose; no warning in `.envrc.example` to keep ports distinct. _Defer reason:_ operator-UX polish; README § Retuning could document "ports must be pairwise distinct" as a note — Story 2.6 `pnpm devbox:env:check` preflight validates. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.6 preflight; alongside the defensive-validation cluster above.

- **Denylist regex case-sensitivity + Windows backslash + filesystem-root-path (`/.envrc`) edge cases.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter (F1) + Edge Case Hunter (E7/E8/E9). _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/check-no-committed-dotfiles.ts:17-19` three denylist entries `/^(.+\/)?\.envrc$/` / `\.envrc\.local$/` / `\.secrets$/`. _Nature:_ three sub-edges: (a) regex is case-sensitive — `.ENVRC` on macOS APFS (case-insensitive default) aliases to `.envrc` on the filesystem but git tracks the staged name as given; `git add .ENVRC` slips past the denylist. (b) regex anchors on forward-slash separator — Windows checkout emitting `packages\devbox\.envrc` is not matched; hook is effectively disabled on Windows. (c) `(.+\/)?` prefix requires 1+ chars before `/` — `/.envrc` (filesystem-root basename) fails to match; prek passes repo-relative paths so this is a direct-CLI edge only. _Defer reason:_ cross-platform hardening is out of Story 2.2 scope (Linux-substrate repo; cc-devbox runs Linux containers; macOS operators run Docker Desktop Linux VM). AC 5 scope is gitignored-secret commit-deny at the default prek-invoked path. Case-insensitivity is a BYPASS; Windows operator support belongs to Epic 15a Growth-tier fork work; filesystem-root is a narrow direct-CLI smoke scenario. _Carry-to:_ Epic 15a Growth-tier fork variants (Windows / enterprise); Vitest regex-fixture table-test lands the test coverage at Epic 13 test-framework landing.

- **Hook zero-argv silent-pass (`pass_filenames: true` invoked with empty argv → exit 0 without warning).** _Source:_ Blind Hunter (F10) + Edge Case Hunter (E10). _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/check-no-committed-dotfiles.ts:22-28` `const stagedFiles = process.argv.slice(2); const violations = stagedFiles.flatMap(...)`. _Nature:_ zero-argv runs exit 0 silently. If `.pre-commit-config.yaml` `files:` regex is ever mis-edited so the hook is invoked with empty filename list, the hook silently "passes" — no "hook received no filenames, aborting" safety net. sync-gate via contentHash catches the `.pre-commit-config.yaml` change but not the semantic regression of the guard becoming a no-op. _Defer reason:_ not exploitable today (sync-gate watches the config file; human review of YAML + sync-gate suffice at 1.0); defense-in-depth hardening class. _Carry-to:_ Epic 13 CI test-harness — a test that runs the hook with empty argv AND with empty-string filename AND with a filename that doesn't exist, asserting expected failure modes. Or a one-line `if (stagedFiles.length === 0) process.exit(0);` with a debug-log warning behind `DEBUG=keel-invariants` env.

- **Missing automated regex test for `check-no-committed-dotfiles.ts`.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter (E15). _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/check-no-committed-dotfiles.ts` (no test file exists). _Nature:_ ATDD-WAIVED at iter-147 (twelfth cumulative precedent — FR14n ATDD-skip + hybrid ground-(a)-(b)-(c)-(d)). The regex is a core security guard; a regression (accidentally dropping the `$` anchor, flipping to case-insensitive too broadly, widening the prefix group) ships green through `pnpm -w typecheck/lint/format:check` and through `docker compose config`. _Defer reason:_ ATDD was formally WAIVED with a precedent chain — deferring test coverage to post-Epic-13 test-framework landing is the stated posture for this class of story. _Carry-to:_ Epic 13 Vitest harness — `check-no-committed-dotfiles.test.ts` with stringified-argv table test covering positive / negative / boundary / case-variant / whitespace / filesystem-root / Windows-path fixtures. Retroactively raises the regression-catch floor.

- **Two manifest entries share `sourcePath: .pre-commit-config.yaml` → latent contentHash drift-trap.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter (F6). _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts:93,109` `INV-prek-pre-commit-config` + `INV-prek-commit-msg-config` both point at `.pre-commit-config.yaml`. _Nature:_ any single-line edit to `.pre-commit-config.yaml` requires simultaneously updating two independent `contentHash` values; if a future contributor updates only one, sync-gate catches drift on only that entry. _Defer reason:_ pre-existing Epic 1 pattern (shares root with the same concern recorded at Story 1.8 iter-7 CR defer "Shared-sourcePath cross-entry `contentHash` consistency refine" — which expected Story 1.9's drift-detection to catch this via whole-file sha256 recomputation at manifest-use time). Story 2.2 inherits the pattern when it adds `INV-gitignored-secret-commit-deny` adjacent to the pre-existing prek entries. _Carry-to:_ Epic 13 test-harness OR a one-shot refactor story that replaces the per-entry `contentHash` with a per-`sourcePath` computed hash at walker time — aligns with Story 1.9's sync-gate semantics and eliminates the manual two-hash update surface.

- **compose v2 non-swarm service-level `mem_limit` / `cpus` / `shm_size` deprecation future-compat.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter (E14). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/docker-compose.yml:69-71`. _Nature:_ upstream Docker Compose v2.x is gradually deprecating top-level service-level `mem_limit` / `cpus` / `shm_size` in favour of `deploy.resources.limits.*` (which itself has non-swarm semantics in v2.20+). Story 2.2's AC 2 scope-clarification EXPLICITLY locks non-swarm service-level form per iter-146 fix (3) — `NOT deploy.resources.limits.*`. This is a correctness decision for the current compose version; future versions may emit deprecation warnings or remove the keys. _Defer reason:_ AC 2 scope-clarification locks the current form; a future compose-version migration is a spec-level change, not a CR patch. _Carry-to:_ Renovate-triggered or periodic "devbox compose version sweep" story when upstream compose deprecation-warning level fires; at that point the full compose file migrates + AC 2 scope clarification is superseded. Epic 13+ release-gated tier is the natural CI-surface to detect deprecation warnings at release time.

- **Manifest-entry description drift re `.env*` coverage breadth.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter (F14). _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts` (new `INV-gitignored-secret-commit-deny` entry, description field). _Nature:_ description says "refuses additions of .envrc, .envrc.local, and .secrets at any path" — accurate for the invariant's scope. But `.gitignore` broader `.env*` coverage is a SEPARATE mechanism, not governed by this invariant. Risk: future reader interprets invariant as covering broader `.env*` scope (e.g. `.env`, `.env.production`). _Defer reason:_ invariant is correctly scoped in its description; the interpretation risk is doc-polish level. Adding a one-line note "(does not cover `.env` / `.env.production` — those are `.gitignore`-only; see Story 2.16 hooks for filesystem-level secret denylist)" would close the drift. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.16 Claude-pretooluse-hooks substrate — when hooks-level secret-denylist lands, cross-reference both mechanisms in a shared invariant-doc index.

- **Pointer-error stderr may reference the refused file itself (self-cross-reference).** _Source:_ Blind Hunter (F11). _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/check-no-committed-dotfiles.ts:32-34` stderr message references `packages/devbox/.envrc.example` + `packages/devbox/.secrets.example` as schema sources. _Nature:_ if the refused path is itself under `packages/devbox/` OR if `.envrc.example` has been deleted from the working tree, the pointer is hollow. Narrow edge — a developer who deleted `.envrc.example` mid-work and tried to commit `.envrc` would get a pointer to the (now-missing) schema file. _Defer reason:_ minor edge; `.envrc.example` is part of the committed schema and wouldn't be deleted in normal workflow; the pointer-error still conveys the essential "refused to commit" message even if the referenced file is momentarily absent. _Carry-to:_ optional polish — add an existence check + fall back to "(see Story 2.2 AC 5 for schema layout)" if file missing; low priority.

- **`.envrc.example.bak` / `.envrc.local.example` / nested-companion variants remain ignored under `.env*` with no dedicated negation.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter (E11). _Location:_ `.gitignore:35-44` rule block. _Nature:_ `.env*` catches backup files (e.g., editor-created `.envrc.example.bak`) and nested copies (e.g., `packages/devbox/sub/.envrc.example`); explicit bang-negations only cover the exact literal names. Operator creating backup files during editing sees `git add` silently no-op. _Defer reason:_ edge operator workflow; conservative scope keeps Story 2.2 at AC-declared companions only (`.envrc.example` + `.secrets.example` at repo root + `packages/devbox/`). Expanding negation rules would admit untested file-name variants. _Carry-to:_ documentation polish — README § Retuning adds a note "don't create `.envrc*.bak` backup files; git silently ignores them"; no code change required.

## Deferred from: code review of 2-3-egress-policy-dnsmasq-nftables-fail-closed-ipv4-ipv6-parity-atomic-reload (2026-04-21)

_Story 2.3 (egress policy: dnsmasq + nftables, fail-closed, IPv4/IPv6 parity, atomic reload) — iter-161 `/bmad-code-review (args: "2")`. Three-layer Ralph-hosted adversarial fan-out (Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter + Acceptance Auditor per skill `step-02-review.md`) against cumulative Story 2.3 substrate diff `69e3103..HEAD` (19 files / 1031+/8−; ~650 LOC implementation + invariants manifest + invariant doc + README updates). **Acceptance Auditor verdict: HIGH-confidence PASS** (5/5 AC SATISFIED + 17/17 SC SATISFIED with file:line substrate evidence, pressure-tested iter-160 SM ZERO-PATCH verdict — upheld). **Blind Hunter: 18 findings** (2 CRITICAL + 5 HIGH + 6 MEDIUM + 5 LOW). **Edge Case Hunter: 15 findings** (1 CRITICAL + 3 HIGH + 6 MEDIUM + 5 LOW). Triaged ~50 raw → **9 PATCH + 9 DEFER + ~9 DISMISS** after live-substrate verification against bash 5.x + nft 1.0.9 + Docker bind-mount behaviour + entrypoint.sh L23 `set -euo pipefail` exit propagation._

_The 9 defers below are all out-of-scope for Story 2.3's substrate-commitment scope: observability-supervision (not enforcement) / architectural trade-offs acknowledged in architecture § S5 / Epic-4 consumer concerns / future-compat / doc-hash-only invariant manifest by design. None are exploitable against Story 2.3's fail-closed AC commitments; they are hardening + observability candidates natural-scope for downstream stories or deferred to operator-workstation bake-time._

- **Rotation synchronously blocks tail pipe during `gzip`.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter HIGH. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/egress-log-tailer.sh:42-78`. _Nature:_ `rotate_if_needed` is called synchronously inside the per-line loop; while `gzip` runs (potentially seconds on 50 MB) the tail pipe buffer fills and dnsmasq log lines may be dropped upstream. _Defer reason:_ 50 MB gzip is typically sub-second on modern CPUs; the SC-4 rotation cadence is operator-workstation-tuned (pinned at 50 MB to cap worst-case disk at ~125 MB per invariant doc L73). Optimisation candidate. _Carry-to:_ operator-workstation bake-time perf verification alongside Task 12.7 log-rotation smoke (iter-158 DEFER-annotation) — if rotation latency impacts observability on baseline NFR2 operator-workstation, fork `gzip` into background with `exec 3>&-; (gzip -f …; mv …) &` and reopen fd 3 against a freshly `touch`-ed file before the background gzip completes.
- **egress-log-tailer.sh has no supervisor — silent death cuts observability.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter MEDIUM + Edge Case Hunter HIGH (cross-layer convergent). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/egress-log-tailer.sh:198-200` + `packages/devbox/scripts/start-egress.sh:100`. _Nature:_ if `tail -F` dies (OOM, fs error, SIGPIPE, rotation-time `gzip` failure under `set -e`) the `while read` loop exits and the tailer script ends; no respawn, pidfile stays pointing at a dead pid, `/workspace/logs/egress-queries.jsonl` stops advancing, nftables + dnsmasq continue enforcing fail-closed policy (egress still works) but FR37 security-evidence stream is silently cut. Epic 4 consumer cannot distinguish "no queries happened" from "tailer dead". _Defer reason:_ observability concern not enforcement guarantee; supervisor/respawn pattern belongs to a dedicated observability-hardening story OR Story 2.13 healthcheck (probe tailer liveness via `kill -0 "$(cat /run/keel-egress-tailer.pid)"` and surface non-zero healthcheck on tailer death). _Carry-to:_ **Story 2.13 healthcheck OR Epic 4 FR37 security-evidence consumer** (whichever lands first should author the liveness probe + respawn pattern).
- **Tailer rotation SIGTERM mid-rotation may leave JSONL file transiently missing.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter MEDIUM. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/egress-log-tailer.sh:71-77`. _Nature:_ the rotation sequence `exec 3>&-; mv to .1.tmp; gzip; touch new; reopen fd` is not atomic against SIGTERM; the `shutdown` trap fires `exec 3>&-` (already closed) and exits 0 — in the window between the first `mv` and the final `touch`, the active `/workspace/logs/egress-queries.jsonl` may not exist. External consumers opening the file during this window get ENOENT; `monitor.sh`'s `tail -F` reattaches on file creation but naive consumers may fail-loudly. _Defer reason:_ low-likelihood race with a documented consumer contract (tail-F recovery is the standard pattern); disabling signal handling during rotation (`trap '' TERM INT` around the block) is a one-line fix but layers trap-state complexity. _Carry-to:_ **Story 2.13 healthcheck hardening** if healthcheck-consumer open-on-path fails during rotation; otherwise hold for an observability-hardening pass.
- **SERVFAIL / upstream-timeout not emitted in JSONL.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter MEDIUM. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/egress-log-tailer.sh:130-180`. _Nature:_ `KEEL_DEVBOX_DNS_UPSTREAM=1.1.1.1` becomes unreachable (partition, rate limit, CF outage) → dnsmasq's forwards time out → returns SERVFAIL; the tailer regex catalog (`query`, `forwarded`, `reply`, `config`) has no pattern for dnsmasq SERVFAIL / REFUSED / upstream-timeout log lines; SC-3 schema advertises `result: "servfail"` but no code path emits it. Fail-closed posture is preserved (clients see resolution failure) but the observability contract is incomplete. _Defer reason:_ Epic 4 FR37 security-evidence consumer may refine the result-classifier; SC-3's declared 5-value result enum (`allow|block|nxdomain|servfail|parse-error`) holds at the schema level; the regex gap is a code-vs-schema drift, not an AC violation. _Carry-to:_ **Epic 4 FR37 security-evidence consumer story** — when Epic 4 authors the JSONL consumer, it will need a dnsmasq SERVFAIL fixture line + a tailer regex branch matching dnsmasq's `reply <domain> is <SERVFAIL|REFUSED>` / `failed to send packet` upstream-failure log lines, emitting `result: "servfail"`.
- **Whitelist-snapshot DNS-rotation drift.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter HIGH. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/reload-egress.sh:100-117`. _Nature:_ nftables allow-list snapshots literal IPs resolved at reload time; domains that rotate A records (cloud CDNs, `api.anthropic.com`, `raw.githubusercontent.com`, `ghcr.io`, `*.npmjs.org`) return new IPs that aren't in the nftables allow-list → TCP SYN gets dropped silently even though dnsmasq correctly resolves (JSONL logs `allow`, layer-3 drops). _Defer reason:_ architectural trade-off ACCEPTED per architecture § S5 dual-layer belt-and-braces; Story 2.4's `whitelist.sh sync` CLI is the mitigation path (frequent reload via operator trigger or Story 2.13 healthcheck-driven reload). An IP-set driven from dnsmasq's `--dnsmasq-script` hook would be strictly better but adds substrate complexity out of scope for 1.0. _Carry-to:_ **Story 2.4 `whitelist.sh sync`** is the sanctioned mitigation; a post-1.0 hardening story may introduce dnsmasq-hook-driven IP-set updates if CDN rotation frequency empirically breaks fork-operator workflows.
- **dnsmasq `bind-interfaces` + `::1` racing container boot.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter MEDIUM. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/dnsmasq/dnsmasq.conf:28`. _Nature:_ `bind-interfaces` asks dnsmasq to bind each matching interface address (not `0.0.0.0`); if `lo` is not yet configured with `::1` when dnsmasq starts (uncommon on backend B where `lo` is typically up-and-dual-stack at boot, but possible on fork-operator workstations with aggressive namespace setup), the `::1` bind fails and dnsmasq exits non-zero → start-egress exits under `set -e` → container dies at boot. _Defer reason:_ low-likelihood on backend B per SM iter-160's operator-workstation-defer-acknowledgment; dnsmasq has no native retry. _Carry-to:_ operator-workstation bake-time verification as part of Task 12.1 smokes; if observed in practice, drop `::1` from `listen-address` or add a retry wrapper around dnsmasq's first-start in `reload-egress.sh`.
- **`INV-devbox-egress-contract` is doc-hash-only — no runtime enforcement.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter LOW. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts:257-263` + `docs/invariants/devbox-egress.md` frontmatter. _Nature:_ the invariant claim is "fail-closed DNS + IPv4/IPv6 parity + atomic reload" but the manifest-side enforcement is only content-hash sync gating between the doc and the `INVARIANTS.md` anchor. There is NO machine-enforced runtime check (live `nft list chain`, JSONL schema `jq` probe, or `kill -HUP` round-trip) — the doc itself explicitly defers these to "a dedicated packages/keel-invariants/ rule + unit test on a later Ralph iteration". _Defer reason:_ acknowledged-in-band; the doc frontmatter declares enforcement as doc-hash only pending future runtime probe. _Carry-to:_ **Epic 13 CI harness OR a dedicated `packages/keel-invariants/` runtime-rule story post-Epic-13** — land the runtime probe so the invariant claim is actually enforced; explicitly mark the manifest entry's enforcement class if the schema adds such a field.
- **In-flight conntrack priming before first `nft -f`.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter LOW. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/nftables/egress.nft:46,70`. _Nature:_ the atomic-reload guarantee relies on `ct state established,related accept` preserving in-flight flows across reload; on the first reload at container start, there are no connections (moot); but any future init-script adding a pre-policy outbound flow (e.g., a probe) would leave that flow with no conntrack state when the first `nft -f` applies rules that require `ct state established,related accept`. If `nf_conntrack` module isn't loaded for the netns before the first apply (unusual but possible on restricted kernels), established flows get dropped. _Defer reason:_ moot on first boot per current `entrypoint.sh` sequence (no outbound flows before start-egress); fragile if a future init-script changes. _Carry-to:_ operator-workstation bake-time verification via `modprobe nf_conntrack` pre-flight in start-egress, OR document in AGENTS.md/Story-2.13 that nothing may open an outbound connection before start-egress completes.
- **monitor.sh `jq` pipeline fragile against malformed lines.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter LOW. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/monitor.sh:21`. _Nature:_ `tail -Fn0 … | jq -c --unbuffered '.'` under `set -euo pipefail` exits non-zero if any JSONL line is malformed (partial write during rotation, parse-error payload with incomplete `tr -d` cleanup); operator tool with a re-run recovery path, not production path. _Defer reason:_ operator-facing; re-run is the recovery; low impact. _Carry-to:_ operator-UX polish (hardening pass) — pipe through `jq -c --unbuffered -R 'fromjson? // .'` so malformed lines pass through as raw strings rather than crashing jq.

## Deferred from: code review of 2-3-egress-policy-dnsmasq-nftables-fail-closed-ipv4-ipv6-parity-atomic-reload.md (2026-04-21 re-run)

_Iter-171 `/bmad-code-review (args: "2")` closure gate after the 9-PATCH drain (AR-1..AR-9 landed iter-162..iter-170). Three-layer Ralph-hosted adversarial fan-out against drain-only diff (bfcd500..HEAD scoped to packages/devbox/, docs/invariants/, packages/keel-invariants/) produced 0 PATCH + 0 DECISION_NEEDED + 8 DEFER + ~36 DISMISS. These 8 deferred items are all defensive-hardening / spec-amendment / diagnostic-precision candidates out-of-scope for a code-review fix-drain. None block the iter-171 `fixes-pending → done` transition; all are sanctioned carry-overs to downstream stories or future `/bmad-edit-prd` / observability-hardening passes._

- **D1 — SC-13 spec-text amendment to carve out AR-1 bootstrap-detour.** _Source:_ Acceptance Auditor iter-171. _Location:_ `_bmad-output/implementation-artifacts/2-3-egress-policy-dnsmasq-nftables-fail-closed-ipv4-ipv6-parity-atomic-reload.md` §Scope clarifications SC-13 (lines 65–66) + `packages/devbox/scripts/reload-egress.sh:156-161`. _Nature:_ SC-13's literal prose "DO NOT write `8.8.8.8`, `1.1.1.1`, or any upstream to `resolv.conf`" was not amended when iter-161 CR elected AR-1's bootstrap-detour; AR-1 temporarily writes `${UPSTREAM_RESOLVER}` (default `1.1.1.1`) to `/etc/resolv.conf` during first-boot resolution before `restore_resolv_pin()` re-pins to `127.0.0.1` on every exit path. SC-13 steady-state contract (`nameserver 127.0.0.1` at steady state) holds on every exit via the EXIT trap; only the first-boot resolution window (getent calls) temporarily repoints. _Defer reason:_ material SC-text amendments are out-of-scope for a code-review fix-drain; the iter-161 CR process implicitly elected AR-1 as the narrowest-scope fix and drained it `[x]` without spec amendment. _Carry-to:_ **`/bmad-edit-prd` pass or dedicated spec-amendment story** — amend SC-13 to add a carve-out for the first-boot bootstrap window with explicit pre/post-condition language matching the `restore_resolv_pin()` contract in code.
- **D2 — Domain regex validation at reload time.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-171. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/reload-egress.sh:181-200,263-288`. _Nature:_ `reload-egress.sh` interpolates each whitelist domain into `server=/<domain>/<upstream>` dnsmasq directives and `ip daddr <ip> accept` nftables rules without `[[ =~ ^[A-Za-z0-9.-]+$ ]]` sanitisation; a malformed whitelist entry (accidental `/`, shell metacharacter, zero-width unicode, percent-encoded) would produce a malformed dnsmasq directive → SIGHUP fails → dnsmasq reload stalls → fail-open gap. _Defer reason:_ whitelist source is developer-controlled + source-versioned at Story 2.3 (baseline `whitelist.default.txt` + `whitelist/*.txt` fragments under repo control); threat model does not include malicious whitelist content. _Carry-to:_ **Story 2.4 `whitelist.sh sync` CLI** is the first operator-editable entry point — domain regex validation should land there so malformed input never reaches `reload-egress.sh`.
- **D3 — SIGTERM-during-flock-trap gap.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-171. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/reload-egress.sh:105-132`. _Nature:_ ~24-line window between `exec 200>"${LOCK_FILE}"` + `flock -x -w 10 200` and `trap cleanup EXIT` registration leaves a tiny race where SIGTERM could leak fd 200 without invoking `cleanup()`. Impact is recoverable (kernel auto-releases fd 200 on process exit; next reload re-acquires flock cleanly). _Defer reason:_ low-likelihood (container receives SIGTERM at shutdown not mid-reload); fd 200 leak is recovered on the next reload; no persistent corruption. _Carry-to:_ observability-hardening pass OR register `trap cleanup EXIT` immediately after `set -euo pipefail` with a no-op cleanup body that's populated later; inverts the current scope-before-trap ordering.
- **D4 — Tailer liveness check post-`nohup` launch.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-171. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/start-egress.sh:125-128`. _Nature:_ `start-egress.sh` records `$!` to `TAILER_PID_FILE` but does not verify the tailer is still alive after a short settle; a tailer that exits immediately (script syntax error, missing `/var/log/dnsmasq.log`, binary incompat) leaves JSONL emitter silently dormant. FR37 security-evidence stream is silently cut; fail-closed enforcement is preserved by nftables + dnsmasq independently. _Defer reason:_ observability concern not enforcement; mirrors the already-deferred "egress-log-tailer.sh has no supervisor" item at iter-161 but at a different layer (launch vs steady-state). _Carry-to:_ **Story 2.13 healthcheck OR Epic 4 FR37 consumer** — same supervisor pattern as the iter-161 deferred observability gap.
- **D5 — getent NODATA not explicitly distinguished from resolution failure.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-171. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/reload-egress.sh:182-199`. _Nature:_ when upstream returns NOERROR NODATA (domain valid, no A record), `getent ahostsv4` exits 0 with empty stdout; current code emits no rule and no WARN, making NODATA indistinguishable from the populated-stdout happy path in logs. Fail-closed default still handles the no-rule case correctly (client sees DNS-level NODATA before hitting layer-3). _Defer reason:_ diagnostic precision improvement; not an AC violation. _Carry-to:_ observability-hardening pass — add an `[[ -z "${ipv4_raw// }" ]] && log "WARN: ipv4 NODATA for ${domain}"` branch inside the `if getent` success path.
- **D6 — `mv /etc/dnsmasq.conf` cross-filesystem failure not explicitly mapped to exit 7.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-171. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/reload-egress.sh:285-295`. _Nature:_ `mv "${dnsmasq_rendered}" "${DNSMASQ_CONF}"` after a successful `nft -f` apply could fail on a cross-filesystem rename if `/etc` and `TMPDIR` are on different overlay mounts; under `set -e` the script aborts without the documented exit-7 diagnostic, leaving nftables applied + dnsmasq on stale config. _Defer reason:_ low-likelihood on standard devbox image layout (`/etc` and `TMPDIR` share overlay fs); partial-state scenario is auditable via the exit code. _Carry-to:_ broader SC-5 partial-state audit — map every fallible seam after `nft -f` to an explicit exit code with diagnostic rather than relying on `set -e` abort.
- **D7 — Drain diff carries no regression tests for new preflight/bootstrap/probe logic.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter iter-171. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/*` (AR-1 bootstrap-detour in `reload-egress.sh`; AR-5 composite-probe in `start-egress.sh`; AR-6 `validate_markers()` preflight in `reload-egress.sh`; AR-9 `mapfile+find` fragment enumeration in `start-egress.sh`). _Nature:_ all four substantive new behaviours ship without `*_test.sh` / shellcheck-harness / fixture coverage. _Defer reason:_ pre-existing condition — Story 2.3 ATDD was explicitly skipped at iter-157 per the `atdd-skip` carve-out; test-runner hasn't landed yet in the project (Epic 13 scope). _Carry-to:_ **Epic 13 CI harness smokes** — when Epic 13 lands a devbox test harness, backfill fixtures for each AR-N behaviour (bootstrap-detour + composite-probe + marker-preflight + mapfile-enumeration).
- **D8 — `INV-devbox-egress-contract` manifest entry lacks `description` / `anchors` enrichment alongside AR-5 contentHash bump.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter iter-171. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts:257-263`. _Nature:_ the iter-166 refresh updated `sourcePath` contentHash to match `docs/invariants/devbox-egress.md`'s new composite-probe section but did not add per-section anchors beyond the existing top-level `INV-devbox-egress-contract` anchor. Readers scanning the manifest see an opaque hash change with no hint that AR-5/AR-6/AR-7/AR-8/AR-9 moved underlying sub-contracts. _Defer reason:_ manifest-UX enhancement; the sync-gate (Story 1.9 FR43) only requires contentHash parity, not anchor precision. _Carry-to:_ invariants-manifest UX pass OR a post-1.0 story that extends the schema with per-hash provenance metadata (iter-N references, drain-item IDs).

## Deferred from: code review of story-2-4 (2026-04-22)

_Story 2.4 (Whitelist source-of-truth + `pnpm devbox:whitelist` atomic-reload CLI) — iter-177 `/bmad-code-review (args: "2")` CR opener. Three-layer Ralph-hosted adversarial fan-out (Blind Hunter cynical review 37 findings / Edge Case Hunter JSON path-tracer 33 entries / Acceptance Auditor spec-fidelity — ALL 5 ACs SATISFIED zero violations). Triage: 5 PATCH (AI-1..AI-5 queued for iter-178..iter-182 drain) + 4 DEFER (below) + ~30 DISMISS. First user-facing-CLI class CR opener precedent — patches cluster at defensive-boundary of CLI layer (filesystem atomicity, redirect/rename primitives, perm-change silence, tempfile predictability) rather than kernel/daemon boundaries (Story 2.3 class)._

- **D1 — `LC_ALL=C` around validator regex + length check.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter iter-177 (finding #11) + confirmatory Edge Case E18. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/whitelist.sh:121-173` (`validate_sources`) + `whitelist.sh:176-182` (`validate_domain`). _Nature:_ bash `[[ =~ ]]` POSIX ERE matching and `${#var}` character-count operator are locale-sensitive under `LC_CTYPE`. The DOMAIN_REGEX character classes `[a-zA-Z0-9-]` are ASCII-scoped and the 253-byte bound is strictly byte-scoped per RFC 1035 SC-5 pin; under non-C locales a regex `a-z` range could unexpectedly match non-ASCII "lowercase" codepoints AND `${#var}` counts characters (not bytes) — mis-accepting multibyte-encoded "valid" domains that exceed 253 bytes. _Defer reason:_ vacuous in current runtime — in-container Ubuntu 24.04 defaults to `C.UTF-8` LC_CTYPE which under glibc keeps `a-z` range ASCII-literal + keeps `${#var}` character-count consistent with byte-count for pure-ASCII input (and DOMAIN_REGEX rejects non-ASCII before `${#}` runs). _Carry-to:_ **Story 2.6 host-side pnpm CLI** wrapping — macOS hosts with non-C `LANG` (e.g., `en_US.UTF-8` + case-folding locales) + Windows Git-Bash locale variance warrant explicit `LC_ALL=C LC_COLLATE=C` prefix on the validator pipeline; aligns with the host-ingress invocation-env hardening scope.
- **D2 — Trap extension to `INT TERM HUP` + explicit fd-201 close in cmd_add/cmd_remove atomic-write sections.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter iter-177 (finding #10) + Edge Case E7 + E10 + E27. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/whitelist.sh:200,303,387` (EXIT-only traps; fd 201 mutation lock released only via explicit `exec 201>&-` at success-path lines 324, 395 + EXIT-driven process exit). _Nature:_ bash EXIT trap fires on most signal-induced termination via implicit shell-cleanup chain, and fd 201 is kernel-reaped on process exit; there is no observable current leak. Defensive-tightening would add explicit `INT TERM HUP` signal handlers that cleanly `exec 201>&-` before abort, making the cleanup deterministic even if the script is embedded in a long-running supervisor (e.g., future `pnpm devbox:watch` wrapper that spawns cmd_add under a persistent shell). _Defer reason:_ no exploitation path in current 1.0 posture (single-shot CLI invocation per `docker exec` / `pnpm` call); cleanup is kernel-guaranteed at process exit. _Carry-to:_ **Story 2.5 container-hardening sweep** — the non-root `dev` user + `cap_drop: [ALL]` + `security_opt: [no-new-privileges:true]` changes the process-lifetime model (e.g., a `dev`-user supervisor loop re-exec'ing whitelist.sh would benefit from deterministic cleanup) enough to warrant a cross-cutting signal-handling audit across all Story 2.3/2.4 scripts (start-egress.sh, reload-egress.sh, whitelist.sh, egress-log-tailer.sh, monitor.sh).
- **D3 — `reload-egress.sh` executable pre-check in cmd_sync.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-177 (E20). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/whitelist.sh:250` (`"${RELOAD_SCRIPT}" "${COMPOSED_WHITELIST}" || reload_rc=$?`). _Nature:_ the direct `${RELOAD_SCRIPT}` invocation would exit 127 under `set -e` if the script is missing or non-executable — bypassing the SC-11 `5/6/7` passthrough contract with a confusing diagnostic (operator sees "exec format error" / "no such file" rather than "reload-egress.sh missing or non-executable"). Cleanest guard is a `[[ -x "${RELOAD_SCRIPT}" ]] || { log "ERROR: reload-egress.sh not executable at ${RELOAD_SCRIPT}"; exit 3; }` preflight. _Defer reason:_ zero operational exposure in current runtime — `reload-egress.sh` is installed alongside `whitelist.sh` in the baked devbox image (Story 2.1 Dockerfile copies both with 0755 perms) and has been executable since iter-158 Story 2.3 landing. The pre-check is a diagnostic-quality improvement, not a correctness fix. _Carry-to:_ **Story 2.3 primitive-polish follow-up** (natural home — the contract "reload-egress.sh must be executable" is Story 2.3's SC-13 commitment; Story 2.4 as downstream consumer inherits but does not own) OR **Epic 13 CI harness smoke** that exercises a deliberately-broken RELOAD_SCRIPT path to verify exit-3 diagnostic.
- **D4 — `whitelist.local.txt` CRLF line-ending normalisation in grep-Fxq / grep-Fxv operations.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-177 (E14) + Blind Hunter concurrence (finding #15). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/whitelist.sh:293,379,390` (`grep -Fxq -- "${domain}" "${WHITELIST_LOCAL}"` idempotent-add + idempotent-remove-check; `grep -Fxv -- "${domain}" "${WHITELIST_LOCAL}" > "${tempfile}"` remove-filter). _Nature:_ `grep -Fx`'s byte-exact match treats a CR-suffixed line (`domain.com\r\n`) as distinct from the input literal (`domain.com`). An operator who hand-edits `whitelist.local.txt` via a Windows/SMB pathway and preserves CRLF would observe: (a) `add domain.com` silently duplicates (idempotent-check misses the CR-suffixed entry → atomic-append writes a second copy; `sort -u` during compose collapses them but the `log "... already present; no-op"` path is bypassed and the mutation lock / reload cycle fires spuriously); (b) `remove domain.com` hits the "not present" idempotent no-op path (false-negative) even when a CR-suffixed entry exists. _Defer reason:_ current in-container edit pathway is `docker exec keel-devbox vi /workspace/.../whitelist.local.txt` which preserves LF line-endings; the hand-edit-via-Windows-SMB pathway is not a documented 1.0 invocation mode. _Carry-to:_ **Epic 13 devbox operator-UX hardening pass** (defensive normalisation at grep boundaries via `tr -d '\r' < file | grep -Fxq ...`) OR **Story 2.6 host-side pnpm CLI wrapping** (the host→container CRLF bridge is a more natural concern at that layer — if `pnpm devbox:whitelist add` on macOS/Windows writes directly to a mounted `whitelist.local.txt`, the CRLF-preservation risk reappears at the host layer).
