Iter-216 closure re-triage kept AR-21 deferred (build/rebuild cosmetic-only log drift; no destructive surface). _Carry-to:_ **Story 2.7+ host-side CLI consolidation** OR **Future hygiene-pass story** — extend AI-12's `unset` block to build + rebuild for complete uniformity across the devbox:* CLI surface.

## Deferred from: Story 2.6 CR closure iter-216 (2026-04-22)

_`/bmad-code-review (args: "2")` closure re-run surfaced 2 PATCH + 7 NITPICK findings against the cumulative Story 2.6 diff (`2f57265..HEAD`, iter-201 landing + iter-205..iter-215 drain). 2 PATCH → QUEUE fix tasks (AI-12 clean.sh AI-8 drain-gap, AI-13 env-check export-whitespace). 7 NITPICK triaged DEFER (AR-22..AR-28 below). These are posture / edge-case / heuristic polish items that do not block Story 2.6 closure; carry-forward to operator-workstation smoke OR downstream stories as noted per-entry._

- **AR-22 — `env-check.sh` silently accepts unterminated quoted values (e.g. `FOO="bar` with no closing quote).** _Source:_ Blind Hunter iter-216. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/env-check.sh:101-113`. _Nature:_ The AI-6 quoting-aware parse (`${rest%%${first_char}*}`) returns `rest` unchanged when no closing quote exists → leading quote stripped but remainder captured verbatim. Operator sees a silently-accepted malformed value rather than a warning. No security risk (the accepted value is still bounded by line-length); UX risk is a confusing parse result that matches the buggy `.envrc` literally. _Defer reason:_ Defensive parser edge case, very low frequency; realistic mis-typings are caught by upstream missing-var check + downstream shape validator. _Carry-to:_ **Future ergonomic-pass story** — add quote-closure detection (compare `rest` to `value` post-strip); if unchanged, warn "unterminated quote in value for KEY on line N". Fold naturally into AR-17 broader env-check hardening.

- **AR-23 — `restart.sh` indefinite-`running` state falls through to `start.sh` on poll timeout (soft-gate posture).** _Source:_ Blind Hunter iter-216. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/restart.sh:55-73`. _Nature:_ AI-11 (iter-215) documented the SOFT-gate decision in its RESOLVED block: on timeout, log "timed out" + proceed regardless. Pathological scenario: `docker compose stop` returns 0 (SIGTERM sent + grace expired) but daemon-state stays `running` (kernel-level container freeze, cgroups-v1 parent-slice lock) → poll loop hits `*)` arm until 10s timeout then proceeds to `start.sh`, which sees `running` and declares success against a doomed-but-not-killed container. _Defer reason:_ Intentional soft-gate; start.sh has its own 120s healthcheck bound as downstream validation, so a truly-stuck container would fail the outer restart via the healthcheck path rather than silently "succeed". Hard-abort would fail transient-daemon-pressure restarts that resolve within the broader 120s outer bound. _Carry-to:_ **Future hardening** — if telemetry shows pathological stuck-`running` daemons trapping operators, add an escalation path: on timeout, `docker kill "${CONTAINER_NAME}" || true` then proceed (or exit 11 with a "stop did not take effect" hint). Re-evaluate at end-of-Epic-2 retrospective.

- **AR-24 — `env-check.sh` `git rev-parse` three-tier resolver leaks into vendored/submodule layouts where fork is INSIDE parent-repo's git tree.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter iter-216. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/env-check.sh:38-46`. _Nature:_ AI-5's three-tier resolver prefers `git rev-parse --show-toplevel` as tier 2 — authoritative when `.git` is present. In the vendored-inside-git layout (fork is a subdirectory of a parent repo that has its own `.git`), rev-parse returns the PARENT repo's toplevel, not the fork's. `.envrc` is then searched at the parent root, missing the substrate `.envrc` at the fork root. _Defer reason:_ `KEEL_DEVBOX_REPO_ROOT` operator escape hatch covers — `env-check.sh:81` error message explicitly guides operators to export it. Tier-1 override is unconditional, so the vendored-inside-git operator has a documented one-line fix. _Carry-to:_ **Future vendoring-UX story** IF fork operator feedback indicates friction — add a `package.json` name-match probe between git-toplevel and `${DEVBOX_DIR}/../..`; prefer the tier-3 arithmetic root when its `package.json` name matches the substrate's package.json name. Otherwise keep the override path.

- **AR-25 — `monitor-host.sh` host-filesystem probe is indirect proxy for container's bind-mounted file.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter iter-216. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/monitor-host.sh:54`. _Nature:_ `[[ ! -f "${DEVBOX_DIR}/scripts/monitor.sh" ]]` checks the HOST filesystem as a proxy for the container's bind-mounted `/workspace/packages/devbox/scripts/monitor.sh`. If the workspace bind-mount is broken (operator edited `docker-compose.yml` removing the mount), host-probe passes but `docker exec` fails with a terser "No such file or directory" error. Blind Hunter's own note flagged as "acceptable heuristic". _Defer reason:_ Correctness-as-heuristic; the common failure mode (fresh clone missing the file after a bad merge) is correctly detected. Bind-mount-broken is a separate Story 2.1 substrate regression that would surface via `pnpm devbox:start` healthcheck failure, not monitor invocation. _Carry-to:_ **Future ergonomic-pass story** OR **AR-19 `_lib.sh` refactor** — add an additional `docker exec "${CONTAINER_NAME}" test -f /workspace/packages/devbox/scripts/monitor.sh` probe OR translate the terser exec-rc into a friendly "workspace bind-mount may be broken — check docker-compose.yml" error.

- **AR-26 — `start.sh`/`restart.sh` arithmetic on non-integer timeout envvar aborts with cryptic bash error.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-216. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/start.sh:75`, `packages/devbox/scripts/restart.sh:51`. _Nature:_ `stop_deadline=$(( $(date +%s) + STOP_POLL_TIMEOUT_S ))` / `healthcheck_deadline=$(( $(date +%s) + HEALTHCHECK_TIMEOUT_S ))` under `set -euo pipefail` aborts with rc 1 + stderr "value too great for base" if operator sets the envvar with units: `KEEL_DEVBOX_START_HEALTHCHECK_TIMEOUT_S=120s` or `KEEL_DEVBOX_RESTART_STOP_POLL_TIMEOUT_S=10s`. No shape validation; no friendly message. _Defer reason:_ Defensive UX polish. No current shape-validation contract for timeout envvars; AR-11 (iter-201) scoped shape validation to tmpfs-MB knobs only. Realistic operator input (integer seconds per the env-var docstring) works correctly. _Carry-to:_ **Future env-check hardening pass** — extend shape validation from tmpfs-MB knobs to timeout knobs (positive-integer seconds); pair with AR-17 broader env-check refactor. Fails `env-check.sh` upstream before the arithmetic ever runs.

- **AR-27 — `start.sh` `created` state falls through to `*)` arm and polls to 120s timeout with misleading "failed to reach healthy state" message.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-216. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/start.sh:105-119`. _Nature:_ If `docker compose up -d` fails AFTER creating the container but before starting it (rare: image-pull race, cgroupsv1 parent-slice resource-limit reject, buildkit failure mid-start), `.State.Status=created` hits the unrecognised-state arm; script polls for 120s then exits 11 with misleading "failed to reach healthy state" (container never reached a healthcheck because it never started). _Defer reason:_ Rare edge case. The AI-2 (iter-206) fix already split the case arm into `unhealthy`/`exited|dead|removing|paused`; extending the fatal-state arm to include `created` is a minor symmetry fix. _Carry-to:_ **Future start.sh hardening** — add `created` to the fatal-state arm at `start.sh:105` with a friendly "container created but never started — check compose config" message.

- **AR-28 — `monitor-host.sh` missing `--user dev` pin (asymmetric with whitelist-host.sh AI-9 posture).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-216. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/monitor-host.sh:66`. _Nature:_ AI-9 (iter-213) added `--user dev` to `whitelist-host.sh` as an explicit-pin defense against fork override flips to `user: root`. `monitor-host.sh` runs `tail -F` on `/workspace/logs/egress-queries.jsonl` without the pin. If the override flips to root, tail reads as root — low-risk (read-only, no write-state footprint), but posture-asymmetric with AI-9. _Defer reason:_ Read-only operation; AI-9's mutation-lock concern (EPERM on flock or atomic-rename) does not apply. Symmetry fix, not correctness fix. _Carry-to:_ **Future posture-consistency pass** OR **AR-19 `_lib.sh` refactor** — add `--user dev` to `monitor-host.sh:66` exec line for posture consistency with AI-9.

## Deferred from: Story 2.6 CR closure iter-219 (2026-04-22)

_`/bmad-code-review (args: "2")` 2nd closure re-run surfaced 7 new DEFER items against the cumulative Story 2.6 diff (`65ef3a3..HEAD` / 14 scripts + README.md + root package.json / 1162 diff lines). Acceptance Auditor ZERO-FINDING for 3rd consecutive pass (iter-204 / iter-216 / iter-219) — AC-to-code mapping clean. Edge Case Hunter surfaced 3 pre-existing env-check.sh parser edge cases (AR-29/30/31); Blind Hunter surfaced 4 docs/cosmetic drifts (AR-32/33/34/35). All DEFERRED — no PATCH remaining; CR closure achieves ZERO-PATCH. Story 2.6 → `done`; within-epic auto-advance to Story 2.7 per § Cross-epic transition._

- **AR-29 — `env-check.sh:89` `declare -A parsed` requires bash ≥ 4; macOS default `/bin/bash` (3.2.57) aborts with cryptic `declare: -A: invalid option`.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-219. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/env-check.sh:89`. _Nature:_ Pre-existing since iter-201 landing (not drain-introduced). On a macOS operator workstation without Homebrew bash (or with default-`/bin/bash`-first PATH), `#!/usr/bin/env bash` picks `/bin/bash` 3.2.57; `declare -A` is bash ≥ 4 syntax and errors with `declare: -A: invalid option` before any useful hint prints. No first-run UX for macOS operators in the unusual-PATH case. _Defer reason:_ Practical M4-Pro Homebrew operators (per NFR2 + direnv-conventional setup) have `/opt/homebrew/bin/bash` first on PATH and hit zero friction. Hardening = 2-line preflight guard `if (( BASH_VERSINFO[0] < 4 )); then echo 'env-check requires bash 4+ (macOS: brew install bash)' >&2; exit 2; fi` at env-check.sh top. First-run UX polish for an edge-case PATH configuration; not load-bearing. _Carry-to:_ **Future env-check hardening pass** OR **Story 2.10 prerequisite-check** — Story 2.10 scope-owns docker/claude-auth/gh-auth prerequisite checks; extending to cover `bash >= 4` aligns naturally.

- **AR-30 — `env-check.sh:85` `.envrc` path resolves to a readable directory (not a regular file) aborts with noisy bash `read: <path> is a directory` instead of clean exit-3.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-219. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/env-check.sh:85`. _Nature:_ `[[ -r "${ENVRC_PATH}" ]]` check passes for a readable directory; the subsequent `while IFS= read -r line` at line 93 errors loudly (not exit 3, not the expected "copy from .envrc.example" hint). Fix = one additional `[[ ! -f "${ENVRC_PATH}" ]]` check alongside `[[ ! -r ]]`. _Defer reason:_ Operator would have to `mkdir .envrc` (reverse of the substrate pattern) to trigger this; the noisy-bash-read-error is its own signal that something is wrong. Extremely low frequency; ergonomic polish at best. _Carry-to:_ **Future env-check hardening pass** — fold into AR-17/AR-22 broader env-check parser refactor.

- **AR-31 — `env-check.sh:93` UTF-8 BOM (EF BB BF) on first `.envrc` line silently skips the first variable (typically `KEEL_DEVBOX_ARCH` → "missing").** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-219. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/env-check.sh:93`. _Nature:_ Operators who edit `.envrc` in Windows Notepad or PowerShell `Set-Content -Encoding UTF8` without `-NoNewline` emit a UTF-8 BOM at file start. AI-7 (iter-211) line-level `\r` strip does NOT strip BOM bytes. First `export KEEL_DEVBOX_ARCH=...` line reads as `<BOM>export ...`; the `^KEEL_DEVBOX_` regex (and the AI-13 `^export[[:space:]]` guard) both fail to match → variable silently skipped → reported missing. Fix = one-line BOM strip at loop head: `line="${line#$'\xef\xbb\xbf'}"` alongside AI-7's `\r` strip. _Defer reason:_ Symmetrical with AI-7 in spirit but pre-existing since iter-201 (not a drain regression); operator workaround is "save as UTF-8 (no BOM)" — same guidance as for CRLF on Windows. AI-7 was drain-addressed because CRLF was the dominant drift-pattern; BOM is secondary. _Carry-to:_ **Future env-check hardening pass** — extend the line-sanitisation block at the top of the parse loop to strip BOM + CR + any future byte-order-mark variants uniformly. Could pair naturally with AR-17/AR-22 env-check refactor.

- **AR-32 — `packages/devbox/README.md:469` verification recipe `pnpm devbox:shell -c 'whoami && pwd && id'` may not forward `-c` cleanly across pnpm versions.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter iter-219. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/README.md:469`. _Nature:_ pnpm 8.x forwards args after the script name automatically, but `-c` is a recognised pnpm global flag in legacy versions (pnpm 7 pre-`--`-convention); the unambiguous safe form is `pnpm devbox:shell -- -c 'whoami && pwd && id'` which ensures the `-c` reaches `shell.sh "$@"` → `bash -l -c '…'` regardless of pnpm version. _Defer reason:_ Project pins pnpm via `packageManager` in root `package.json`; modern pnpm is known to forward unrecognised flags to the script. Real-world operator impact is near-zero; docs polish. _Carry-to:_ **Future README polish pass** OR **AR-18 (per-script `--help` rollout)** — update the verification recipe to the `--`-form at the same time as adding `--help` handling to `shell.sh`.

- **AR-33 — `packages/devbox/scripts/clean.sh:16` docstring "RESERVED; rejected at 1.0 (SC-11)" wording vs actual no-op-with-log behaviour.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter iter-219. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/clean.sh:16`. _Nature:_ Top-of-file comment block line 16 says `--allow-broad-prune` is "rejected at 1.0" (suggesting exit non-zero), but the implementation (lines 78-83) accepts the flag as a no-op with a warning log per SC-11. The usage() block at line 59 uses the correct wording ("RESERVED at 1.0; no-op"); only the top-of-file comment drifts. Fix = 1-word edit: `rejected` → `no-op`. _Defer reason:_ Operator reading `clean.sh --help` (future AR-18) or the usage block on unknown-flag sees the correct wording; only a reader of the top-of-file docstring sees the drift. Aesthetic, not functional. _Carry-to:_ **Future README/docs polish pass** OR **AR-18 `--help` rollout** — align the top-of-file comment block with the usage() wording at the same pass.

- **AR-34 — `packages/devbox/README.md:476` operator-verification recipe uses raw `docker volume inspect keel-devbox_keel_home_dev` without FR1-exception annotation.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter iter-219. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/README.md:476`. _Nature:_ FR1 says "Operators never type `docker`, `docker compose`, or `docker exec` directly" — the migration-recovery verification section (§ Operator migration § Verification) intentionally uses `docker volume inspect` as the read-only primitive because there is no `pnpm devbox:volume:inspect` verb. Fix options: (a) add a `pnpm devbox:volume:inspect` verb (scope-creep; would couple to volume naming which Story 2.11 shared-devbox-mode may refactor); (b) add a prose annotation acknowledging the FR1 exception for emergency migration. _Defer reason:_ Section is operator-recovery, not day-to-day operation; FR1 applies to routine interaction, not emergency migration. Annotation would be nice but not load-bearing. _Carry-to:_ **Future README polish pass** OR **Story 2.11 shared-devbox-mode** — if Story 2.11 adds a volume-naming abstraction, it could also add volume-introspection verbs.

- **AR-35 — `.envrc.example` ↔ `env-check.sh:471-485` `REQUIRED_VARS` array drift risk (no pre-merge gate asserts byte-for-byte parity).** _Source:_ Blind Hunter iter-219. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/.envrc.example` ↔ `packages/devbox/scripts/env-check.sh:471-485`. _Nature:_ Story 2.2 shipped `.envrc.example`; Story 2.6 iter-201 landed `REQUIRED_VARS` in env-check.sh. If a future PR edits one without the other, drift goes undetected until an operator's `pnpm devbox:env:check` reports a phantom-missing or missing-required variable. Fix = runtime contract-shape check (pnpm devbox:env:check-contract: parse `.envrc.example` → extract `KEEL_DEVBOX_*` names → diff against `REQUIRED_VARS` → exit 2 on drift) OR pre-merge sync-gate invariant. _Defer reason:_ Story 2.17 (compose-shape runtime check via `packages/keel-invariants/src/check-devbox-compose-shape.ts`) is the explicit scope-owner for runtime shape-drift detection per Story 2.5 carry-forward; `.envrc`-shape is the natural companion check. _Carry-to:_ **Story 2.17 `check-devbox-compose-shape.ts`** — extend scope to include `.envrc.example` ↔ `env-check.sh REQUIRED_VARS` parity, OR create a sibling `check-devbox-envrc-shape.ts` invariant.

## Deferred from: Story 2.7 CR iter-226 (2026-04-22)

_`/bmad-code-review (args: "2")` one-pass closure against Story 2.7 iter-223 implementation commit `098aa41` (5 files / 231 diff lines: `packages/devbox/scripts/ralph-build-host.sh` + `ralph-plan-host.sh` + `package.json` + `packages/devbox/README.md` + `AGENTS.md`). 3-layer adversarial triage: Blind Hunter 17 findings + Edge Case Hunter 20 findings + Acceptance Auditor 0 findings = 37 raw → **0 PATCH / 0 DECISION / 15 DEFER / 22 DISMISS** after deduplication + classification. ZERO-PATCH means no fix-drain queue — CR closure achieved in a single pass (contrast Story 2.6: 3 CR passes + 13 AI drains). SECOND cumulative CR-gate ZERO-PATCH precedent; FIRST one-pass outcome. Story 2.7 → `done`; within-epic auto-advance to Story 2.8 per § Cross-epic transition._

- **AR-36 — `KEEL_RALPH_MODE` host-shell export does not propagate to container PID 1 via `docker attach`.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter iter-226. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/ralph-build-host.sh:60` + `ralph-plan-host.sh:60`. _Nature:_ `export KEEL_RALPH_MODE="${RALPH_MODE}"` sets the variable in the host shell. `docker attach` then connects host stdio to a container PID 1 whose environment was frozen at container-start (via `docker compose up`). The export happens AFTER `start.sh` is invoked, so compose-env pass-through cannot see it either. Under current `CMD: [sleep, infinity]`, no consumer exists in the container; SC-2 Epic-3 carve-out governs. _Defer reason:_ Epic 3 owns the in-container Ralph TUI runtime and the mode-signal consumer design. Epic 3 can choose to (a) read a sidecar file the wrapper writes to a mounted volume before attach, (b) require the wrapper to `export KEEL_RALPH_MODE` before `start.sh` so compose's `environment:` clause propagates it to the container's PID 1, or (c) inject via `docker exec -e KEEL_RALPH_MODE=...` ahead of each iteration. Envelope-level export is the spec-sanctioned AC 5 signal; consumer wiring is Epic 3's scope. _Carry-to:_ **Epic 3 Story 3.x — in-container Ralph TUI runtime** — verify mode-signal mechanism; may require `ralph-*-host.sh` to move the export BEFORE `start.sh` invocation AND add `KEEL_RALPH_MODE: ${KEEL_RALPH_MODE:-build}` to `packages/devbox/docker-compose.yml environment:` stanza (substrate touch — AMEND path per FR44), OR switch to sidecar-file signalling (wrapper-only change, no substrate touch).

- **AR-37 — `start.sh || exit $?` passthrough swallows per-exit-code differentiation.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter iter-226. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/ralph-build-host.sh:46` + `ralph-plan-host.sh:46`. _Nature:_ The wrapper cannot distinguish "image not built (10)" from "healthcheck timeout (11)" from "docker unreachable (8)" for its own log output; operator sees only `start.sh`'s own stderr + the final exit code. The exit-code-meaning table in README § Ralph loop promises differentiated meaning the wrapper does not deliver at its own log layer. _Defer reason:_ SC-12 pins the exit-code passthrough contract (schema is inherited from Story 2.6 unchanged); per-code logging is UX polish, not correctness. Story 2.6 *-host.sh shims follow the same passthrough pattern — posture consistency governs. _Carry-to:_ **`_lib.sh` refactor** (Story 2.6 AR-19 substrate-wide threshold; reached at Story 2.8/2.9 potentially) — add shared `log_and_exit <code> <context>` helper that branches on the exit code and emits a contextual hint (e.g. "image not built; run `pnpm devbox:build`" for 10, "healthcheck timeout; check `pnpm devbox:logs`" for 11). Applies uniformly to all shims that call `start.sh`.

- **AR-38 — Post-auto-start race fallback is a single re-inspect with no retry/backoff.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter iter-226. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/ralph-build-host.sh:49-53` + `ralph-plan-host.sh:49-53`. _Nature:_ Between `start.sh` returning 0 and the wrapper's `docker inspect` re-check, the container could enter `running → exited` (PID 1 crash), `starting → restarting` (init failure), or still be in eventual-consistency lag (docker daemon caching). A single re-inspect misses legitimate in-flight transitions; the wrapper emits `exit 9` when a short retry-with-backoff (e.g. 3 × 1s) would have captured the settled state. _Defer reason:_ Spec explicitly scopes this as a "rare race" (Story 2.7 Task 1 PATCH 3 comment at `ralph-build-host.sh:50`); healthcheck polling inside `start.sh` already eliminates most eventual-consistency windows. Retry-with-backoff is infrastructure-grade complexity for a near-zero-frequency scenario. _Carry-to:_ **`_lib.sh` refactor** — shared `wait_for_container_running <name> <timeout>` helper with configurable retry/backoff. Applies to any shim that performs post-start state reconciliation.

- **AR-39 — `AGENTS.md § Ralph loop` "NEVER call `docker attach` directly" wording contradicts wrapper's own `exec docker attach` (substrate carve-out implicit but unstated).** _Source:_ Blind Hunter iter-226. _Location:_ `AGENTS.md:114` (new § Ralph loop (Story 2.7)). _Nature:_ The FR1 non-toggle-able invariant text reads as a blanket prohibition; the wrapper itself is the implementation that makes `docker attach` unnecessary for operators/agents. A future grep-based invariant-lint scanning `packages/devbox/scripts/` for `docker attach` would flag this file as a violation if naive. The same implicit carve-out applies to `docker compose`, `docker exec`, `docker info`, `docker inspect` usage inside `packages/devbox/scripts/`. _Defer reason:_ Readers currently understand the carve-out from context (the surrounding bullets describe the wrapper implementation, so the "NEVER" clearly governs operators/agents, not the shim itself). Explicit wording is a polish pass, not a correctness fix. _Carry-to:_ **AGENTS.md invariant-rules wording pass** (potentially Story 2.17 sync-gate integration) — add "(substrate scripts under `packages/devbox/scripts/` are the implementing carve-out — they wrap docker primitives so operators and agents don't have to)" clarification to the FR1 bullet.

- **AR-40 — `log()` writes all output to stderr unconditionally — info and error messages undifferentiated.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter iter-226. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/ralph-build-host.sh:32` + `ralph-plan-host.sh:32`. _Nature:_ `log() { printf '[ralph:%s] %s\n' "${RALPH_MODE}" "$*" >&2; }` sends benign info messages ("container already running; attaching directly") to stderr alongside genuine errors ("docker unreachable"). Tooling that captures stderr separately (CI log aggregators, operator terminal multiplexers) will see false positives for info-level events. _Defer reason:_ Story 2.6 *-host.sh shims (13 of them) follow identical stderr-only logging pattern — refactoring just the 2 Ralph wrappers creates cross-shim inconsistency. Info/error differentiation is a substrate-wide concern, not a Story 2.7 concern. _Carry-to:_ **`_lib.sh` refactor** — shared `log_info` (stdout) + `log_error` (stderr) differentiated helpers. Applies uniformly to all 15 host-side shims.

- **AR-41 — No `command -v docker` pre-flight guard — missing docker CLI produces interleaved `command not found` on stderr before the documented "docker unreachable" log + exit 8.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter iter-226. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/ralph-build-host.sh:36` + `ralph-plan-host.sh:36`. _Nature:_ `if ! docker info --format '...' >/dev/null 2>&1;` sends `docker`'s own "command not found" to stderr when the binary is absent, BEFORE the `log "docker unreachable"` line runs. Operator sees `bash: docker: command not found` immediately followed by `[ralph:build] docker unreachable — is the daemon running?` — confusing because the message blames the daemon when the real cause is the CLI itself. _Defer reason:_ Story 2.6 *-host.sh shims don't guard `command -v docker` either — extending the guard only to Ralph shims creates 13-vs-2 inconsistency. Extremely rare scenario (docker binary absent but pnpm reachable implies a severely broken operator environment). _Carry-to:_ **`_lib.sh` refactor** OR **Story 2.10 prerequisite-check** (scope-owner for docker CLI availability gating) — uniform `ensure_docker_cli` pre-flight across all shims.

- **AR-42 — `status=paused` not handled (attach proceeds against paused PID 1 instead of unpause-or-abort).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-226. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/ralph-build-host.sh:42-47` + `ralph-plan-host.sh:42-47`. _Nature:_ `if [[ "${status}" != "running" ]]` treats `paused` as "not running" and invokes `start.sh`, but `docker compose up -d` on a paused container does not unpause it — the container stays paused and the subsequent `docker attach` hangs because PID 1 cannot process stdio. _Defer reason:_ Operator-explicit `docker pause keel-devbox` is non-standard workflow; no pnpm verb pauses the container. Extremely rare. Workaround is `docker unpause` + retry. _Carry-to:_ **`_lib.sh` refactor** — shared `ensure_container_runnable` helper treats paused/exited/restarting as uniform preconditions (unpause-if-paused, start-if-exited, wait-if-restarting).

- **AR-43 — `status=restarting` transient state treated as "not running" → redundant `start.sh` invocation during restart loop.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-226. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/ralph-build-host.sh:44` + `ralph-plan-host.sh:44`. _Nature:_ When a container is mid-restart (docker's `restart: unless-stopped` or manual `docker restart` in flight), `status=restarting`; the wrapper invokes `start.sh` redundantly. Compose's `up -d` is idempotent, so this is wasteful rather than destructive — but it adds latency + muddies logs. _Defer reason:_ Compose's idempotency means no correctness impact; the only cost is a few seconds of unnecessary healthcheck polling. _Carry-to:_ **`_lib.sh` refactor** — shared container-state reconciler handles `paused` + `restarting` + `exited` uniformly.

- **AR-44 — Container running-but-unhealthy → wrapper attaches to broken PID 1 (no pre-attach health gate on skip-start branch).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-226. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/ralph-build-host.sh:65` + `ralph-plan-host.sh:65`. _Nature:_ The skip-start branch trusts `status=running` and proceeds directly to `docker attach`. If the container's healthcheck has transitioned `healthy → unhealthy` mid-session (e.g., dnsmasq crashed; whitelist-reload stuck), the operator attaches to a container whose PID 1 may be unresponsive or mid-recovery. Under current `CMD: [sleep, infinity]` there is no Ralph process to attach to anyway; Epic 3's TUI would observe a blank terminal. _Defer reason:_ `start.sh` owns the healthcheck contract on the auto-start branch; the skip-start branch explicitly opts out per SC-2 ("AC 2 skip-start"). Health gating on re-attach is Story 2.13's scope (healthcheck endpoints). _Carry-to:_ **`_lib.sh` refactor** OR **Story 2.13 healthcheck endpoints** — add pre-attach `docker inspect --format '{{.State.Health.Status}}'` gate; exit `11` on unhealthy.

- **AR-45 — Concurrent wrapper invocations (multi-terminal) multiplex stdin to same PID 1; no single-attach lock.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-226. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/ralph-build-host.sh:65` + `ralph-plan-host.sh:65`. _Nature:_ Two operators running `pnpm ralph:build` from separate terminals both call `exec docker attach` against the same container. Docker's native semantics multiplex — both stdin streams interleave, both see duplicate stdout, detach-keys from either session detach both. This is surprising but spec-silent. _Defer reason:_ Docker's multiplex behavior is documented + long-standing; fighting it with a flock-based lock would break operator workflows that intentionally share terminals (pair programming, multi-screen setup). Operator-discipline is the norm. _Carry-to:_ **Future operator-UX pass** — add "only one attach at a time" note to README § Ralph loop.

- **AR-46 — `docker attach` silent exit on PID 1 crash (no post-exec log message; operator sees only shell prompt return).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-226. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/ralph-build-host.sh:65` + `ralph-plan-host.sh:65`. _Nature:_ `exec docker attach` replaces the wrapper shell; post-exec instrumentation is impossible without dropping `exec` (which re-introduces the "No signal trapping" gotcha — Story 2.7 PATCH 3 comment explicitly guards against defensive traps). On container crash, docker attach exits with the container's exit code and the operator returns to the host shell with no contextual message beyond `[docker output]`. _Defer reason:_ `exec` is load-bearing for signal propagation (SIGINT/SIGTERM/SIGPIPE reach PID 1 directly). Any post-exec instrumentation breaks the propagation guarantee. _Carry-to:_ **`_lib.sh` refactor** — if ever wrapping `exec`, document the signal-forwarding contract explicitly so the wrapper can be removed if contract breaks.

- **AR-47 — `docker info` succeeds but operator lacks `inspect` permission → wrapper proceeds to `start.sh` which re-fails opaquely.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-226. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/ralph-build-host.sh:42` + `ralph-plan-host.sh:42`. _Nature:_ Custom docker RBAC (some enterprise setups) grants `docker info` (server-version read) but not per-container `docker inspect`. The pre-flight at line 36 passes; the inspect at line 42 returns empty `status=""`; the wrapper enters the auto-start branch; `start.sh`'s own `docker inspect` also fails opaquely. _Defer reason:_ Default dockerd grants equal rights for info + inspect on containers owned by the calling user; custom RBAC is non-standard. Extremely rare; no real-world reports. _Carry-to:_ **Future docker-permission hardening pass** (no immediate action needed given zero evidence of occurrence).

- **AR-48 — `docker inspect` has no timeout gate → daemon hang blocks wrapper indefinitely.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-226. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/ralph-build-host.sh:42,49` + `ralph-plan-host.sh:42,49`. _Nature:_ An unresponsive docker daemon (OS-level hang, out-of-disk on `/var/lib/docker`) causes `docker inspect` to block. The wrapper offers no `timeout 10 docker inspect` guard; operator sees hung terminal with no feedback. _Defer reason:_ Daemon-hang is an OS-level failure; hardcoded timeout could introduce false-positive exits on cold-start daemons (RAM-pressure, post-reboot warm-up). Operator response to hang is `docker restart` or machine reboot. _Carry-to:_ **`_lib.sh` refactor** — shared `docker_with_timeout <seconds> <cmd...>` helper, gated by evidence of daemon-hang occurrence.

- **AR-49 — `BASH_SOURCE[0]` symlink drift: `SCRIPT_DIR` resolution doesn't `readlink -f` before `cd`.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-226. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/ralph-build-host.sh:29` + `ralph-plan-host.sh:29`. _Nature:_ If an operator symlinks `/usr/local/bin/ralph-build` → `packages/devbox/scripts/ralph-build-host.sh` and invokes the symlink, `BASH_SOURCE[0]` resolves to the symlink path; `dirname + cd + pwd` gives `/usr/local/bin`, not `packages/devbox/scripts/`. The subsequent `"${SCRIPT_DIR}/start.sh"` fails with "No such file". _Defer reason:_ All 13 Story 2.6 *-host.sh shims use the same pattern — consistency governs. Symlinking shims is non-standard; pnpm invokes them directly via `package.json`'s script mapping, not via PATH-symlink. Zero real-world risk for the documented invocation surface. _Carry-to:_ **`_lib.sh` refactor** — shared `SCRIPT_DIR` derivation using `readlink -f` for symlink safety. Applies uniformly to all shims.

- **AR-50 — `KEEL_DEVBOX_CONTAINER_NAME` override is not documented in README § Ralph loop (nor in AGENTS.md § Ralph loop).** _Source:_ Blind Hunter iter-226. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/README.md:505` (new § Ralph loop). _Nature:_ The wrapper honors `KEEL_DEVBOX_CONTAINER_NAME` per SC-11 (`CONTAINER_NAME="${KEEL_DEVBOX_CONTAINER_NAME:-keel-devbox}"`), but neither the operator-facing README section nor the agent-facing AGENTS.md section mentions this override. Operators running multiple devboxes (fork + worktree + main) have no visible knob documented in the Story 2.7 section. _Defer reason:_ Story 2.2 introduced the override and documented it in `.envrc.example`; Story 2.7 correctly inherits it without re-documenting. Documenting every env-var flow in every consuming story's README would balloon each section; cross-reference to Story 2.2's upstream doc is the cleaner pattern. _Carry-to:_ **Future README polish pass** — add consolidated `## Environment variables` section at `packages/devbox/README.md` root OR add a one-line cross-ref bullet "(container name override via `KEEL_DEVBOX_CONTAINER_NAME` — see `.envrc.example`)" under § Auto-start contract.

## Deferred from: code review of story-2.8 (2026-04-22)

_Story 2.8 (`claude-code-oauth-via-pnpm-claude.sh` — FR3 Claude-side invocation path) — iter-233 `/bmad-code-review (args: "2")`. Three-layer adversarial review (Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter + Acceptance Auditor). **Zero PATCHes surfaced** — THIRD cumulative one-pass ZERO-PATCH CR precedent (Story 1.13 iter-85 first; Story 2.7 iter-226 second; Story 2.8 iter-233 third). The nine defers below are: (a) spec-authorised choices pinned by SC-4 / SC-6 / SC-13 / SC-15 / SC-16; (b) substrate-owned contracts (Story 2.5 image + named-volume); (c) upstream-CLI-owned semantics (Anthropic token lifecycle); or (d) narrow races (TOCTOU between `docker inspect` and `docker exec`). Auditor returned zero AC/SC violations; wrapper matches § Shim structure template verbatim._

- **AR-51 — Non-TTY invocation fails on hardcoded `-it` (cron / CI / piped stdin).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-233 (HIGH) + Blind Hunter iter-233 (LOW). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/claude-host.sh:58`. _Nature:_ Hardcoded `docker exec -it` fails with "the input device is not a TTY" in non-TTY contexts (`pnpm claude < /dev/null`, cron, CI runners, `pnpm claude | tee log.txt`). Sibling `shell.sh:37-42` forks on `$#` to pick `-i` vs `-it`; `claude-host.sh` has no such fork. _Defer reason:_ SC-6 explicitly pins hardcoded `-it` — "OAuth flow IS the AC" — and the wrapper is interactive-only by contract. Non-TTY contexts are outside the AC 1-5 scope at 1.0. Story 2.7's `ralph-build-host.sh` shares the same interactive-by-contract posture. _Carry-to:_ **Post-Epic-2 polish** — if a downstream story (e.g., CI-driven `pnpm claude -p "hello"` composition) surfaces a non-TTY use case, fork on `[[ -t 0 && -t 1 ]]` to drop `-t` like sibling `shell.sh`; requires an FR44 AMEND because SC-6 is a pinned contract.
- **AR-52 — TOCTOU between `docker inspect` status check and `docker exec`.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter iter-233 (LOW). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/claude-host.sh:46-58`. _Nature:_ Container could stop between the inspect call (line 46-49) and `docker exec` (line 58); `docker exec` then fails with its own error and propagates a non-uniform exit code (not `9`), violating the documented exit-code schema. _Defer reason:_ Narrow race — container stopping mid-wrapper is rare in operator workflows. AGENTS.md § Ralph loop (Story 2.7) documents an identical "rare race" precedent for the ralph wrappers ("container exited between start.sh's success and the attach call"). Docker's own error bubbles via the `*` schema slot. _Carry-to:_ **`_lib.sh` refactor** — shared `docker_exec_with_retry <N> <cmd...>` helper could collapse the gap, but only if evidence shows the race fires in practice. Low priority.
- **AR-53 — Exit code `8` catches only `docker info`; daemon-dies-between races collapse to misleading exit `9`.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter iter-233 (LOW). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/claude-host.sh:40-49`. _Nature:_ If the docker daemon dies between the `docker info` check (line 40) and `docker inspect` (line 46), the inspect's `|| true` swallows the daemon error and `state` becomes empty, producing exit `9` ("container not running") instead of `8` ("docker unreachable"). _Defer reason:_ Narrow race; spec-silent on mid-flight-daemon-death semantics. The swallow pattern is inherited from the § Shim structure template and matches sibling scripts. _Carry-to:_ **`_lib.sh` refactor** — distinguish empty-state from docker-error via stderr capture in the shared helper.
- **AR-54 — Non-running container states (paused/exited/restarting/created) all collapse to a single exit-9 message.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-233 (LOW). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/claude-host.sh:49-52`. _Nature:_ `docker inspect --format '{{.State.Status}}'` returns one of `created/restarting/running/removing/paused/exited/dead`; the wrapper compares only to `"running"` and emits "container 'X' is not running — run 'pnpm devbox:start' first". This is wrong for `paused` (needs `unpause`) and misleading for `restarting` (may auto-recover). _Defer reason:_ UX refinement, not a functional issue. Aligns with sibling `shell.sh` / `attach.sh` precedent which share the same collapse. _Carry-to:_ **`_lib.sh` refactor** — shared `assert_container_running <name>` helper with per-state guidance (`paused → unpause`, `exited → start`, `restarting → wait`). Would apply uniformly to all 16 shims.
- **AR-55 — Nonexistent vs stopped container indistinguishable in exit-9 message.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-233 (LOW). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/claude-host.sh:46-52`. _Nature:_ `docker inspect … 2>/dev/null || true` masks stderr; when the container doesn't exist at all (typo in `KEEL_DEVBOX_CONTAINER_NAME`, e.g. `keel-devbx`), `state=""` and the message says "container 'keel-devbx' is not running — run 'pnpm devbox:start' first" which will not help because `start.sh` creates a differently-named container. _Defer reason:_ Same UX family as AR-54; operator-typo recovery is low-value vs. template consistency cost. _Carry-to:_ **`_lib.sh` refactor** — distinguish empty-state from non-empty-non-running state in the shared helper.
- **AR-56 — UID 1000 ≠ `dev` inside container → token lands at wrong HOME.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-233 (MEDIUM). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/claude-host.sh:58`. _Nature:_ The wrapper passes `--user dev`, which resolves via container's `/etc/passwd` to whatever UID/HOME that entry has. If `dev`'s HOME is not `/home/dev`, the token persists elsewhere and the volume mount `/home/dev/.claude/` stays empty → re-prompts OAuth on every invocation. Wrapper exit is clean (exit 0); user perceives "auth didn't stick." _Defer reason:_ Substrate concern owned by Story 2.5 image contract (Dockerfile `useradd --uid 1000 --gid 1000 --shell /bin/bash --create-home dev` + HOME=/home/dev fixed). Wrapper cannot enforce HOME; image-drift is caught by Story 1.9 sync-gate for Dockerfile drift. _Carry-to:_ **Substrate invariant** — could tighten `INV-devbox-homedev-named-volume` to also assert `dev` user's HOME resolves to `/home/dev` at image build time; not load-bearing at 1.0.
- **AR-57 — `/home/dev/.claude/` non-writable by UID 1000 silently fails inside claude.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-233 (MEDIUM). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/claude-host.sh:58`. _Nature:_ If the named volume is pre-populated as root (e.g., by a prior `--user root` exec), `dev` cannot write. Wrapper cannot see claude's internal error; claude may exit 0 after printing a warning, or may retry OAuth on every invocation. _Defer reason:_ Substrate concern; Dockerfile:251-252 placeholder (`/home/dev/.claude/` pre-created chown'd to `dev:dev`) + Story 2.5 named-volume auto-init semantics own the writability contract. SC-13 explicitly forbids the wrapper from attempting `mkdir` / `chmod`. _Carry-to:_ **Operator runbook** — document triage with `ls -la /home/dev/.claude` pointer in a future README polish; no wrapper change.
- **AR-58 — Concurrent `pnpm claude` races OAuth token write on first-run.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-233 (LOW). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/claude-host.sh:58`. _Nature:_ Two terminals running `pnpm claude` simultaneously on first-run both spawn `docker exec`, both hit the OAuth flow, last writer wins in `/home/dev/.claude/`. Not corrupting (token file is atomic), but wasted UX. _Defer reason:_ First-run race only; multi-terminal OAuth flow is outside AC 1-5 scope. Spec does not mandate concurrency control at the wrapper layer. _Carry-to:_ **Upstream CLI concern** — if `@anthropic-ai/claude-code` gains a lockfile or token-write serialization, wrapper inherits it for free.
- **AR-59 — `pnpm claude --help` consumed by pnpm; operator must use `pnpm claude -- --help`.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter iter-233 (MEDIUM). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/README.md:91-102` (Quick start). _Nature:_ `pnpm <script> --flag` may have pnpm consume specific flags like `--help`; operators expecting `claude --help` behaviour get pnpm's help instead. Wrapper itself (`"$@"`) is correct; issue is in pnpm's invocation contract. _Defer reason:_ pnpm CLI contract outside wrapper scope. SC-16 carries Story 2.6 AR-18 `--help` interception deferral explicitly. _Carry-to:_ **Future README polish pass** — add a one-line note to `packages/devbox/README.md § Quick start` reminding operators to use `pnpm claude -- --help` for claude's own help; grouped with the post-Epic-2 `_lib.sh` + README consolidation work.

## Deferred from: code review of story-2.9 (2026-04-23)

_Story 2.9 (`gh` CLI OAuth via `pnpm gh:auth` — FR3 gh-side invocation path) — iter-244 `/bmad-code-review (args: "2")`. Three-layer Ralph-hosted adversarial review (Blind Hunter as `bmad-review-adversarial-general` via `general-purpose` subagent; Edge Case Hunter as `bmad-review-edge-case-hunter` via `general-purpose` subagent with repo read access; Acceptance Auditor via `general-purpose` subagent with spec file + substrate cross-refs). **Zero PATCHes surfaced** — FOURTH cumulative one-pass ZERO-PATCH CR precedent (Story 1.13 iter-85 first; Story 2.7 iter-226 second; Story 2.8 iter-233 third; Story 2.9 iter-244 fourth). Scope: iter-237 impl commit `fdbd5a2` — 4 files (1 new `gh-auth-host.sh` 68 lines + `package.json` +1 + `README.md` +59 + `AGENTS.md` +14) = 222-line diff. Iter-238..241 orthogonal infrastructure retrofits explicitly out of AC envelope per IP § Context + iter-243 post-dev SM subagent-A verdict. The 11 defers below are: (a) substrate-wide pre-existing patterns inherited from shell.sh + attach.sh + claude-host.sh carrying to the post-Epic-2 `_lib.sh` refactor (SC-14 chain); (b) upstream-CLI-owned semantics already documented in SC-15; (c) narrow races + substrate-UX improvements natural-scope for Story 2.17 Epic 2 close-out or a dedicated lib-extraction story. Acceptance Auditor returned zero AC/SC violations ("All ACs and SCs verified satisfied by the diff"); wrapper matches § Shim structure template verbatim. Triage counts: **0 PATCH / 11 DEFER / 19 DISMISS** after dedupe + SC cross-check._

- **AR-60 — `docker inspect` TOCTOU race between inspect + exec.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (convergent). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/gh-auth-host.sh:62-68`. _Nature:_ Between the `docker inspect` (line ~62) and `docker exec` (line ~68), the container can stop, restart, or be removed. If the race fires, `docker exec` fails with a raw exit-code mapped to `*` rather than the advertised exit 9. Identical race exists in shell.sh:32-35 + attach.sh:32-36 + claude-host.sh:49-52 (AR-52 duplicate confirmation). _Defer reason:_ Fixing it for gh-auth-host.sh alone breaks SC-17 mirror discipline ("MIRRORS claude-host.sh verbatim"); substrate-wide pattern. _Carry-to:_ **post-Epic-2 `_lib.sh` refactor** (SC-14 chain) — shared `ensure_container_running()` helper can add retry-after-inspect loop or race-safe `docker exec` with container-status-check propagation. Applies uniformly to all 17 host-side shims.
- **AR-61 — `state` assignment masks `docker inspect` non-ENOENT failures behind `|| true`.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (convergent). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/gh-auth-host.sh:62`. _Nature:_ `|| true` collapses permission-denied, API-version-mismatch, daemon-hiccup, and malformed-name errors into empty state string → exit 9 "container not running" diagnostic, misdirecting the operator when the real fault is docker-daemon auth/state rather than container state. AR-53 duplicate confirmation. _Defer reason:_ Identical inherited pattern across all 17 host-side shims. _Carry-to:_ **post-Epic-2 `_lib.sh` refactor** — shared helper can branch on `docker inspect` distinct exit codes (2 = no such object vs other = daemon/API fault) and emit exit 8 vs exit 9 appropriately.
- **AR-62 — `CONTAINER_NAME` env var not validated against leading-dash / whitespace / metacharacters.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter (convergent). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/gh-auth-host.sh:45`. _Nature:_ `${KEEL_DEVBOX_CONTAINER_NAME:-keel-devbox}` fallback with no `--` separator before `"${CONTAINER_NAME}"` in the subsequent `docker inspect` / `docker exec` calls; a value with a leading `-` is mis-parsed by docker as a flag, and whitespace-bearing values produce unpredictable target containers. _Defer reason:_ Story 2.6 SC-11 + SC-2 precedent — the `${VAR:-default}` pattern is substrate-wide convention; fork operators are trusted not to set malicious env vars (threat model: operator-trusted input, not attacker-controlled). Substrate-wide; all 17 shims share the pattern. _Carry-to:_ **post-Epic-2 `_lib.sh` refactor** — shared `validate_container_name()` helper can enforce `[A-Za-z0-9_.-]+` pattern + emit exit 2 on violation.
- **AR-63 — SIGPIPE-forwarding claim in wrapper comment + SC-10 is technically imprecise.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/gh-auth-host.sh:64-66`. _Nature:_ Wrapper comment states "`docker exec` forwards SIGINT/SIGTERM/SIGPIPE to gh's PID inside the container." `docker exec` does forward SIGINT/SIGTERM via the Docker API, but SIGPIPE is a per-process kernel signal raised on write-to-closed-pipe inside the target process — it is not "forwarded" from the host. Comment is verbatim inheritance from SC-10 + Story 2.1 iter-144 SIGPIPE precedent + claude-host.sh:45. _Defer reason:_ Correcting it in gh-auth-host.sh alone breaks SC-17 "mirrors claude-host.sh verbatim" discipline. _Carry-to:_ **post-Epic-2 `_lib.sh` refactor** or a standalone docs-cleanup pass — refine comment to "`docker exec` forwards SIGINT/SIGTERM to gh's PID; SIGPIPE is raised locally in the target process by the kernel on write-to-closed-pipe" across all 17 shims atomically.
- **AR-64 — `github.txt` 7-entry enumeration cited across AGENTS.md + README.md + story file without drift gate.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter. _Location:_ `AGENTS.md § gh CLI authentication (Story 2.9) § Scope carve-out` + mirrored in story file Dev Notes + CR forecast text. _Nature:_ AGENTS.md enumerates all 7 GitHub whitelist entries inline; if `packages/devbox/whitelist/github.txt` drifts (entry added/removed at CI security review), the AGENTS.md enumeration becomes stale with no lint gate to catch it. _Defer reason:_ Story 1.9 INVARIANTS.md↔manifest sync-gate covers content-hash drift (`INV-devbox-egress-contract` hashes the whitelist file) but the cross-file prose enumerations in AGENTS.md + README.md are not currently sync-gate-watched. Same class as Story 2.7 AR-50 `KEEL_DEVBOX_CONTAINER_NAME` doc-drift concern. _Carry-to:_ **Story 1.9+ sync-gate extension** OR a dedicated substrate lint rule (`tools/lint-substrate-enumerations.ts`) that diffs `packages/devbox/whitelist/github.txt` content against AGENTS.md + README.md prose enumerations and fails on drift. Low-cost once framework lands.
- **AR-65 — OAuth device-code surface on stdout → log-leak risk if operator `tee`s output.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/README.md § First-run OAuth flow (AC 1, AC 2)`. _Nature:_ OAuth device codes (valid ~15 min, single-use per GitHub's device-flow spec) appear on operator stdout during `gh auth login`. If operator runs `pnpm gh:auth 2>&1 | tee gh-auth.log` (common troubleshooting pattern), the code lands in a logfile. Practically low severity (attacker would race the operator's own OAuth completion and GitHub allows multiple tokens per account), but worth operator-warning. Applies symmetrically to `pnpm claude` OAuth flow (Story 2.8). _Defer reason:_ Substrate-wide (both auth verbs); docs-hint addition is a polish-pass scope item. _Carry-to:_ **Story 2.17 Epic 2 close-out polish** — add a `> **Security note:** OAuth flow emits a short-lived device code to stdout; do not `tee`/pipe the output to a logfile during the flow.` callout to README.md sections for both auth verbs atomically.
- **AR-66 — No `IFS=$' \t\n'` reset at top of wrapper.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/gh-auth-host.sh:31` (just after `set -euo pipefail`). _Nature:_ A parent shell with non-default IFS could affect `"$@"` expansion in edge cases (whitespace in scope lists, tab characters, etc.). Defensive bash scripts normally pin `IFS=$' \t\n'` alongside `set -euo pipefail`. Zero live exposure at 1.0 (pnpm shell-out strips abnormal IFS; no explicit word-splitting on untrusted values inside the script body). _Defer reason:_ Identical inherited pattern across all 17 host-side shims. _Carry-to:_ **post-Epic-2 `_lib.sh` refactor** — shared boilerplate block can set `IFS=$' \t\n'` + `set -euo pipefail` + `unset COMPOSE_PROJECT_NAME` atomically.
- **AR-67 — `docker info` has no timeout (hangs if daemon alive but unresponsive).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/gh-auth-host.sh:53`. _Nature:_ Bare `docker info --format '{{.ServerVersion}}'` hangs indefinitely on a slow/unresponsive daemon; operator cannot distinguish from an in-progress OAuth prompt. `timeout 10s docker info ...` would fail-closed with exit 8 after bound. Matches Story 2.7 AR-48 duplicate confirmation. _Defer reason:_ Identical inherited pattern across all 17 host-side shims; daemon-hang is OS-level failure. _Carry-to:_ **post-Epic-2 `_lib.sh` refactor** — shared `docker_info_check()` helper can wrap the call in `timeout 10s` and emit exit 8 on timeout with a distinct diagnostic ("docker daemon unresponsive after 10s").
- **AR-68 — Ambiguous container name across multi-compose-project scenarios.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/gh-auth-host.sh:62`. _Nature:_ If two containers share the name via compose-project override (unlikely under `unset COMPOSE_PROJECT_NAME` pin but theoretically possible if operator runs two worktrees with overlapping `.envrc` values), `docker inspect` targets one non-deterministically. A `docker ps -aq --filter "name=^${CONTAINER_NAME}$" | wc -l` pre-check catches the duplicate case. _Defer reason:_ Same substrate-wide pattern; the `unset COMPOSE_PROJECT_NAME` + `.envrc` `KEEL_DEVBOX_CONTAINER_NAME` convention at 1.0 makes duplicates unlikely in practice. _Carry-to:_ **post-Epic-2 `_lib.sh` refactor** or a dedicated Story 2.11 (shared-devbox mode) task — the shared-mode work explicitly touches multi-container naming and is the natural home for this guard.
- **AR-69 — `paused` / `restarting` / `removing` container states misdiagnosed as "not running".** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/gh-auth-host.sh:63`. _Nature:_ `[[ "${state}" != "running" ]]` branch emits "container is not running — run `pnpm devbox:start` first" for any non-running state, including transient (`restarting`, `removing`) and suspended (`paused`) states. A `case`-based dispatch could emit more-diagnostic messages per state. AR-54 + AR-43 duplicate confirmation. _Defer reason:_ Identical inherited pattern; no operator friction has surfaced in Stories 2.1-2.8 usage. _Carry-to:_ **post-Epic-2 `_lib.sh` refactor** — shared `ensure_container_running()` helper can branch on `paused` (hint: `docker unpause`), `restarting` (hint: "wait 10s and retry"), `removing` (hint: "stale container; `pnpm devbox:clean` to cycle"), `exited`/`dead`/`created` (hint: `pnpm devbox:start`).
- **AR-70 — "Mirrors `claude-host.sh` verbatim" has no drift gate.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/gh-auth-host.sh` vs `packages/devbox/scripts/claude-host.sh`. _Nature:_ AGENTS.md + spec Dev Notes SC-1 claim the two scripts mirror each other 1:1 with documented substitutions. If `claude-host.sh` receives a security/robustness fix in isolation (e.g., the `docker inspect` TOCTOU fix, or a `docker info` timeout), nothing auto-propagates to `gh-auth-host.sh` — the mirror claim silently degrades over time. _Defer reason:_ This is exactly the problem the SC-14 `_lib.sh` refactor solves by factoring the shared pre-flight into one sourced library; the forcing-function for that refactor is the post-Epic-2 amortization point. _Carry-to:_ **post-Epic-2 `_lib.sh` refactor** — extract `packages/devbox/scripts/lib/docker-preflight.sh` (shared `unset COMPOSE_PROJECT_NAME` + `docker_info_check()` + `ensure_container_running()` + `log()`). Story 2.9 post-iter-239 retrofit already extracted `lib/main-repo-resolver.sh` + `lib/check-mount-source.sh` as a first slice of this refactor — trajectory is now visible + the amortization point is closer than forecast at iter-233.

Task 1 spec phrases "one optional positional arg" (singular) but neither the spec nor SC-16 explicitly forbids extras. Creates a subtle bypass illusion: an operator inventing `--force` sees silent pass-through on Tier-1 and believes they bypassed Tier-2 (when in fact Tier-1 just passed naturally). _Defer reason:_ No observable harm at 1.0; consistent with Story 2.6 shim permissive arg-passing; no automation consumer exists that would invent a flag. _Carry-to:_ **SC-17 Epic 2 close-out polish** — `[[ $# -gt 1 ]]` guard emits usage + exit 2; natural fit alongside AR-18 `--help` surface and SC-16 `--help` deferral.

- **AR-73 — `rm`ing `prereq-check.sh` leaves 17 wired shims dead with exit 127 "No such file or directory" and no recovery pointer.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter (MEDIUM). _Location:_ All 17 wired shims under `packages/devbox/scripts/{build,rebuild,start,stop,restart,clean,shell,attach,status,logs,monitor-host,whitelist-host,env-check,claude-host,gh-auth-host,ralph-build-host,ralph-plan-host}.sh`. _Nature:_ Every wired shim does `"${SCRIPT_DIR}/prereq-check.sh" --tier<N>` with no `[[ -x … ]]` existence guard and no `git checkout` recovery hint. Contrast `monitor-host.sh:58-61` which DOES guard missing `monitor.sh` with exit 3 + `git checkout` hint. prereq-check.sh is load-bearing but unguarded — an accidental `rm` (or partial branch checkout during a merge) silently breaks every `pnpm devbox:*` + `pnpm ralph:*` entry point. _Defer reason:_ 17-shim cross-cut change; operational-only concern (not code-correctness); low-probability operator-error scenario. _Carry-to:_ **post-Epic-2 `_lib.sh` refactor (SC-14 chain; merges with AR-60..AR-70 scope)** — shared `invoke_prereq_check <tier>` helper in `lib/preflight.sh` guards once for all callers, factoring the `[[ -x ... ]]` check and the `git checkout packages/devbox/scripts/prereq-check.sh` recovery hint into a single source of truth.

- **AR-74 — Magic strings (install URL, Claude/gh pointer strings, alpine pin, token paths) repeated across 3 source-of-truth sites with only convention-enforced lockstep.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter (NIT) + Edge Case Hunter (LOW, convergent with composite-ordering-not-pinned concern). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/prereq-check.sh` + `docs/invariants/devbox-prereq-check.md` + `packages/devbox/README.md`. _Nature:_ Install URL `https://docs.docker.com/desktop/install/`; pointer strings `Claude Code not authed — run 'pnpm claude' first` + `gh CLI not authed — run 'pnpm gh:auth' first` (em-dash U+2014); image pin `alpine:3.19`; token paths `/home/dev/.claude/.credentials.json` + `/home/dev/.config/gh/hosts.yml`. Story 1.9 contentHash sync-gate binds the INV doc BUT not the shell script or README. A typo fix in one site silently drifts the other two. SC-7 acknowledges "All three must update in lockstep (manifest contentHash binds the doc; source + README are convention-enforced)" — convention under multi-iter Ralph is fragile. _Defer reason:_ A pre-commit regex gate comparing shell literal ↔ doc literal ↔ README literal would eliminate the drift class entirely, but it's an invariants-package substrate feature (new `substrate-string-lockstep.ts` check or extension of existing sync-gate). Out of scope for Story 2.10 PATCH-1 impl. _Carry-to:_ **Story 2.17 Epic 2 close-out OR a dedicated substrate-polish story** — `packages/keel-invariants/src/substrate-string-lockstep.ts` check that extracts `log "…"` string literals from `packages/devbox/scripts/*.sh` and diffs against pinned strings referenced in `docs/invariants/*.md` + `packages/devbox/README.md`. Drift → fail + emit per-site-diff diagnostic. Same class of lint as Story 1.9 sync-gate but string-level rather than contentHash-level.

- **AR-80 — Resolver double-flip hazard if `resolve_mode_specific_state` is called twice in same shell without re-running `resolve_main_repo_and_workdir` between calls.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter #6+#7 + Edge Case Hunter E7 (convergent). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/lib/main-repo-resolver.sh:160`. _Nature:_ Shared branch does `shared_parent="$(dirname "$MAIN_REPO")"` and assigns `MAIN_REPO="$shared_parent"`. Second invocation without reset would apply `dirname` twice (landing at grandparent). No guard against this. Subprocess boundary preserves integrity across 18 shims (verified — each shim spawned as independent process), but in-process re-invocation would corrupt state. `prereq-check.sh` claims "re-running here is idempotent (same inputs, same exports)" — this is only true under subprocess invocation; in-process re-call would double-flip. _Defer reason:_ No in-process re-invocation pattern across 18 shims; idempotency is caller-responsibility documented in resolver comment block. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.12+ or Story 2.17 — add early-return guard in `resolve_mode_specific_state` if `KEEL_DEVBOX_COMPOSE_PROJECT_RESOLVED_BY_STORY_2_11=1` sentinel is already set; idempotency becomes hardcoded rather than convention.

- **AR-81 — restart.sh invokes resolver 3× (self + transitive stop.sh + start.sh subprocesses); potential race window if operator flips `.envrc` mid-restart under direnv auto-reload.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter #11 + Edge Case Hunter E23 (convergent). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/restart.sh:41-42`. _Nature:_ restart.sh resolves its own mode, then delegates to stop.sh (which re-resolves) and start.sh (which re-resolves). If direnv reloads `.envrc` between restart.sh's resolver call and the delegated subprocess's resolver call (rare but possible on a stalled stop), stop.sh stops `keel-devbox` but start.sh boots `keel-devbox-shared`. _Defer reason:_ Narrow race window; documented in restart.sh comment at L38-42 as "Transitive delegates ... prepend here for fail-fast inspect consistency"; operator-responsibility to avoid mid-restart `.envrc` edits. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.12+ — cache resolved mode at restart.sh entry in an env var that subprocess resolver-calls inherit verbatim, bypassing direnv re-read.

- **AR-82 — Silent clobber of operator `KEEL_DEVBOX_COMPOSE_PROJECT` in per-fork mode — resolver unconditionally assigns `"keel-devbox"` regardless of operator setting; no warning emitted.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter #16 + Edge Case Hunter E6 per-fork branch. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/lib/main-repo-resolver.sh:151`. _Nature:_ Operator may set `KEEL_DEVBOX_COMPOSE_PROJECT=foo` in `.envrc` expecting it to flow into compose's top-level `name:` interpolation. Resolver clobbers to `keel-devbox` without warning. Invariant doc claims "operator's `KEEL_DEVBOX_COMPOSE_PROJECT` setting is intentionally ignored" but per-fork branch of resolver doesn't document this clobber in-line. Grep-for-override reveals no override path exists. _Defer reason:_ Operator-transparency class; behavioural consistency with invariant doc claim; SC-17 documentation sweep candidate. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 Epic 2 close-out documentation pass — add stderr warning when `KEEL_DEVBOX_COMPOSE_PROJECT` is set by operator and differs from the mode-hardcoded value.

- **AR-83 — `unset COMPOSE_PROJECT_NAME` ordering audit required across 18 shims.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter #12 + Edge Case Hunter E32. _Location:_ substrate-wide (all 18 host-side shims; resolver library has defensive unset at line 92). _Nature:_ Resolver library's `unset COMPOSE_PROJECT_NAME` at L92 covers the source-time path; individual shims MAY unset above or below their resolver-source block inconsistently. A shim that unsets AFTER source would allow operator's stale `COMPOSE_PROJECT_NAME` to win over resolver's output for any brief time window before the shim proceeds. _Defer reason:_ No known failure case demonstrated; resolver L92 unset covers the common path; individual-shim audit is precautionary. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 Epic 2 close-out audit — `grep -n 'unset COMPOSE_PROJECT_NAME' packages/devbox/scripts/*.sh` + `grep -n 'source.*main-repo-resolver.sh' packages/devbox/scripts/*.sh` → verify unset precedes source in every shim.

- **AR-84 — `KEEL_DEVBOX_SHARED` whitespace + non-boolean-synonym tolerance — resolver case-folds but does NOT trim whitespace or accept `1`/`yes`/`on`/`y`/`t`.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter E1+E2. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/lib/main-repo-resolver.sh:146`. _Nature:_ Operator `.envrc` with `KEEL_DEVBOX_SHARED=" true"` (leading space) or `KEEL_DEVBOX_SHARED=yes` silently routes to per-fork mode (the safe fail-closed posture). No warning. Documented at line 65-68: "Anything else (false, 0, no, empty, unset) resolves to per-fork mode." _Defer reason:_ Typo-tolerance UX class; fail-closed-to-per-fork is the documented and safe posture; surfacing would require explicit warning path for non-matched input. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.12+ — add resolver-emit `printf 'resolver: WARNING: KEEL_DEVBOX_SHARED=%s not in {true,false}; defaulting per-fork\n' "$shared" >&2` for any non-empty non-matched input (whitespace, synonyms).

- **AR-85 — env-check.sh line 208 `parsed[KEEL_DEVBOX_SHARED]` equality compare lacks resolver's case-fold; `KEEL_DEVBOX_SHARED=TRUE` in `.envrc` routes resolver to shared but env-check computes `OTHER_MODE=shared` → false-positive warning about the CURRENT container.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter E10. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/env-check.sh:208`. _Nature:_ Resolver case-folds at L146 (accepts TRUE/True/true); env-check's `[[ "${parsed[KEEL_DEVBOX_SHARED]}" == "true" ]]` at L208 is byte-exact. Divergence produces spurious warning "orphaned shared-mode container 'keel-devbox-shared' detected..." when the shared container is actually the CURRENT one (because resolver routed shared but env-check's branch logic thinks we're in per-fork). _Defer reason:_ False-positive-warning noise class only (no functional break); one-liner fix `shared_lc=$(echo "${parsed[KEEL_DEVBOX_SHARED]}" | tr '[:upper:]' '[:lower:]'); if [[ "$shared_lc" == "true" ]]; then` held separate from PATCH-1 for single-PATCH-per-CR iter-253 discipline. _Carry-to:_ PATCH-2 candidate if CR re-run surfaces (after PATCH-1 landing); otherwise Story 2.12 first task.

- **AR-86 — `docker inspect` rc>1 (daemon transient/permission error) silently skipped in env-check orphan probe; operator misses legitimate orphan warning on daemon hiccup.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter E11+E24 (convergent with restart.sh inspect masking). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/env-check.sh:222-233`. _Nature:_ rc-capture `case` swallows rc>1 with `*) : ;;`. Tier 1 prereq-check already cleared basic reachability upstream, but a mid-env-check daemon hiccup (e.g., Docker Desktop wake-race) produces silent skip. No "probe skipped (rc=<N>)" diagnostic. _Defer reason:_ SC-5 warning-only-posture preserved (exit schema 0/2/3/8 unchanged); surfacing daemon transients would complicate exit-code schema. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 or Story 3.N (Ralph halt schema extension) — emit `env-check: warning: orphan probe skipped (docker inspect rc=${rc}); rerun env-check if daemon was transient` so operator knows probe ran but couldn't conclude.

- **AR-87 — Orphan-container volume leak — env-check probes container presence only; mode-specific named volume `keel-devbox-shared_keel_home_dev` (or per-fork equivalent) persists silently when container is `docker rm`-ed but volume was not removed.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter E14. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/env-check.sh:194-233`. _Nature:_ OAuth-token volume survives container removal by default (Docker's design); operator's `docker rm -f <orphan>` leaves the volume consuming disk and potentially polluting fresh OAuth flows at next `pnpm devbox:start`. Env-check probes container but not volume. _Defer reason:_ Disk-leak class; operator remediation path via `pnpm devbox:clean --with-volumes` exists. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 Epic 2 close-out — add `docker volume inspect "${OTHER_CONTAINER}_keel_home_dev" >/dev/null 2>&1 && log "warning: orphaned ${OTHER_MODE}-mode volume detected; run 'pnpm devbox:clean --with-volumes'"` after the container-probe case block.

- **AR-88 — Standalone `prereq-check.sh` invocation in non-direnv shell — process-env `KEEL_DEVBOX_SHARED` stale vs `.envrc` file content; Tier 2 volume probe targets wrong-mode volume.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter E16+E30 (convergent pattern with stop.sh). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/prereq-check.sh:60-65`. _Nature:_ env-check.sh parses `.envrc` authoritatively (L201 `export KEEL_DEVBOX_SHARED="${parsed[KEEL_DEVBOX_SHARED]:-false}"`) before resolver invocation. prereq-check.sh does NOT parse `.envrc`; inherits process env only. Under non-direnv host shell, fresh operator invocation of `pnpm devbox:prereq:check` after flipping `.envrc` value but before `direnv allow` would probe the stale-mode volume. _Defer reason:_ Non-direnv host edge (every canonical Ralph + Devbox invocation path uses direnv-exported env); mirror-fix against env-check.sh pattern is available. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.12+ — mirror env-check.sh's parse-then-export pattern in prereq-check.sh's standalone-invocation branch.

- **AR-89 — Shim UX enhancements for shared-mode awareness (attach/build/status/logs/clean hints).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter E19+E21+E25+E26+E27. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/attach.sh:41`, `build.sh:17-23`, `status.sh:22-32`, `logs.sh:28-32`, `clean.sh:137`. _Nature:_ (a) `attach.sh` mid-flip hint when target container not-running but other-mode is (E19); (b) `build.sh` warning when rebuilding with other-mode container running (E25); (c) `status.sh` doesn't name current mode (E26); (d) `logs.sh` doesn't suggest other-mode container on "no output" (E27); (e) `clean.sh --with-volumes` doesn't clarify per-mode-only scope (E21). _Defer reason:_ UX-polish class — no correctness regression; Story 2.11's convention-first doctrine is satisfied. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.12+ (loopback-bound ports) or Story 2.13+ (healthcheck replacement) — co-land UX hints during shim re-entry under those stories' scope.

- **AR-90 — Concurrent `devbox:start` + `devbox:clean` race windows in shared mode (two forks overlapping wall-clock windows).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter E18+E22. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/start.sh:86`, `clean.sh:163`. _Nature:_ Two forks simultaneously run `pnpm devbox:start` or `pnpm devbox:clean` against shared mode — Docker provides no built-in serialization of compose-up or compose-down operations against the same project name. Race produces duplicate env-check runs, phantom orphan warnings, or partial teardowns. _Defer reason:_ AC 4 explicitly pins "single-operator-at-a-time by convention, NOT by Docker enforcement" — adding `flock`-based mutex would fight the convention-first doctrine. _Carry-to:_ No carry (convention-first is the 1.0 posture); re-evaluate only if operator feedback surfaces mutex as a forced requirement.

## Deferred from: code review of story-2.12 (2026-04-24)

_Story 2.12 (Loopback-bound port publication + opt-in `KEEL_DEVBOX_SSH` sshd) — iter-271 `/bmad-code-review (args: "2")`. Three-layer Ralph-hosted adversarial fan-out (Blind Hunter as `general-purpose` diff-only / Edge Case Hunter as `general-purpose` diff+project-read / Acceptance Auditor as `bmad-agent-architect` Winston diff+spec+context). Convergent 5 PATCH (4 substantive HIGH/MEDIUM-HIGH on substrate-runtime defects unverified-by-construction at iter-270 SM static smokes + 1 MEDIUM scope refactor on paths-with-spaces idiom across 15 sites) + 11 DEFER (operator-edges + Story 2.17 close-out scope + future-hardening). Forecast band breach: 5 PATCH lands ABOVE iter-270 SM ZERO-PATCH carry-forward + iter-264 LESSON 0-3 first-class PATCH band; the breach traces to iter-266 NOVEL LESSON's "novel-runtime-behaviour" surface (sshd-host-key bootstrap + cap_drop posture interaction + entrypoint set -e discipline) which static smokes cannot exercise. The 11 defers below are spec-silent or future-story-scope; none are exploitable in the default operator config (loopback-bound + cap_drop:[ALL] + named-volume persistence)._

- **PrivSep chroot may fail under `cap_drop: [ALL]` — empirical-verification-required.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter MEDIUM solo. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/sshd/sshd_config (full file)` + `packages/devbox/entrypoint.sh:169`. _Nature:_ OpenSSH 7.5+ removed the `UsePrivilegeSeparation` directive and made sandbox-mode the default (seccomp_filter, NOT chroot). Modern Ubuntu 24.04 builds (iter-123 image bake) should use sandbox mode → no CAP_SYS_CHROOT needed. If first-live-operator-workstation test surfaces "fatal: chroot: Operation not permitted", remediate by adding `UsePrivilegeSeparation no` to sshd_config OR add CAP_SYS_CHROOT to compose `cap_add` (latter weakens Story 2.5 hardening posture). _Carry-to:_ first live operator-workstation smoke verification; Story 2.13 healthcheck would surface this loudly via failed-liveness signal.
- **SFTP subsystem enabled — sshd_config:30 widens "pubkey-only debug shell" surface to file-transfer.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter MEDIUM + Edge Case Hunter MEDIUM convergent. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/sshd/sshd_config:30` (`Subsystem sftp /usr/lib/openssh/sftp-server`). _Nature:_ AC 3 spec text says "pubkey-only ssh into dev shell" — does not explicitly cover SFTP. Authenticated pubkey-holder can `sftp dev@127.0.0.1:2222` and bulk-transfer `/home/dev/.claude/.credentials.json` (Story 2.8 OAuth tokens) or `/workspace/.envrc.local` (secrets) without producing shell session logs. Operator-trust boundary (only operators authorised the pubkey), so impact is bounded. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 close-out polish — either remove SFTP (one-line sshd_config edit; changes operator UX no `scp` workflow) or document as intentional with explicit AC clause. Or future Story 2.18+ hardening pass.
- **`KEEL_DEVBOX_SSH_PORT` undocumented + unvalidated.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter LOW + Edge Case Hunter MEDIUM + Acceptance Auditor LOW convergent. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/docker-compose.ssh.yml:19` + `packages/devbox/.envrc.example:40` + `packages/devbox/scripts/env-check.sh REQUIRED_VARS`. _Nature:_ Override interpolates `${KEEL_DEVBOX_SSH_PORT:-2222}` but the var is absent from `.envrc.example`, env-check REQUIRED_VARS, and operator README walkthroughs. Embedded colons or non-integer values mangle publish-port spec; privileged-port escape (`KEEL_DEVBOX_SSH_PORT=22`) requires Docker daemon root which it has → silently shadows host sshd. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 — add `.envrc.example` line + env-check REQUIRED_VARS entry + resolver-side validation (regex `^[0-9]{1,5}$` + range check 1024-65535).
- **AC 4 / invariant doc claim about `userland-proxy=false` overstates IPv6 confinement.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter MEDIUM solo. _Location:_ `docs/invariants/devbox-ssh.md § External connection refusal` + `AGENTS.md § Container-side ListenAddress`. _Nature:_ Docker installs IPv4 DNAT scoped to `127.0.0.1` under `userland-proxy=false`, but IPv6 paths governed by separate `ip6tables` daemon flag (default disabled until ~Docker 26.x). Operator with LAN-IPv6 connectivity and Docker daemon `ip6tables=false` may reach `[::]:2222` on the host's IPv6 stack. Invariant doc claim "BOTH modes refuse LAN-sourced traffic" is conditional on daemon-config combinations not enumerated. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 invariant-doc polish — extend § External connection refusal to enumerate the `(userland-proxy, ip6tables)` matrix.
- **`StrictModes` parent-dir `/home/dev` perms not chmod-enforced — silent auth refuse on backup-restored named volume.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter MEDIUM solo. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/entrypoint.sh:146`. _Nature:_ Idempotent `chmod 0700` covers `.ssh` and `.ssh/host_keys` but not `/home/dev` itself. If named volume restored from rsync backup with non-default `/home/dev` perms (group/other write), sshd's StrictModes silently rejects auth with cryptic `/var/log/sshd.log` entry. Operator-edge: requires operator to restore named volume from non-Docker-init source. Dockerfile `chmod 0755 /home/dev` (line 254) sets initial state cleanly; only operator-restore paths get the surprise. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 — consider adding `/home/dev` to chmod block OR documenting operator-restore prerequisite.
- **`/etc/ssh/ssh_host_*_key` baked-but-unused by `openssh-server` postinst — fingerprinting surface if config drifts.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter LOW + Edge Case Hunter LOW convergent. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/Dockerfile:66`. _Nature:_ Ubuntu's openssh-server postinst generates `/etc/ssh/ssh_host_{rsa,ecdsa,ed25519}_key` at apt install time → baked into image layer, identical across every fork's build. sshd_config doesn't reference these paths (HostKey points at `/home/dev/.ssh/host_keys/...`), so they're unused bytes. If sshd_config ever reverts/amends to default paths, every fork's sshd would present the same fingerprint → MITM-vector / cross-fork key-reuse. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 image-tidy pass — `RUN rm -f /etc/ssh/ssh_host_*_key` after openssh-server install; minimal layer-cost change.
- **No `MaxAuthTries` / `LoginGraceTime` / `MaxStartups` overrides + `AllowUsers dev` lacks source-IP.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter LOW + Edge Case Hunter LOW convergent. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/sshd/sshd_config (full file)`. _Nature:_ sshd defaults: 6 / 120s / 10:30:100; `AllowUsers dev` permits any source IP that traverses the publish gate. Pubkey-only + loopback-bound mitigates brute-force impact; defence-in-depth would specify `AllowUsers dev@127.0.0.1` to refuse if Docker's host-side confinement lapses (AC4 ip6tables edge). Design choice was single-layer host-side confinement per sshd_config L13-16 comment. _Carry-to:_ post-Epic 2 hardening story; Story 2.18+ if added.
- **Mode-flip orphan warning missing — no parallel to Story 2.11 `KEEL_DEVBOX_SHARED` env-check warning.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter MEDIUM solo. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/env-check.sh + start.sh`. _Nature:_ Operator started container with `KEEL_DEVBOX_SSH=true`, then flips `.envrc` to false without restart, then runs `pnpm devbox:status` / `stop` / `clean` — env-check has no analog warning to Story 2.11's mid-flip orphan-container probe. Story 2.12 § Mode-flip discipline pins "container teardown required" but no machine-enforced reminder. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 close-out — add SSH-mode-flip probe + warning-only stderr emit (mirrors Story 2.11 pattern; orthogonal to SHARED-mode probe).
- **`docker exec` shims (shell, attach, claude-host, gh-auth-host, ralph-build/plan-host, whitelist-host, monitor-host) bypass SSH override entirely — latent regression-trap.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter LOW solo. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/scripts/{shell,attach,claude-host,gh-auth-host,ralph-build-host,ralph-plan-host,whitelist-host,monitor-host}.sh`. _Nature:_ These shims `docker exec` against a presumed-running container; current behaviour is loud-fail when container missing. They do NOT call `resolve_ssh_state` and do NOT thread the SSH compose override. If a future story adds "auto-start if missing" to any of these shims, the absent SSH override would silently start a no-SSH container despite `KEEL_DEVBOX_SSH=true`. No correctness regression at 1.0. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 close-out audit OR Epic 3+ Ralph TUI auto-start path.
- **`pnpm devbox:clean --with-volumes` regenerates host keys → operator's `~/.ssh/known_hosts` mismatch — operator-lockout/revoke flow.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter MEDIUM + Edge Case Hunter MEDIUM + Acceptance Auditor LOW convergent. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/entrypoint.sh:151` + `packages/devbox/scripts/clean.sh`. _Nature:_ Operator runs clean --with-volumes → host keys regenerate on next opt-in → `ssh -p 2222 dev@127.0.0.1` errors with "REMOTE HOST IDENTIFICATION HAS CHANGED" → manual `ssh-keygen -R '[127.0.0.1]:2222'` recovery. Story 2.12 § Scope carve-out explicitly defers operator-lockout/revoke flow to Story 2.17. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 owns operator-lockout/revoke flow + recovery doc + clean-script in-band pointer to recovery command.
- **Various LOW operator-edges (10+).** _Source:_ Blind Hunter LOW + Edge Case Hunter LOW. _Locations:_ `sshd/sshd_config:27` `UsePAM no` skips per-user limits; `entrypoint.sh:162` `chmod` follows symlinks; `lib/main-repo-resolver.sh:240-241` `KEEL_DEVBOX_COMPOSE_FILE_SSH=""` exported empty-string ambiguity; `entrypoint.sh:174` `tail -n 20` runs even when sshd_config syntax was rejected at parse time; `sshd/sshd_config:17` container-side `Port 2222` hardcoded (KEEL_DEVBOX_SSH_PORT only changes HOST-side); `sshd/sshd_config:29` `AcceptEnv LANG LC_*` widens client-controlled env; `entrypoint.sh:169` `/var/log/sshd.log` no rotation; `entrypoint.sh:155-156` `ssh-keygen -q` no-stderr-capture; `lib/main-repo-resolver.sh:251` `pwd -P` worktree-symlink edge; `lib/main-repo-resolver.sh:251` resolver does NOT honour `KEEL_DEVBOX_REPO_ROOT`. _Nature:_ Cumulative ~10 narrow operator-edge findings; none triggers in default operator config; each fix is 1-3 lines but cumulative dispatch density is higher than benefit at this story scope. iter-264 LESSON severity-class-first rule applies. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 close-out reconciliation pass sweeps cumulative DEFER queue across Epic 2; Story 2.18+ may absorb hardening-class items.
